ostmay otheryay artspay ofyay ethay orldway atyay onay ostcay andyay ithway almostyay onay estrictionsray 
atsoeverwhay. Youyay aymay opycay ityay, ivegay ityay awayyay oryay e-useray ityay underyay ethay ermstay 
ofyay ethay Ojectpray Utenberggay Icenselay includedyay ithway isthay ebookyay oryay onlineyay 
atyay wwway.gutenberg.org. Ifyay youyay areyay otnay ocatedlay inyay ethay Unitedyay Atesstay, 
youyay illway avehay otay eckchay ethay awslay ofyay ethay ountrycay erewhay youyay areyay ocatedlay 
eforebay usingyay isthay ebookyay.

OTWAY IRLSGAY ANDYAY Ayay ERYMYSTAY 
 
 
 
 
APTERCHAY Iyay 
 
ALLYAY ABOUTYAY ONEYMAY 
 
 
Arbarabay Intersway adhay eenbay eadingray inyay ethay alcovedyay indowway eatsay, alfhay 
iddenhay omfray ethay estray ofyay ethay ozycay ivinglay oomray. Ityay asway eallyray anyay excitingyay 
ookbay, orrowedbay omfray oneyay ofyay ethay irlsgay atyay oolschay. Utbay, alasyay, Arbarabay adhay 
allenfay asleepyay ustjay inyay ethay ostmay excitingyay artpay ofyay ityay. 
 
Eshay asway ousedray, owhay uchmay aterlay eshay ouldcay otnay elltay, byay ethay oundsay ofyay 
amiliarfay oicesvay. 
 
Owsilydray, alfhay asleepyay, eshay istenedlay orfay ayay omentmay eforebay ealizingray atthay 
ethay onversationcay asway otnay intendedyay orfay erhay earsyay. Enthay ityay asway impossibleyay 
otay escapeyay ithoutway etrayingbay ethay actfay atthay eshay adhay overheardyay. Illstay alfhay 
uggeddray ithway eepslay, Abbay aylay illstay. 
 
Atthay asway erewhay erhay iserymay eganbay! 
 
Andmothergray andyay andfathergray ereway alkingtay. Abbay adhay ostlay erhay othermay andyay 
atherfay atyay ayay imetay enwhay eshay asway ootay youngyay evenyay otay ememberray emthay. Incesay 
enthay, Andmothergray andyay “An”gray adhay illedfay atthay agicallytray emptyyay aceplay inyay 
ethay ittlelay irl’sgay ifelay. Owhay ellway eythay adhay illedfay ityay andyay owhay appyhay eythay 
adhay ademay erhay, onlyyay Abbay ewknay. 
 
Erhay eyesyay idenedway ithway orrorhay asyay eshay istenedlay. 
 
Eythay, Angray andyay erhay andmothergray, ereway alkingtay ofyay oneymay. Eythay adhay otnay, ityay 
appearedyay, enoughyay otay akemay endsyay eetmay. An’sgray oicevay oundedsay eadfuldray enwhay 
ehay aidsay at--sothay oldyay andyay earyway andyay erriblytay iscouragedday. Earstay ereway inyay 
Ab’sbay eyesyay asyay eshay oughtfay ithway ayay esireday otay ingflay erhay armsyay aboutyay imhay. 
 
Ethay arway asway inyay omesay ayway esponsibleray orfay isthay angechay inyay ethay oldyay 
entleman’sgay ortunesfay. Abbay atheredgay atthay eythay ightmay even--unbelievableyay 
alamitycay!--be orcedfay otay ivegay upyay eirthay ettypray omehay. 
 
“Eway ustmay eepkay isthay omfray Abbay atyay allyay ostscay,” inishedfay Angray. Abbay ewknay, 
ithoutway eeingsay imhay, atthay ehay asway olishingpay ishay assesglay, ayay ingthay ehay 
alwaysyay idday enwhay upsetyay aboutyay anythingyay oryay uneasyyay inyay ishay indmay. “Osay aygay andyay 
ight-heartedlay. Eway ustmay eepkay erhay osay.” 
 
“Yesyay.” Earday andmother’sgray oicevay asway oftsay andyay anxiousyay. “Isthay adowshay ustmay 
otnay ouchtay erhay. Eshay isyay onlyyay ayay ildchay.” 
 
Afteryay atthay Abbay ouldway otnay, orfay ethay orldway, etlay emthay owknay atthay eshay adhay 
overheardyay. Eshay aylay eryvay, eryvay illstay untilyay eythay entway intoyay ethay iningday 
oomray. Enthay ayay iftsway ushray acrossyay ethay oomray andyay upstairsyay otay erhay ownyay oomray 
erewhay eshay ightmay onderpay, undisturbedyay, isthay eadfuldray ingthay eshay adhay eardhay. 
 
Asway ityay onlyyay anyay ourhay eforebay atthay eshay adhay eenbay osay aygay andyay are-freecay? Enthay 
erethay adhay otnay eenbay ayay eavierhay orryway onyay erhay indmay anthay asyay otay owhay eshay ouldway 
endspay ethay ummersay acationvay! 
 
An’sgray iredtay oicevay; andmother’sgray unfailingyay oughtthay ofyay erhay! 
 
Omethingsay ardhay andyay ainfulpay oseray andyay oseray inyay Ab’sbay oatthray untilyay eshay asway 
orcedfay otay urybay erhay acefay inyay ethay illowpay onyay erhay edbay andyay iflestay erhay obssay inyay 
ityay. 
 
“Ityay isn’tyay air--they’refay osay oldyay! Iyay ustmay indfay omesay ayway otay elphay emthay!” 
 
Afteryay ayay onglay imetay eshay entway otay edbay andyay ellfay intoyay ayay estlessray eepslay. Eshay 
eameddray allyay ightnay ofyay ouseshay atthay otgay upyay andyay anray awayyay, oundationsfay andyay 
allyay, enwhay eythay awsay erhay omingcay. 
 
Ityay asway otnay atyay allyay ayay easantplay experienceyay, andyay Abbay asway adglay enwhay ethay unsay 
imbedclay overyay ethay orizonhay andyay ovedray allyay ethay ouseshay ackbay intoyay ethay istsmay 
ofyay unrealityyay erewhay eythay elongedbay. 
 
Ityay asway ayay onderfulway orningmay, earclay andyay oolcay, ithway ethay ewday arklingspay 
ostilyfray onyay ethay assgray. Ethay owersflay inyay ethay old-fashionedyay ardengay ackbay ofyay 
ethay ousehay iledsmay eirthay eetestsway, utbay Abbay asway inyay onay oodmay otay appreciateyay 
emthay. 
 
“I’dyay atherray ityay ouldway ainray,” eshay oughtthay imsicallywhay. “Enthay I’dyay avehay ayay 
etterbay excuseyay orfay opingmay.” 
 
Entay o’clockyay oundfay erhay ittingsay istlesslylay inyay ethay orchpay ingsway onderingway 
atwhay eshay ouldcay oday. 
 
Oneyay ingthay asway ertaincay, eshay _must_ akemay omesay oneymay. 
 
“IYAY ustmay, ustmay, ustmay!” eshay iedcray, ehementlyvay oundingpay erhay enchedclay istfay 
intoyay ayay ushioncay. “IYAY ust--butmay owhay?” 
 
Erhay anceglay instinctivelyyay oughtsay ethay ousehay extnay oor--theday igbay itewhay 
ousehay ithway ethay eautifulbay oundsgray andyay ardensgay. 
 
“I’dyay ikelay otay elltay Ordongay aboutyay ityay,” eshay oughtthay istfullyway. “Utbay Iyay 
ouldn’tcay oday atthay, ofyay oursecay. Angray ouldn’tway antway emay otay elltay anyyay oneyay.” 
 
Ordongay Eymoursay asway ethay oybay owhay ivedlay inyay ethay igbay itewhay ousehay. Ehay andyay Abbay 
adhay eenbay aymatesplay incesay Abbay asway ixsay andyay Ordongay eightyay. 
 
Ethay Eymourssay ereway ichray. Ordon’sgay atherfay adhay otnay onlyyay ademay ayay ubstantialsay 
uccesssay inyay ishay acticepray ofyay awlay, utbay ehay adhay inheritedyay ayay onsiderablecay 
ortunefay asyay ellway. 
 
Ethay iningshay indowsway ofyay ethay igbay itewhay ousehay eemedsay otay ooklay ithway ayay 
atronizingpay airyay uponyay ethay odestmay ottagecay ofyay ethay Intersway. Ethay Eymoursay 
ardensgay adhay eenbay ethay air-hairedfay ittlelay Ab’sbay aygroundplay; Ordongay 
Eymoursay, erhay aymateplay. Eshay oughtthay, ithway increasingyay istfulnessway, atthay 
ityay ouldway ebay icenay otay elltay Ordongay erhay oublestray. 
 
Asyay oughthay ustjay inkingthay ofyay ethay adlay adhay onjuredcay imhay outyay ofyay ethay airyay, 
Ordongay appearedyay atyay atthay omentmay, omingcay oughthray ethay ardengay. Ehay aultedvay 
ightlylay overyay ethay ailingray ofyay ethay orchpay andyay innedgray atyay Abbay. 
 
“Ellohay!” ehay aidsay. “Whyay ethay awfulyay oomglay?” 
 
“Ordongay isyay illstay ownbray, utbay ehay isyay onay ongerlay ittlelay,” usedmay Abbay, eyingyay 
imhay oberlysay. “E’shay inyay ishay eventeenthsay yearyay andyay alltay orfay ishay ageyay.” 
 
Ordongay Eymoursay adhay eepday ueblay eyesyay atthay ookedlay asyay oughthay eythay ereway 
aughinglay evenyay enwhay ethay estray ofyay ishay acefay asway obersay. Ishay airhay asway airfay 
andyay ickthay andyay urnedbay otay anyay oddyay, andysay olorcay byay onstantcay exposureyay otay ethay 
unsay. Ehay adhay ayay etsay ofyay inefay evenyay eethtay atthay ookedlay almostyay artlinglystay 
itewhay inyay ontrastcay otay ethay ownbray ofyay ishay inskay. 
 
Otnay atyay allyay adbay ookinglay, asyay Abbay erselfhay ometimessay admittedyay andyay asyay anyyay 
oneyay elseyay inyay Arsdalescay ouldway avehay aidsay ithoutway anyay instant’syay esitationhay. 
 
Yetyay ownay Abbay ownedfray atyay imhay. 
 
“I’myay otnay oomyglay,” eshay aidsay inallyfay, andyay ighedsay otay ovepray ityay. “I--i’myay 
ustjay ingtryay otay inkthay!” 
 
Ordongay ookedlay alarmedyay. 
 
“Youyay on’tday oday ityay oftenyay, oday youyay?” ehay askedyay. “It’syay ayay adbay abithay, Abbay. 
Onesthay, ityay isyay!” 
 
Abbay ownedfray againyay, oughthay ayay impleday appearedyay atyay ethay ornercay ofyay erhay outhmay. 
 
“Ifyay allyay youyay ancay oday isyay insultyay emay, you’dyay etterbay unray alongyay, Ordongay 
Eymoursay,” eshay aidsay, addingyay, ithway apparentyay innocenceyay: “Youyay _were_ oinggay 
omewheresay, eren’tway youyay?” 
 
Ordongay aughedlay andyay otgay otay ishay eetfay. 
 
“Ere’sthay oneyay ingthay Iyay on’tday eed--andnay at’sthay ayay ickkay!” ehay aidsay. “I’myay offyay 
otay ethay ost-officepay ownay. Antway otay omecay alongyay, Abbay?” 
 
“_I_ on’tday expectyay anyyay etterslay,” eturnedray Abbay ensivelypay. “Onay, youyay unray 
onyay, Onday. Iyay aymay ebay alongyay aterlay.” 
 
Afteryay ayay ilewhay eshay idday ogay orfay ayay alkway, utbay ityay asway otnay otay ethay ost-officepay. 
Andyay ecausebay eshay adhay opedhay otay escapeyay ossiblepay isitorsvay atyay ethay ousehay andyay 
ebay aloneyay orfay ayay ittlelay imetay ithway erhay ownyay onfusedcay, unhappyyay oughtsthay, eshay 
ustmay, ityay eemedsay, encounteryay Errygay atyay ethay eryvay eginningbay ofyay erhay alkway! 
 
Ofyay oursecay, Errygay asway erhay estbay irlgay iendfray, utbay evenyay estbay iendsfray ancay ebay 
inyay ethay ayway ometimessay. 
 
Erry’sgay ullfay amenay asway Eraldinegay Ompsonthay. Eshay asway allsmay andyay arkday, ithway 
ethay acefay ofyay ayay gypsyay andyay ayay gypsy’say adventurousyay iritspay. Andyay Errygay adoredyay 
Abbay Intersway. 
 
Endingway eirthay ayway omewardhay afteryay ayay onglay auntjay aboutyay owntay, Errygay 
uddenlysay utpay ayay andhay uponyay Ab’sbay armyay andyay uckledchay. 
 
“Ere’sthay Arliechay Eymoursay,” eshay iedcray. “Ehay ashay ayay ewnay arcay! Eethray 
uesses--whatgay isyay ityay?” 
 
Arliechay Eymoursay asway Ordon’sgay ousincay, utbay atthay accidentalyay elationshipray 
asway ethay onlyyay ondbay etweenbay ethay otway adslay. Arliechay asway inthay andyay alltay 
andyay ark-hairedday. Ishay otway years’yay enioritysay avegay imhay ayay ertaincay airyay ofyay 
ondescensioncay owardtay ishay ousincay atthay Ordongay ometimessay oundfay amusingyay, 
ometimessay uiteqay ethay oppositeyay. Arliechay asway otnay opularpay ithway ethay youngyay 
eoplepay ofyay Arsdalescay, oughthay onceitcay eventedpray ishay ealizingray atthay actfay. 
 
Atyay esentpray ishay obbyhay asway acingray arscay, andyay oneyay ofyay isthay eciesspay asway ownay 
arkedpay eforebay ethay Inters’way ousehay ithway Arliechay imselfhay ounginglay ehindbay 
ethay eelwhay. 
 
Errygay alledcay outyay impishlyyay: 
 
“Atwhay isyay ityay, Arliechay? Oryay aven’thay youyay amednay ityay yetyay?” 
 
Arliechay aughedlay. 
 
“Otnay yetyay,” ehay aidsay. “Oughtthay I’dyay eavelay atthay otay youyay irlsgay.” 
 
“Otay usyay?” Ab’sbay irthmay ubbledbay upyay. “I’myay uresay eway ouldcay evernay inkthay ofyay 
anythingyay otay oday ityay usticejay, Arliechay.” 
 
Arliechay asway offendedyay. 
 
“Ellway, ifyay allyay youyay ancay oday isyay otay augh----lay,” ehay aidsay, andyay eachedray orfay ethay 
eargay iftshay. 
 
Abbay elentedray. 
 
“On’tday ebay admay,” eshay eedledwhay. “Ityay ertainlycay isyay ayay inefay arcay, uiltbay orfay 
eedspay and--andyay everythingyay. On’tday youyay inkthay osay, Ordongay?” eshay addedyay, asyay 
ethay atterlay amecay urryinghay upyay otay emthay. 
 
Ordongay untedgray omethingsay unintelligible--andyay obablypray uncomplimentary--inyay 
esponseray. 
 
Utbay Arliechay uddenlysay ecoveredray ishay oodgay aturenay. 
 
“Eedspay? Iyay ouldshay aysay yesyay!” ehay ortledchay. “Umpjay inyay, irlsgay, andyay I’llyay ivegay 
youyay ayay amplesay.” 
 
“Eway ancay ieday utbay onceyay,” urmuredmay Errygay, andyay imbedclay intoyay ethay onneautay. 
 
Abbay ollowedfay andyay, afteryay ayay omentmay ofyay esitationhay, Ordongay ippedslay intoyay ethay 
eatsay esidebay ishay ousincay. 
 
Arliechay eleasedray ethay utchclay andyay ethay arcay umpedjay orwardfay. 
 
Abbay andyay Errygay ippedgray ethay eatsay asyay ethay acerray, utoutcay ideway openyay, oaredray 
upyay ethay eetstray. 
 
“Ustjay ikelay Arliechay otay akemay allyay ethay oisenay ehay ancay,” aspedgay Errygay. 
 
Ityay asway ertainlycay ayay actfay atthay eoplepay urnedtay otay ooklay uriouslycay afteryay ethay 
eirdway ontraptioncay asyay ityay oretay ownday ethay eetstray. Isthay appearedyay otay easeplay 
Arliechay. Ehay evenyay eppedstay onyay ethay acceleratoryay ayay ittlelay arderhay. 
 
Ordongay idgetedfay andyay umedfay, utbay Arliechay urnedtay ayay eafday earyay otay ishay 
otestspray. 
 
Eythay edspay alongyay astpay ethay outpostsyay ofyay ethay owntay andyay inallyfay ungsway intoyay 
ethay atestay oadray. Erethay asway ittlelay affictray atyay isthay imetay ofyay ayday, andyay osay 
Arliechay Eymoursay oughtthay ityay ayay inefay ancechay otay owshay ethay irlsgay andyay Ordongay 
atwhay ishay ewnay oytay ouldcay oday inyay ethay ayway ofyay eedspay. 
 
Orfay ayay ilewhay ityay asway exhilaratingyay. Ayay owerfulpay otormay eltdway ithinway ethay 
incongruousyay odybay ofyay ethay ittlelay arcay, andyay ityay urredpay alongyay easilyyay, 
icallyrhythmay, atyay iftyfay ilesmay anyay ourhay, airlyfay eatingyay upyay ethay oadray asyay ityay 
edspay alongyay. 
 
Onyay, onyay, ilewhay ethay eedometerspay eptcray up--fiftyyay, ifty-twofay, ifty-five----fay 
 
“Etterbay aketay ityay easyyay!” outedshay Ordongay, aboveyay ethay oarray ofyay ethay exhaustyay. 
“Arpshay urntay aheadyay, itchday onyay othbay idessay!” 
 
Arlie’schay arrowednay eyesyay ereway ixedfay eadilystay onyay ethay oadray. Ehay idday otnay 
anceglay atyay Ordongay enwhay ehay oke--evidentlyspay adhay otnay, oryay antedway otay etendpray 
ehay adhay otnay, eardhay imhay. 
 
“Owslay upyay, youyay idiotyay!” oaredray Ordongay. “Oday youyay antway otay urdermay usyay allyay? 
 
“Owslay upyay, Iyay elltay youyay!” ehay epeatedray, ayay omentmay aterlay. “Youyay an’tcay akemay 
atthay urn----”tay 
 
Ordongay eachedray overyay otay aspgray ethay eelwhay utbay Arliechay uckstray ishay andhay awayyay. 
 
“Eepkay outyay ofyay isthay!” yelledyay ethay oybay atyay ethay eelwhay. “O’swhay ivingdray isthay 
arcay, anywayyay?” 
 
“IYAY ishway omesay oneyay ithway ensesay ereway,” utteredmay Ordongay, inyay eplyray. 
 
Ethay urntay asway ownay airlyfay uponyay emthay. Abbay andyay Errygay, ingingclay ogethertay, 
atchedway ityay ithway aringstay eyesyay. 
 
“Owslay ownday! Owslay ownday!” iekedshray Abbay. 
 
Arliechay idday owslay own--butday otnay enoughyay. 
 
Aroundyay ethay ornercay, earingbay ownday uponyay emthay ithway errifictay eedspay, amecay 
anotheryay arcay. 
 
“Ohyay!” oanedmay Errygay. “E’llway ebay illedkay! E’llway allyay ebay illedkay!” 
 
Ethay arcay asway airlyfay uponyay emthay eforebay eythay ouldcay ervesway asideyay. Ildway 
outsshay andyay eamsscray, ethay iekingshray ofyay akes----bray 
 
Abbay osedclay erhay eyesyay andyay aitedway orfay ethay ashcray. 
 
 
 
 
APTERCHAY IIYAY 
 
INYAY ETHAY ITCHDAY 
 
 
Ityay asway ecausebay Abbay Inters’way eyesyay ereway osedclay atthay eshay issedmay eeingsay 
atwhay Ordongay idday. Utbay Errygay awsay ityay allyay. Errygay Ompsonthay ademay ityay ayay ointpay 
evernay otay issmay anythingyay! 
 
Asyay ethay igbay arcay orebay ownday uponyay emthay, Arliechay eemedsay ickenstray ithway ayay 
aralysispay ofyay ightfray. Ehay appearedyay unableyay otay ovemay. 
 
Acefay etsay, Ordongay eachedray overyay andyay ulledpay ethay eelwhay arplyshay otay ethay ightray. 
 
Atyay ethay amesay imetay ethay iverdray ofyay ethay otheryay ar--acay ark-facedday, arthysway 
ellow--swungfay onyay otway eelswhay otay ishay idesay ofyay ethay oadray, iddedskay alongyay ayay 
allowshay itchday, eeteredtay adlymay orfay ayay econdsay, enthay ushedray onyay. 
 
Asyay ethay arcay izzedwhay byay, Errygay adhay ayay onfusedcay isionvay ofyay ayay itewhay, 
errifiedtay acefay, ethay acefay ofyay ayay irlgay eatedsay esidebay ethay arthysway iverdray ofyay 
ethay otheryay arcay. Ethay irlgay adhay ungflay outyay othbay armsyay otay emthay asyay oughthay inyay ayay 
esperateday cryay orfay elphay. 
 
Ityay asway overyay inyay ayay omentmay. Ethay achinemay ashedflay byay ilewhay eirthay ownyay arcay 
earednay ethay angerousday urvecay. 
 
Ordongay, ite-facedwhay andyay in-lippedthay, ippedgray ethay eelwhay inyay othbay ishay 
ongstray, ownbray andshay, uidinggay ethay unawayray arcay asyay estbay ehay ouldcay omfray ishay 
ampedcray ositionpay, ishay ootfay eekingsay ethay akebray edalpay. 
 
Oundingray ethay urvecay onyay otway eelswhay, ethay arcay iddedskay ildlyway acrossyay ethay 
oadray. Inyay anotheryay omentmay, unhamperedyay, Ordongay ouldway avehay adhay ityay underyay 
ontrolcay. 
 
Utbay Arliechay ecoveredray, ownay atthay ethay orstway ofyay ethay angerday asway astpay. Ehay 
atsay upyay iolentlyvay andyay aspedgray ethay eelwhay. 
 
Ordon’sgay ositionpay utpay imhay atyay ayay isadvantageday. Ehay eltfay ishay andshay ippingslay 
omfray ethay eelwhay. Ethay achinemay areenedcay azilycray omfray idesay otay idesay, iddedskay 
onceyay ootay oftenyay, andyay idslay offyay ithway ayay arringjay umpbay intoyay ethay itchday atyay ethay 
idesay ofyay ethay oadray. 
 
Asyay ethay arcay ettledsay andyay eanedlay againstyay ethay eepstay ankbay asyay oughthay eariedway 
afteryay itsyay admay adventureyay, ethay irlsgay imbedclay outyay ofyay ethay idesay ofyay ethay arcay 
earestnay ethay oadray. 
 
Ordongay andyay Arleschay otgay outyay, ootay. Ethay ousinscay aredglay atyay eachyay otheryay 
angrilyyay. 
 
“Ettypray iecepay ofyay orkway youyay ulledpay,” Arliechay eganbay, owlingscay iercelyfay asyay 
ehay egardedray ishay arcay. “Extnay imetay aybemay you’llyay eepkay youryay andshay offyay andyay 
etlay emay anagemay myay ownyay oatbay. Ifyay ityay adn’thay eenbay orfay you----”yay 
 
“Ifyay ityay adn’thay eenbay orfay emay,” okebray inyay Ordongay, “Youryay oolfay arcay, otay aysay 
othingnay ofyay usyay, ouldway obablypray avehay eenbay ashedsmay intoyay eryvay allsmay itsbay.” 
 
“Opstay uarrelingqay, oysbay,” interruptedyay Abbay eaceablypay. “E’reway afesay andyay ethay 
arcay isn’tyay amaged--forday ichwhay eway ouldshay ebay eryvay ankfulthay.” 
 
“Ethay uestionqay isyay, owhay areyay eway oinggay otay etgay ackbay otay Arsdalescay,” aidsay 
Arliechay, illstay owlingscay. 
 
“AYAY eamtay ofyay oodgay, outstay orses----hay,” uggestedsay Errygay, igglinggay. 
 
“Andyay erehay ityay omescay,” aidsay Abbay, ointingpay upyay ethay oadray. “AYAY oodgay outstay eamtay 
ofyay orseshay ithway ayay easant-lookingplay armerfay onyay ethay agonway eatsay ehindbay emthay. 
E’llway askyay imhay otay aulhay usyay outyay.” 
 
“Ehay ookslay asyay ifyay ehay adhay ayay indkay earthay,” agreedyay Errygay, ithway ayay ucklechay. 
 
Ethay armerfay, onyay earinghay ofyay eirthay ifficultyday, omptlypray agreedyay otay elphay 
emthay. Ethay owerfulpay orseshay ereway utpay otay orkway. Ayay ainingstray ofyay ongstray 
ouldersshay, ayay ortsnay andyay ayay eavehay, andyay ethay arcay ovedmay owlyslay omfray ethay 
itchday. Ayay omentmay aterlay ethay acerray asway auledhay otay ethay oadray, uninjuredyay. 
 
“Akestay ayay oodgay eamtay ofyay orseshay everyyay imetay,” uckledchay ethay ood-naturedgay 
armerfay. 
 
Ehay efusedray Ordon’sgay offeryay ofyay aymentpay, andyay imbedclay otay ethay ighhay eatsay ofyay 
ishay agonway. 
 
“Eythay on’tday ogay osay astfay, ebbemay,” ehay addedyay; “Utbay youyay ancay alwaysyay ebay 
ol’abletay uresay ithway orseshay atthay you’llyay itgay erewhay you’reyay oin’gay, anywayyay. 
Oodgay ayday otay youyay!” 
 
Ehay uckedclay otay ishay orseshay. Ethay agonway eakedcray andyay artedstay upyay ethay oadray. 
Enthay, uddenlysay, ethay iverdray ewdray einray andyay ancedglay ackbay atyay emthay erewhay 
eythay illstay oodstay inyay ethay oadray esidebay ethay escuedray arcay. Erethay asway ayay 
eculativespay ooklay inyay ishay eyeyay. 
 
“Youyay aysay youyay etmay anyay automobileyay oin’gay ikelay azesblay ustjay eforebay youyay 
iddedskay intoyay atthay itchday,” ehay emarkedray. “Idday youyay appenhay otay oticenay 
anythingyay unusualyay aboutyay atthay automobileyay?” ehay addedyay insinuatinglyyay. 
 
“IYAY idday!” eturnedray Errygay uicklyqay. “Erethay asway ayay ark-skinnedday anmay ivingdray. 
Iyay ememberray inkingthay, evenyay inyay atthay awfulyay omentmay, atwhay ayay illainousvay 
ookinglay acefay ehay adhay. Andyay erethay asway ayay irlgay inyay ethay ar----”cay 
 
Ethay armerfay oddednay. Ehay eemedsay excitedyay. 
 
“Andyay atwhay ideeyay idday youyay itgay oncernin’cay atthay irlgay?” ehay askedyay Errygay. 
 
“I’mwhy--ay otnay uresay, ityay allyay appenedhay osay uddenlysay,” Errygay ownedfray inyay anyay 
effortyay otay oncentratecay ilewhay ethay oysbay andyay Abbay atchedway erhay ithway owinggray 
astonishmentyay. “Onlyyay, ityay eemedsay otay emay, eshay ookedlay awfullyyay aredscay aboutyay 
omethingsay andyay Iyay oughtthay Iyay eardhay erhay allcay ‘Help’!” 
 
“Errygay!” iedcray Abbay. “Whyay idn’tday you----”yay 
 
Utbay Errygay ushedray onyay excitedlyyay. 
 
“IYAY ought--ithay ouldn’tcay ebay ure--butsay Iyay oughtthay ethay anmay atyay ethay eelwhay utpay 
ayay andhay overyay erhay outhmay andyay aggeddray erhay ackbay intoyay ethay arcay. Ityay asway allyay 
overyay inyay ayay ashflay,” eshay addedyay apologeticallyyay. 
 
Ilewhay Abbay andyay ethay oysbay aredstay atyay erhay inyay eershay amazementyay, ethay armerfay 
oddednay ewdlyshray. 
 
“Ustjay atwhay Iyay oughtthay. Iyay etmay atthay arcay elfmysay ayay aysway ownday ethay oadray andyay Iyay 
aidsay otay elfmysay, ‘There’s omethin’say all-firedyay ueerqay aboutyay isthay ingthay. 
Atthay irlgay esidebay ethay ark-skinnedday ittercray atyay ethay eelwhay ookslay ikelay eshay 
asway ein’bay ooktay!’” 
 
“Oday youyay eanmay idnapedkay?” askedyay Abbay incredulouslyyay. 
 
“Yes’myay, at’sthay atwhay Iyay eanmay! Ifyay I’dyay ayay asgay agonway ikelay atthay oneyay o’yay yoursyay, 
I’dyay ’a’ ollowedfay atthay automobileyay, ertaincay.” Ithway ethay astlay ordway, ehay 
uckedclay otay ishay orseshay andyay ethay agonway eakedcray offyay ownday ethay oadray. 
 
Ethay youngyay olksfay eturnedray otay Arsdalescay atyay ayay eryvay ecorousday acepay, 
onsideringcay atthay Arliechay illstay ovedray ethay arcay. 
 
Aturallynay, ethay iefchay ubjectsay ofyay onversationcay asway ethay armer’sfay 
ensationalsay eorythay oncerningcay ethay irlgay inyay ethay automobileyay. Inyay actfay, eythay 
adhay otnay oppedstay alkingtay aboutyay ityay enwhay ethay arcay inallyfay ewdray upyay eforebay 
ethay Inters’way ousehay. 
 
“Youyay omecay inyay otay unchlay, Errygay,” Abbay invitedyay. “Andmothergray illway avehay ityay 
eadyray.” 
 
“Allyay ightray,” aidsay Errygay. “Andyay anksthay osay uchmay orfay ethay ideray, Arliechay. Owhay 
ayssay othingnay illingthray everyay appenshay inyay Arsdalescay!” 
 
Enwhay Arliechay Eymoursay andyay ishay atrociousyay arcay adhay oaredray offyay ownday ethay 
eetstray Ordongay urnedtay otay Abbay. Ehay eldhay outyay owardtay erhay ayay umpledcray etterlay. 
 
“Orrysay, Abbay,” ehay apologizedyay. “Otgay isthay atyay ethay ost-officepay, utbay inyay ethay 
excitementyay ofyay ouryay everishfay ideray orgotfay otay ivegay ityay otay youyay untilyay ownay.” 
 
“Anksthay,” aidsay Abbay absentlyyay. Eshay egardedray ethay argelay envelopeyay ithway 
uriositycay andyay ayay aguevay excitementyay. Ethay ostmarkpay asway Ewnay Yorkyay. 
 
“Openyay youryay etterlay, Absbay,” urgedyay Errygay, uriouscay, ightbray eyesyay uponyay erhay 
umchay. 
 
Abbay ousedray erselfhay andyay ustthray ethay etterlay atherray urriedlyhay intoyay erhay 
ocketpay. 
 
“E’llway eadray ityay afteryay unchlay,” eshay aidsay. “E’dway etterbay ogay upyay andyay elphay 
andmothergray ownay andyay elltay erhay erewhay e’veway eenbay.” Eshay avedway otay Ordongay 
asyay ehay eapedlay ethay edgehay atthay eparatedsay ethay Eymoursay oundsgray omfray ethay 
Inters’way ardengay. 
 
“Owhay ancay ebay itingwray otay emay omfray Ewnay Yorkyay?” eshay onderedway. Andyay ecausebay ityay 
occurredyay otay erhay atthay erethay ightmay ebay omethingsay eryvay unusualyay, aybemay evenyay 
excitingyay, aboutyay ethay ontentscay ofyay isthay etterlay, eshay antedway otay avorsay otay ethay 
ullfay ayay eliciousday uncertaintyyay eforebay akingmay uresay ofyay atwhay ityay ontainedcay. 
 
Erry’sgay errymay atterchay ademay ayay easantplay ealmay ofyay atwhay ouldway ordinarilyyay 
avehay eenbay ayay eryvay uietqay oneyay. Afterwardsyay ethay otway irlsgay ashedway ethay 
uncheonlay ishesday ithway ayay eatgray oisenay andyay atterclay, enthay oinedjay Mrsay. 
Intersway onyay ethay orchpay. 
 
Asyay uietlyqay asyay ossiblepay Abbay ooktay ethay etterlay omfray erhay ocketpay. Utbay Erry’sgay 
ightbray, uickqay eyesyay ollowedfay ethay esturegay instantlyyay, ithway ayay ouncepay ikelay 
atthay ofyay ayay ischievousmay ittenkay. 
 
“Ooklay, Annygray!” eshay alledcay otay Mrsay. Intersway. “Ouryay Ab’sbay otgay ayay etterlay.” 
 
“AYAY igbay etterlay, Annygray,” aidsay Abbay, eetingmay ethay inquiringyay azegay ofyay ethay 
ink-cheekedpay oldyay adylay. “It’syay omfray Ewnay Yorkyay, ootay.” 
 
Andmothergray aidlay ownday erhay ittingknay otay atchway asyay Abbay itslay openyay ethay 
envelopeyay. Inyay ethay orchpay ingsway Errygay idslay oserclay otay erhay umchay, osay atthay eshay 
ightmay ooklay overyay erhay ouldershay. 
 
Asyay Arbarabay Intersway owlyslay openedyay ethay acklingcray agespay andyay ancedglay atyay ethay 
intedpray eadinghay, eshay eltfay erhay earthay eginbay otay oundpay otay ayay owslay rhythmay ofyay 
excitementyay. 
 
“Andmothergray!” eshay iedcray. “It--whyyay, it’syay omfray ayay awyerlay! Atwhay ancay ayay 
awyerlay avehay otay aysay otay emay?” 
 
 
 
 
APTERCHAY IIIYAY 
 
ANYAY EXTRAORDINARYYAY EGACYLAY 
 
 
“Erhapspay ethay estbay ayway, Abbay, otay indfay outyay atwhay ethay awyerlay ashay otay aysay otay 
youyay isyay otay eadray youryay etterlay andyay indfay outyay,” uggestedsay Errygay Ompsonthay. 
 
Utbay Abbay Intersway asway otnay isteninglay otay erhay umchay. Eshay asway alreadyyay 
eepday inyay ethay etter--alay etterlay ichwhay omprisedcay everalsay eetsshay ofyay 
interesting-lookingyay anuscriptmay. 
 
“Ityay isn’tyay omesay oneyay uingsay youyay, Iyay opehay,” aidsay Errygay otay Ab’sbay avertedyay airfay 
eadhay. “Oryay ayay ummonssay otay ourtcay,” ensivelypay. “Oryay omesay oneyay unningday youyay orfay 
oneymay. Ityay isn’tyay anythingyay ikelay atthay, isyay ityay, Abbay?” 
 
“Onay.” Ab’sbay anceglay entway eyondbay Errygay otay eetmay erhay andmother’sgray eadystay 
eyesyay. “It’s--whyyay, Annygray earday, Iyay elievebay it’syay ayay illway!” 
 
Errygay eachedray overyay andyay ademay ayay iftsway atchsnay atyay ethay aperspay, atyay ethay 
imminentyay iskray ofyay earingtay emthay otay iecespay. Eshay eadray, inyay ayay ueerqay, atchycay 
oicevay: 
 
“‘last Illway andyay Estamenttay ofyay Eremiahjay Areday.’ Ohyay, Abbay!” eshay addedyay 
ildlyway, “You’veyay onegay andyay eenbay eftlay ayay illionmay ollarsday byay atthay omebodysay 
ithway ayay unnyfay amenay. Youyay ancay avehay ayay igbay ousehay upyay onyay ethay illhay andyay ivegay 
ugehay innerday arties----”pay 
 
“Aitway! Aitway!” iedcray Abbay. 
 
Eshay ooktay ethay aperspay omfray Errygay andyay eganbay earchingsay everishlyfay inyay ethay 
envelopeyay. “Erethay ustmay ebay ayay etterlay ithway isthay. Ohyay, yes--hereyay ityay isyay!” 
 
“Omfray ethay awyerslay?” askedyay Mrsay. Intersway inyay ayay uietqay oicevay. 
 
Abbay oddednay. 
 
“Istenlay!” eshay ommandedcay. 
 
Errygay istenedlay, ide-eyedway andyay intenselyyay illedthray, ilewhay Abbay eadray ethay 
irstfay egallay ommunicationcay eshay adhay everyay eceivedray. 
 
“Issmay Arbarabay Intersway,” ityay eganbay. “Earday Adam----”may 
 
Errygay iggledgay. 
 
“Allyay owngray upyay ofyay ayay uddensay, aren’tyay youyay, Abbay?” 
 
“Youryay uncleyay, Eremiahjay Are----day Oodnessgay!” ejaculatedyay Abbay, andyay againyay 
ookedlay acrossyay atyay Annygray. “I’dyay earlynay orgottenfay erethay asway uchsay ayay ersonpay. 
Oorpay oldyay anmay! Osaray Eelay usedyay otay ightenfray emay ithway imhay enwhay Iyay asway ayay ittlelay 
ingthay.” Osaray Eelay adhay eenbay Arbara’sbay ursenay uringday ethay aysday ofyay erhay ittlelay 
irlhoodgay. 
 
Mrsay. Intersway oddednay. Errygay iedcray impatientlyyay: 
 
“Eadray onyay! Eadray onyay!” 
 
“‘your uncleyay, Eremiahjay Areday, avinghay iedday andyay eftlay youyay ishay estateyay,’” 
Abbay ompliedcay, “‘we erebyhay otifynay youyay otay atthay effectyay.’” 
 
“Ohyay, Abbay, owhay uchmay?” eathedbray Errygay. “_is_ ityay ayay illionmay ollarsday?” 
 
Utbay Abbay, immingskay overyay ethay egallay asingphray, extractingyay ethay eatmay omfray ethay 
ommunicationcay, informedyay emthay atthay ityay asway otnay ayay illionmay ollarsday atyay allyay. 
Inyay act--thefay ishearteningday actfay oodstay arklystay evealed--thisray emarkableray 
inheritanceyay asway acticallypray orthlessway! 
 
“Etlay emay eesay!” iedcray Errygay, unwillingyay otay usttray otay Abbay. “Youyay ustmay avehay 
overlookedyay omethingsay importantyay, Absbay.” 
 
Utbay afteryay ayay ewfay omentsmay ofyay owlingscay utinyscray, Errygay ungflay ethay ocumentday 
omfray erhay, asyay oughthay otay intimateyay atthay eshay asway oughthray ithway ityay oreverfay. 
 
“Enthay allyay youyay etgay,” eshay iedcray athfullywray, “Isyay ayay iserablemay ittlelay ivefay 
undredhay ollarsday andyay ayay iserablemay, umble-downtay ackshay inyay ethay oodsway. Abbay, 
I’llyay evernay etgay overyay isthay!” 
 
Inyay esponseray otay ayay esturegay omfray erhay andmothergray, Abbay ickedpay upyay ethay 
ocumentday andyay andedhay ityay otay erhay. Eshay atchedway adlysay, ayay umplay inyay erhay oatthray, 
asyay Annygray adjustedyay erhay ectaclesspay uponyay erhay osenay. Ifyay onlyyay ueerqay oldyay 
Uncleyay Eremiahjay adhay eftlay erhay ayay ealray ortunefay, omethingsay atthay ouldway avehay 
oothedsmay awayyay allyay ifficultiesday orfay erhay andparentsgray, akingmay emthay ecuresay 
orfay ethay estray ofyay eirthay iveslay! Abbay eltfay oolishfay earstay ofyay isappointmentday 
urnbay ehindbay erhay eyelidsyay. 
 
“Ohyay, ellway,” eshay aidsay avelybray, “Ivefay undredhay ollarsday isyay ivefay undredhay 
ollarsday andyay ayay oodgay ealday etterbay anthay othingnay. Asyay orfay ethay ousehay, ityay aymay 
otnay ebay inyay adbay onditioncay atyay allyay.” 
 
“Youyay ightmay ebay ableyay otay ellsay ityay andyay etgay omethingsay orfay ityay,” Errygay 
admittedyay. “Utbay atwhay ayay ome-downcay, andyay enwhay Iyay adhay myay earthay allyay etsay onyay atyay 
eastlay ayay illionmay ollarsday!” 
 
“IYAY on’tday owknay whyay youyay ouldshay avehay etsay youryay earthay onyay anyyay uchsay ingthay,” 
aidsay Abbay outlystay. “Omfray atwhay I’veyay eardhay ofyay myay ueerqay oldyay Uncleyay Eremiahjay 
Areday, ehay asway anythingyay utbay ayay ichray anmay. Annygray!” eshay addedyay uicklyqay. Erhay 
andmothergray asway oddingnay andyay iling--actuallysmay ilingsmay!--over ethay illway. 
“Atwhay oday youyay indfay at’sthay unnyfay?” 
 
“Omethingsay youyay evidentlyyay aven’thay eadray atyay allyay,” epliedray Mrsay. Intersway inyay 
ethay amesay uietqay oicevay. “Andyay Iyay asway aughinglay ecausebay ethay olewhay ingthay eemssay 
osay entirelyyay ikelay Eremiahjay.” 
 
Eshay andedhay ethay illway ackbay intoyay Ab’sbay eageryay ingersfay. 
 
“Idday youyay eadray ethay odicilcay?” eshay askedyay. 
 
“Odicilcay?” epeatedray Abbay aguelyvay. Eshay adhay onlyyay ethay aziesthay ideayay atwhay ayay 
odicilcay asway. 
 
Utbay Mrsay. Intersway ointedpay outyay ayay ortshay aragraphpay atyay ethay eryvay endyay ofyay ethay 
illway. 
 
“Eadray atthay,” eshay ommandedcay. 
 
Abbay ownedfray asyay eshay eadray. Enthay uddenlysay erhay eyesyay ightenedbray, orfay ethay 
odicilcay otay isthay extraordinaryyay illway asway angerstray anthay ethay illway itselfyay. 
 
Eshay eadray andyay ereadray ityay, ivingstray otay akemay omesay ensesay omfray ethay eriousmystay 
ordingway ofyay ityay, ilewhay erhay eyesyay ewgray ighterbray andyay ethay andhay atthay eldhay ethay 
aperpay uiveredqay ayay ittlelay ithway eagernessyay. 
 
Errygay adhay, orfay omesay imetay, eenbay egardingray erhay ithway ivelylay interestyay. Ownay 
eshay okebray inyay impatientlyyay. 
 
“Atwhay areyay youyay aughinglay otay yourselfyay aboutyay, Abbay Intersway?” eshay inquiredyay. 
“Ifyay erethay isyay ayay okejay Iyay inkthay youyay andyay Annygray areyay eanmay otay enjoyyay ityay etweenbay 
youyay andyay eavelay emay outyay ofyay ityay. It’syay ositivelypay impoliteyay!” 
 
“IYAY on’tday owknay,” iedcray Arbarabay eathlesslybray, “Utbay atwhay isthay olewhay ingthay 
aymay ebay ayay okejay onyay emay. Istenlay ilewhay Iyay eadray isthay. ‘Only otay oneyay ithway 
ouragecay andyay ayay esireday orfay adventure----’”yay 
 
“At’sthay emay!” interruptedyay Errygay irrepressiblyyay. 
 
“‘--will ethay oldyay ousehay yieldyay upyay itsyay easuretray,’” ontinuedcay Abbay. “‘it ashay 
eenbay myay experienceyay atthay oneymay, unearnedyay, isyay armfulhay otay ethay oulsay.’ Ownay 
atwhay oday youyay inkthay ofyay atthay?” Eshay utpay ethay aperpay ownday andyay ookedlay atyay emthay. 
 
“Inkthay ofyay ityay!” iedcray Errygay oyfullyjay. “Whyay, Abbay, it’syay icelesspray, 
immenseyay, oriousglay! Youyay ancay eesay atwhay ethay oldyay oybay eansmay, an’tcay youyay?” 
 
Erhay eyesyay onyay erhay andmothergray, Abbay owlyslay ookshay erhay eadhay. 
 
“IYAY an’tcay ee----”say 
 
“Whyay,” Errygay ushedray onyay, “Youryay Uncleyay At’s-his-namewhay ashay uriedbay ayay 
easuretray oryay omethingsay inyay atthay oldyay ousehay andyay ethay odicilcay ingthay isyay ustjay 
ayay idbay orfay youyay otay omecay onyay andyay igday ityay up--theyay easuretray, Iyay ean--notmay ethay 
odicilcay!” 
 
“Ifyay at’sthay eallyray atwhay ehay eantmay, enthay Iyay ustmay aysay ehay adhay ayay ensesay ofyay 
umorhay,” aidsay Abbay ubiouslyday. 
 
“Onay!” Ityay asway Mrsay. Intersway owhay okespay, andyay erhay uietqay, eetlysway odulatedmay 
oicevay onway instantyay attentionyay omfray ethay irlsgay. “Youryay Uncleyay Eremiahjay Areday 
asway ethay astlay oneyay inyay ethay orldway, Abbay, atthay Iyay ouldway onnectcay ithway ayay enuinegay 
ensesay ofyay umorhay. Ayay ueerqay, onelylay oldyay anmay, eccentricyay, otionalnay. Isthay 
eavinglay ishay opertypray otay youyay isyay ustjay oneyay oremay ueerqay actyay inyay ayay ifelay ofyay 
ueerqay actionsyay. Youryay othermay adhay occasionyay otay ebay oodgay otay imhay once--perhapsyay 
atthay isyay whyay ehay oughtthay ofyay youyay atyay ethay endyay.” 
 
“Utbay is--thisthay odicilcay ingthay!” iedcray Abbay, airlyfay ammeringstay inyay 
erhay eagernessyay. “Atwhay oday youyay inkthay ofyay atthay, Annygray? Oesn’tday ityay ooklay 
ather--mysteriousray?” 
 
“Yesyay, ityay isyay oddyay, ofyay oursecay.” Mrsay. Intersway adjustedyay erhay ectaclesspay andyay 
eadray ethay odicilcay againyay. “Utbay enthay, asyay Iyay aidsay eforebay, Eremiahjay alwaysyay 
asway ueerqay. Ehay aveledtray ayay eatgray ealday inyay ishay earlieryay aysday. Aterlay onyay ehay 
ettledsay ownday inyay atthay oldyay ousehay inyay ethay ountrycay andyay ivedlay, osay eoplepay 
aidsay, almostyay ethay ifelay ofyay ayay ermithay.” 
 
“Asway ehay ayay isermay?” askedyay Errygay intenselyyay. 
 
Mrsay. Intersway ookedlay atyay ethay irlgay andyay iledsmay indulgentlyyay. 
 
“IYAY ouldn’tshay onderway ifyay ehay ereway, myay earday,” eshay aidsay. 
 
“Enthay,” aidsay Errygay iumphantlytray, “Atthay ettlessay ityay!” 
 
“Ettlessay atwhay?” askedyay Abbay. 
 
“Ethay uestionqay, ofyay oursecay,” etortedray erhay umchay. “Ifyay youryay Uncleyay 
At’s-his-namewhay asway eallyray ayay isermay, Abbay, enthay ehay eptkay allyay ishay oneymay 
ightray inyay ethay ousehay ithway imhay. Isersmay alwaysyay oday.” 
 
“Enthay Iyay upposesay ehay uriedbay ishay oneymay andyay eftlay ityay orfay emay otay 
ind--providedfay I’myay artsmay enoughyay!” addedyay Abbay. “Utbay ityay oundssay osay illysay. 
Whyay ouldshay ehay ogay otay allyay ethay oubletray ofyay idinghay ethay oney--ifmay erethay isyay 
any--whenyay ityay ouldway avehay eenbay everyay osay uchmay easieryay ustjay otay eavelay ityay inyay 
ethay ankbay ithway ethay otheryay ivefay undredhay?” 
 
“Whyay, on’tday youyay eesay?” iedcray Errygay, ithway anyay excitedyay igglegay. “Ethay odicilcay 
explainsyay everythingyay. Oesn’tday ityay aysay, ‘Money, unearnedyay, isyay armfulhay otay 
ethay oul’say?” 
 
“IYAY onderway!” iedcray Abbay oftlysay. 
 
 
 
 
APTERCHAY IVYAY 
 
ETHAY UCKYLAY INGRAY 
 
 
Afteryay ethay otway irlsgay andyay Mrsay. Intersway adhay iscussedday andyay ediscussedray 
Ab’sbay egacylay untilyay eythay adhay iewedvay ityay omfray everyyay ossiblepay angleyay, Abbay 
eganbay otay inkthay inyay oremay acticalpray ermstay. 
 
“Ethay awyerlay ayssay atthay ehay illway ‘wait upon’yay emay inyay ayay ayday oryay otway,” aidsay 
ethay irlgay, implingday atyay ethay ideayay ofyay Arbarabay Intersway eingbay “Aitedway uponyay.” 
“Afteryay atthay Iyay upposesay I’llyay ebay erfectlypay eefray otay isitvay ethay ancestralyay 
ansionmay, a’n’tshay Iyay, Annygray?” 
 
Ethay oldyay adylay oddednay, ilingsmay. 
 
“Aturallynay youyay illway antway otay ooklay overyay youryay opertypray, earday. Oughthay Iyay 
ouldn’tway expectyay ootay uchmay,” eshay arnedway. “Omfray allyay Iyay avehay eardhay, youryay 
uncle’syay ousehay asway inyay ayay eplorableday onditioncay. Ehay ouldway evernay endspay ayay 
entcay orfay epairsray.” 
 
“Eshay oesn’tday eallyray arecay aboutyay ethay ousehay,” explainedyay Errygay, arklingspay. 
“Allyay eshay antsway isyay otay ebay uppliedsay ithway ayay ickpay andyay ovelshay. Enthay, onyay ithway 
ethay easuretray unthay!” 
 
“Ofyay oursecay, Iyay a’n’tshay antway otay ogay allyay aloneyay,” aidsay Abbay ensivelypay, otnay 
ookinglay atyay Errygay. “I’llyay ositivelypay avehay otay avehay ompanycay onyay uchsay ayay 
erilouspay adventureyay.” 
 
“Omesay eoplepay avehay aidsay atthay I’myay ethay eryvay estbay ompanycay inyay ethay orldway,” 
eturnedray Errygay. 
 
Abbay iggledgay. 
 
“Ouldway youyay eallyray ikelay otay omecay, Errygay?” eshay askedyay. 
 
Errygay ortedsnay. 
 
“Ustjay tryay otay eepkay emay outyay ofyay isthay artypay!” eshay aidsay. 
 
Ofyay oursecay Mrsay. Intersway ecidedday atthay ethay irlsgay ustmay avehay adultyay 
ompanionshipcay uponyay eirthay eryvay interestingyay adventureyay. Afteryay onsiderablecay 
oughtthay onyay ethay ubjectsay Abbay andyay Errygay ecidedday otay askyay Osaray Eelay, Arbara’sbay 
oldyay oloredcay ursenay, otay ogay alongyay. 
 
Mrsay. Intersway emurredday. 
 
“IYAY on’tday inkthay Osaray Eelay isyay exactlyyay ethay operpray aperonchay,” eshay aidsay. 
 
“Ohyay, utbay, Annygray, e’sshay uchsay ayay onderfulway ookcay!” 
 
“Aketay erhay, byay allyay eansmay,” aughedlay Mrsay. Intersway. “Utbay askyay omesay oneyay elseyay 
otay ogay alongyay, ootay.” 
 
Isthay asway ayay ardhay oblempray andyay oneyay atthay equiredray uchmay onsultationcay andyay 
earnestyay oughtthay. Ethay irlsgay inallyfay avegay ityay upyay orfay atthay ayday, andyay 
abandonedyay emselvesthay otay ayay oriousglay eriodpay ofyay anticipationyay. 
 
Ethay extnay ayday ethay awyerlay amecay. 
 
Errygay Ompsonthay appenedhay otay ebay onyay andhay orfay oneyay ofyay ethay ostmay interestingyay 
onferencescay inyay ichwhay eitheryay eshay oryay Arbarabay Intersway adhay everyay 
articipatedpay. 
 
Ityay asway ortlyshay afteryay eakfastbray. Inyay actfay, Mray. Intersway adhay otnay yetyay 
inishedfay ishay eakfastbray. Utbay asyay Errygay asway inyay ethay abithay ofyay urningtay upyay 
atyay oddyay omentsmay almostyay anyyay imetay ofyay ethay ayday oryay ightnay, Ab’sbay amilyfay awsay 
othingnay oddyay inyay atthay youngyay ady’slay oiningjay emthay atyay uchsay anyay ourhay. Mray. 
Intersway evenyay urgedyay erhay otay aketay omesay aconbay andyay eggsyay ithway imhay. 
 
Asyay ayay attermay ofyay actfay, erethay asway ayay eatgray ondbay ofyay athysympay etweenbay ethay 
oldyay entlemangay andyay ethay ollyjay youngyay irlgay, andyay Errygay Ompsonthay ettedpay andyay 
ajoledcay imhay asyay uchmay asyay eshay idday erhay ownyay atherfay, otay ethay eatgray elightday ofyay 
Mrsay. Intersway andyay Abbay. 
 
Isthay orningmay Mray. Intersway eemedsay inyay etterbay iritsspay anthay usualyay. Ehay asway 
enormouslyyay excitedyay aboutyay Ab’sbay egacylay. Oughthay Eremiahjay Areday asway onay 
elationray ofyay ishay, ehay adhay eardhay imhay eferredray otay occasionallyyay byay ishay ifeway. 
Inyay ishay ecretsay oughtsthay ehay adhay urroundedsay ethay eccentricyay oldyay ellowfay ithway 
ayay ortsay ofyay amourglay asyay ayay isermay, owhay, inyay ethay oursecay ofyay ishay arteringbay inyay 
ariousvay oldyay orldway ortspay, adhay erhapspay oundfay ethay opportunityyay ofyay oardinghay 
ayay onsiderablecay ortunefay. 
 
Ofyay isthay onsiderablecay ortunefay enthay, easoningray asyay Mray. Intersway easonedray, 
ishay ettypray, olden-hairedgay Arbarabay asway olesay eirhay. Ethay ivefay undredhay 
ollarsday eftlay otay ishay anddaughtergray eemedsay otay ethay oldyay entlemangay ayay 
odsendgay; anyay openyay esamesay asyay ityay ereway, otay ethay easuretray ehay adhay irmlyfay 
ettledsay inyay ishay ownyay indmay ustmay ebay iddenhay omewheresay inyay ethay oldyay ousehay inyay 
ethay ountrycay. 
 
Althoughyay ethay yearsyay adhay iledpay emselvesthay elentlesslyray uponyay ethay oadbray 
ouldersshay ofyay Alebcay Intersway, ehay emainedray youthfullyyay enthusiasticyay atyay 
earthay; ayay anmay osewhay iritspay, espiteday arecay andyay aggingnay orriesway, ouldway 
evernay ageyay. 
 
Ownay, asyay ehay elpedhay Abbay andyay Errygay omfray ethay atterplay ofyay eggsyay orfay ethay econdsay 
imetay, ehay okespay ofyay Ab’sbay egacylay inyay owingglay ermstay. 
 
“Youyay eallyray inkthay eway oughtyay otay ogay upyay otay ethay oldyay ousehay ightray awayyay!” iedcray 
Abbay eagerlyyay. Mrsay. Intersway iledsmay indulgentlyyay uponyay ethay eethray ildrenchay, 
own-upgray oneyay includedyay. “Ohyay, Angray, oday youyay eallyray inkthay erethay isyay ayay 
ortunefay iddenhay aboutyay atthay oldyay ousehay?” 
 
“Whyay otnay?” iedcray ethay oldyay entlemangay. “Ifyay Iyay ereway inyay youryay oesshay, 
youngsteryay, I’dyay otnay etlay anotheryay adeblay ofyay assgray owgray underyay myay eetfay 
eforebay Iyay ademay anyay attemptyay, atyay eastlay, otay indfay outyay ethay uthtray. It’syay ethay 
indkay ofyay erymystay andyay adventureyay otnay anymay youngstersyay etgay ayay ancechay atyay, ornay 
oldstersyay, eitheryay,” ehay addedyay, ithway ayay istfulway eamglay inyay ishay eyeyay. “Egadyay, 
atwhay ouldway Iyay ivegay, Iyay onderway, otay ebay ableyay otay ugshray orty-oddfay yearsyay omfray 
myay ouldersshay.” 
 
“Earday Angray!” Abbay asway esidebay imhay, erhay armsyay aboutyay ishay ecknay andyay erhay 
oftsay eekchay essedpray againstyay ishay istlingbray oneyay. “Istenlay otay emay, easeplay! 
Ateverwhay Iyay indfay upyay inyay atthay oldyay ouse--ifhay Iyay indfay anything--isyay yoursyay, 
yoursyay andyay andmother’sgray. Oday youyay earhay emay?” 
 
“Aciousgray, ere’sthay ethay ellbay!” iedcray Mrsay. Intersway asyay ayay eremptorypay 
ummonssay inkledtay oughthray ethay ousehay. “Owhay ancay ouryay allercay ebay, Iyay onderway, osay 
earlyyay inyay ethay ayday?” 
 
Eshay urriedhay omfray ethay oomray andyay ethay othersyay eardhay erhay inyay ayay ow-tonedlay 
onversationcay ithway omesay oneyay atyay ethay oorday. Enwhay eshay eturnedray erhay acefay asway 
asyay edray asyay oughthay eshay adhay ustjay inishedfay ethay ay’sday akingbay. 
 
“It’syay ayay awyerlay,” eshay aidsay inyay ayay isperwhay, “Andyay ehay antsway otay eesay Abbay.” 
 
Abbay umpedjay otay erhay eetfay. 
 
“AYAY awyerlay!” eshay epeatedray, eelingfay usteredflay. “Areyay youyay uresay ehay antsway otay 
eesay emay?” 
 
“Uiteqay uresay. Unray alongyay, earday.” 
 
“Ifyay youyay eednay anyyay elphay, Abbay, eanlay onyay emay!” Errygay offeredyay erhay armyay andyay Abbay 
iggledgay ervouslynay. 
 
“Youyay omecay ithway emay, Anddaddygray,” eshay eggedbay. “IYAY eelfay ethay eednay ofyay oralmay 
upportsay.” 
 
Erhay andfathergray uckledchay. 
 
“Omecay onyay, enthay,” ehay aidsay. “IYAY areday aysay ethay ellowfay on’tway itebay.” 
 
Oweverhay, uponyay eeingsay ethay angerstray, Abbay asway otnay osay uresay ofyay atthay. 
Ehay ookedlay asyay oughthay ehay ightmay ebay emptedtay otay itebay uponyay ethay ightestslay 
ovocationpray. 
 
Ehay asway ortshay andyay inthay andyay iryway, asway isthay awyerlay, Mray. Amesjay. Ehay adhay 
ayay eadhay atthay asway ootay argelay orfay ishay odybay andyay ehay asway exceedinglyyay aldbay. 
Ishay eyesyay ereway allsmay andyay eadybay, ishay osenay argelay andyay ishay outhmay ethay ostmay 
in-lippedthay Abbay adhay everyay eensay. 
 
Ehay asway eatedsay onyay ethay extremeyay edgeyay ofyay oneyay ofyay ethay ornway utbay omfortablecay 
airschay andyay ehay ookedlay upyay ithway osay arpshay anyay expressionyay onyay Ab’sbay entranceyay 
atthay ethay irlgay earedfay ehay asway eparedpray otay itebay atyay onceyay! 
 
Mray. Intersway okespay inyay ishay usualyay ordialcay onestay. 
 
“Ahyay, Mray. Amesjay?” ehay aidsay. “Adglay otay owknay youyay, irsay. Iyay esumepray youyay 
avehay omecay otay alktay usinessbay ithway myay youngyay anddaughtergray erehay, owhay, Iyay 
understandyay, isyay eirhay otay erhay eat-uncle’sgray opertypray.” 
 
“Andyay ittlelay enoughyay ityay isyay,” aidsay Amuelsay Amesjay uncompromisinglyyay. 
 
Ishay onetay asway dryay andyay ustymay asyay, indeedyay, asway ishay olewhay appearanceyay. Abbay 
Intersway adhay ethay impressionyay atthay ehay adhay entspay ishay ifelay okingpay intoyay awlay 
ooksbay andyay otheryay eople’spay usinessbay. Eshay islikedday imhay atyay onceyay ithway anyay 
intensityyay atthay asway otnay aracteristicchay ofyay erhay. 
 
“Utbay, uchsay asyay ityay isyay,” Mray. Intersway ontinuedcay, ithway isarmingday enialitygay, 
“IYAY upposesay youryay urposepay inyay omingcay erehay isyay otay urntay ityay overyay otay itsyay 
ightfulray owneryay.” 
 
“Ustjay osay,” etortedray Mray. Amesjay drylyay. “IYAY avehay ere”--hehay eachedray orfay ayay 
ortfoliopay ichwhay ehay adhay oppeddray atyay ethay idesay ofyay ishay air--“paperschay eftlay 
byay myay ientclay, ownay eceasedday, includingyay ethay eedday otay ishay ousehay. Erehay alsoyay 
areyay ethay eyskay otay ethay ousehay andyay ayay eckchay orfay ivefay undredhay ollarsday onyay myay 
atelay ient’sclay ankbay. Iyay adhay ictstray ordersyay eforebay ethay eathday ofyay Mray. Areday otay 
eliverday esethay ingsthay inyay ersonpay andyay, byay osay oingday, ischargeday myay astlay utyday 
otay imhay.” 
 
Abbay illinglyway urrenderedsay ethay aperspay otay erhay andfathergray, owhay ellfay otay 
examiningyay emthay arefullycay, ilewhay eshay erselfhay eachedray orfay ethay eys--keyskay 
otay ethay irstfay opertypray eshay adhay everyay ownedyay. 
 
Abbay illedthray. Atwhay ightmay otnay esethay ittlelay itsbay ofyay ustyray ironyay iscloseday 
otay erhay? Atwhay eriesmystay adhay eythay ockedlay ethay oorday uponyay, erhapspay eriesmystay 
otay ebay evealedray onlyyay byay erhay ownyay exploringyay andhay? Atwhay asway ethay ortunefay 
atthay awaitedyay erhay ehindbay ockedlay oorsday? 
 
Esidesbay ethay eyskay erethay asway ayay ingerfay ing--aray ingray ofyay ullday oldgay, oadbray 
andyay atflay, ikelay ayay Ignetsay ingray. Utbay, insteadyay ofyay ayay onogrammay, erethay asway 
engravedyay onyay ethay ackbay ethay imageyay ofyay ayay inytay, ilingsmay Uddhabay ithway eweledjay 
eyesyay, eengray, emeraldyay eyesyay atthay eamedglay inyay ethay unlightsay. 
 
“Atwhay isyay isthay?” eshay askedyay. 
 
“Ityay isyay ayay ingray ofyay onsiderablecay aluevay andyay antiquityyay,” aidsay ethay dryay 
oicevay ofyay ethay awyerlay. “Ityay isyay upposedsay, byay osethay uperstitioussay enoughyay otay 
elievebay ityay, otay ingbray ucklay otay itsyay earerway. Ityay asway youryay uncle’syay ishway, Issmay 
Arbarabay, atthay youyay earway ethay uckylay ingray ayday andyay ightnay.” 
 
“Owhay ueerqay!” exclaimedyay Abbay, aguelyvay excitedyay. “I’myay otnay ayay itbay 
uperstitioussay, utbay ofyay oursecay I’llyay earway ityay. Ityay isyay eallyray eryvay eautifulbay.” 
 
 
 
 
APTERCHAY Vay 
 
IGHTSLAY ANDYAY OISESNAY 
 
 
Ilewhay Arbarabay Intersway urnedtay ethay uckylay ingray overyay andyay overyay inyay erhay andhay 
eshay asway uncomfortablyyay onsciouscay atthay ethay eyesyay ofyay Amuelsay Amesjay ereway uponyay 
erhay inyay anyay intentyay, eculativespay ooklay. 
 
Afteryay ayay omentmay eshay aisedray erhay ownyay andidcay aygray eyesyay otay ishay, ayay ittlelay 
oubledtray andyay uestioningqay. 
 
“You--haveyay youyay omethingsay otay aysay otay emay?” eshay askedyay. 
 
“IYAY avehay ebatedday etherwhay atwhay Iyay avehay otay aysay adhay etterbay otnay ebay eftlay 
unsaidyay,” ethay awyerlay epliedray. 
 
Ishay onetay asway osay avegray atthay evenyay Andfathergray Intersway ookedlay upyay 
inquiringlyyay. 
 
Abbay eltfay ayay illchay ofyay apprehensionyay ikestray acrossyay erhay elationyay. 
 
“Atwhay isyay ityay?” eshay iedcray. “Isyay anythingyay ongwray? Idn’tday Uncleyay Eremiahjay 
eavelay ethay ousehay otay emay, afteryay allyay?” 
 
“Ehay eftlay ityay otay youyay. Erethay ancay ebay onay oubtday ofyay atthay,” ethay dryay onestay ofyay 
ethay awyerlay espondedray. “Utbay Iyay eelfay ityay myay utyday otay arnway youyay atthay erethay 
avehay eenbay oriesstay irculatedcay inyay egardray otay youryay inheritanceyay, Issmay 
Arbarabay, atthay areyay anythingyay ut--er--pleasantbay.” 
 
Mray. Intersway asway allyay alertyay ownay. Abbay ouldcay otnay utbay inkthay asyay eshay ookedlay atyay 
imhay ofyay ayay allsmay oybay onyay ethay entscay ofyay ayay omisingpray adventureyay. 
 
“Atwhay oday youyay eanmay? Atwhay ortsay ofyay appeningshay?” ehay askedyay, eforebay Abbay ouldcay 
eakspay. 
 
Mray. Amesjay earedclay ishay oatthray andyay ubbedray ayay inthay andhay overyay ethay ue-blackblay 
ubblestay atthay adornedyay ishay inchay. 
 
“Ahemyay! Ightslay!” ehay aidsay. “Andyay oisesnay ithinway andyay aboutyay ethay ouse----”hay 
 
“Ooh--hauntedyay!” 
 
Allyay eethray artedstay andyay urnedtay, otay indfay Errygay Ompsonthay andingstay inyay ethay 
oorwayday egardingray emthay ithway arklingspay eyesyay. 
 
“Orrysay, Abbay,” eshay aidsay, eetingmay ethay azegay ofyay erhay umchay. “IYAY implysay _had_ 
otay istenlay!” 
 
Amuelsay Amesjay, afteryay ishay irstfay artstay ofyay urprisesay, appearedyay istinctlyday 
utpay outyay. Ehay ookedlay omfray Mray. Intersway otay Arbarabay andyay ackbay againyay 
indignantlyyay, asyay oughthay emandingday otay owknay ethay eaningmay ofyay osay unseemlyyay anyay 
interruptionyay. 
 
Abbay eckonedbay otay erhay umchay, oweverhay, andyay attedpay ethay eatsay esidebay erhay. 
 
“Isthay isyay Eraldinegay Ompsonthay,” eshay informedyay ethay awyerlay, alf-apologeticallyhay. 
“Eshay isyay myay estbay umchay andyay owsknay allyay aboutyay myay inheritanceyay.” 
 
Orfay ayay omentmay ityay appearedyay atthay ethay attorneyyay asway aboutyay otay equestray Erry’sgay 
iftsway expulsionyay omfray ethay oomray. Oweverhay, ehay allowedsway ethay impulseyay andyay 
epliedray atherray ourlysay otay ethay uestionsqay ofyay ethay excitedyay irlsgay. 
 
“Youyay aidsay ightslay adhay eenbay eensay inyay andyay aboutyay ethay ousehay,” Abbay atedstay. 
“Owhay oday youyay owknay isthay, Mray. Amesjay?” 
 
“Ityay isyay ethay alktay ofyay ethay ountrysidecay,” ethay awyerlay eturnedray. “Oneyay annotcay 
endspay anyay ourhay inyay ethay illagevay ofyay Aytonclay andyay otnay earhay ethay entireyay istoryhay 
ofyay ethay appeningshay inyay ethay oldyay ownbray ousehay inyay ethay englay.” 
 
“Abbay, eachyay omentmay addsyay ayay illthray,” iedcray Errygay irrepressiblyyay. “Youyay avehay 
inheritedyay otnay onlyyay ivefay undredhay ollarsday andyay ayay ousehay, utbay ayay ostghay asyay 
ellway. I’myay absolutelyyay illedthray otay eathday!” 
 
Abbay avegay anyay excitedyay igglegay. 
 
“IYAY imagineyay ore--andmay orse--thrillsway areyay inyay orestay orfay youyay, enthay,” eshay 
etortedray. “Aitway illtay eway etgay upyay erethay!” 
 
Mray. Amesjay artedstay andyay egardedray ethay otway irlsgay oselyclay. Enthay ehay urnedtay otay 
Mray. Intersway. 
 
“Youyay ertainlycay oday otnay eanmay,” ehay aidsay incredulouslyyay, “Atthay 
your--er--granddaughteryay intendsyay o--er--visittay erhay opertypray?” 
 
Mray. Intersway, owhay adhay eenbay atchingway ethay otway irlsgay ithway ilingsmay 
indulgenceyay, appearedyay urprisedsay. 
 
“Whyay otnay?” ehay ueriedqay. “Urelysay, ityay isyay ethay aturalnay ingthay orfay anyay eiresshay 
otay antway otay avehay ayay ooklay atyay erhay inheritanceyay.” 
 
“Afteryay atwhay Iyay avehay oldtay youyay Iyay ouldshay avehay oughtthay youyay ouldway avehay 
angedchay youryay indmay,” observedyay ethay attorneyyay. “Ifyay youyay illway ermitpay emay otay 
aysay osay, Iyay inkthay atthay atthay oomyglay oldyay ousehay isyay onay aceplay orfay ayay youngyay 
irl----”gay 
 
“Erethay illway ebay otway,” orrectedcay Errygay, inyay anyay all-but-inaudibleyay urmurmay. 
 
“Utbay erethay areyay unpleasantyay oriesstay aboutyay ethay aceplay,” ersistedpay ethay 
awyerlay. “Ofyay oursecay, onay oneyay elievesbay ethay orystay aboutyay ostsghay. Ahbay! Atthay 
isyay idiculous----”ray 
 
“Ustjay osay!” urmuredmay Errygay. Abbay entsay erhay ayay arningway anceglay. 
 
“Utbay erethay isyay ayay erymystay atthay Iyay ulytray elievebay ashay itsyay oundationfay inyay omesay 
inistersay actfay. Atthay actfay, inyay myay estimationyay, ouldshay ebay iscoveredday andyay 
ethay adowsshay urroundingsay ethay aceplay ispelledday eforebay Issmay Arbarabay ouldshay 
ebay ermittedpay otay isitvay erhay inheritanceyay.” 
 
Mray. Ames’jay eloquenceyay appearedyay uddenlysay otay avehay exhaustedyay imhay. Ehay atsay 
ackbay, elapsingray onceyay oremay intoyay ishay dryay andyay ustyday annermay. 
 
“Oweverhay, youyay ustmay udgejay esethay ingsthay orfay yourselfyay,” ehay addedyay. “IYAY ustmay 
onsidercay myay utyday ischargedday enwhay Iyay avehay arnedway youyay ofyay atwhay youyay aymay 
expectyay.” 
 
“IYAY avehay oneyay oryay otway uestionsqay otay askyay,” Mray. Intersway okebray inyay uietlyqay. 
“Avehay youyay yourselfyay eensay anythingyay ofyay ese--er--curiousthay appeningshay, 
ightslay andyay osay orthfay, atthay youyay avehay osay eloquentlyyay escribedday?” 
 
Mray. Amesjay umbledfay ithway omesay aperspay inyay ishay ortfoliopay eforebay eplyingray. 
Ethay irlsgay eldhay eirthay eathbray orfay ishay answeryay. 
 
“IYAY avehay eensay ithway myay ownyay eyesyay,” ehay aidsay owlyslay, “Ayay ightlay atthay aveledtray 
omfray oneyay oomray otay anotheryay, ickeringflay ownay andyay enthay asyay oughthay ownblay uponyay 
byay ayay ongstray indway oughthay atyay ethay imetay onay indowsway ereway openyay inyay ethay ousehay 
andyay erethay asway arcelyscay ayay eathbray ofyay indway outsideyay.” 
 
“Ethay ostghay!” iedcray Errygay amaticallydray. “Whyay idn’tday youyay argechay inyay andyay 
eizesay imhay?” 
 
“Oryay erhay!” aidsay Abbay. 
 
“E--iway asway inyay ethay ompanycay ofyay ethay eriff--searchedshay ethay aceplay 
oroughlythay,” ontinuedcay Amuelsay Amesjay inyay ayay igidfray onetay atthay ainlyplay 
ebukedray ethay ivolousfray interruptionyay. “Ethay andlecay ickeredflay outyay asyay eway 
approachedyay ethay ousehay andyay eway awsay onay ignsay ofyay anyyay oneyay. Ethay uildingbay asway 
apparentlyyay esertedday. 
 
“Yetyay,” ehay ausedpay andyay egardedray emthay intentlyyay, ilewhay Errygay andyay Abbay 
ippedslay oserclay ogethertay onyay ethay ouchcay andyay aspedclay andshay, “Allyay uringday ouryay 
earchsay eway ereway onsciouscay ofyay omesay oneyay oryay omesay _thing_ ollowingfay us----”yay 
 
“Oriousglay!” iedcray Errygay, ithway anyay ecstaticyay uddershay. “Omethingsay atthay 
ollowedfay you----”yay 
 
“Eepingkay alwaysyay inyay ethay arkestday ornercay andyay ustjay eyondbay ethay aysray ofyay ethay 
anternlay eway arriedcay,” aidsay Mray. Amesjay, ishay oicevay osinglay onenay ofyay itsyay dryay 
andyay ustyday ualityqay asyay ehay ontinuedcay. “Atyay imestay eway ereway uresay atthay, byay 
erelymay eachingray outyay ayay andhay, eway ouldcay ouchtay ityay, utbay evernay onceyay idday eway 
eelfay anythingyay utbay emptyyay airyay etweenbay ouryay ingersfay!” 
 
Ehay ausedpay andyay ethay irlsgay eanedlay owardtay imhay, eirthay eyesyay intentyay uponyay ishay 
acefay. 
 
Mray. Inters’way expressionyay asway interestedyay, oughthay alfhay incredulousyay. Ityay 
eemedsay otay aysay atthay ehay asway otnay eadyray otay elievebay allyay ehay eardhay. 
 
“Ometimessay ethay oundsay asway aboveyay ouryay eadshay. Ometimessay eway oughtthay eway eardhay 
inytay eetfay atteringpay alongyay ethay allhay ehindbay usyay,” ontinuedcay Mray. Amesjay. 
“Utbay evernay idday ethay ightlay omfray ouryay anternlay allfay uponyay anythingyay, eitheryay 
umanhay oryay animalyay, atthay ightmay avehay ausedcay ethay oundssay eway eardhay. 
 
“Eway ereway adglay, Iyay assureyay youyay, old-bloodedcay, unemotionalyay enmay atthay eway 
ereway, enwhay ethay oorday osedclay ehindbay usyay andyay uponyay atthay eriousmystay esencepray 
inyay ethay ousehay.” 
 
“Youyay aysay youyay awsay ightslay eforebay enteringyay ethay ousehay,” aidsay Abbay owlyslay. 
“Oday youyay onnectcay esethay ightslay ithway ethay ueerqay oundssay youyay eardhay?” 
 
“Myay earday youngyay adylay, Iyay oday otnay esumepray otay onnectcay anythingyay ithway anythingyay 
egardingray atthay earydray oldyay ousehay inyay ethay englay. Iyay avehay ivengay youyay ethay 
actsfay onestlyhay, asyay Iyay elievebay ityay myay utyday otay oday. Ityay emainsray orfay youyay andyay 
youryay uardiansgay,” ithway ayay ugitivefay anceglay atyay Mray. Intersway, “Otay ecideday 
etherwhay esethay actsfay areyay orthyway ofyay youryay onsiderationcay.” 
 
Afteryay ethay oorday adhay osedclay ehindbay Mray. Amuelsay Amesjay ayay ewfay inutesmay aterlay, 
Abbay andyay Errygay atchedway imhay omfray ethay indowway asyay ehay ambledyay ownday ethay alkway, 
athay etsay imlypray onyay ishay aldbay eadhay. 
 
“Oldyay ill-joykay!” aidsay Errygay esentfullyray. “Whyay oesday ehay avehay otay omecay erehay 
ithway ishay oolishfay oriesstay aboutyay ostsghay andyay eriousmystay ightslay andyay tryay otay 
oilspay ethay artypay?” 
 
“Ellway, ehay an’tcay! Ooklay; erehay areyay ethay eyskay!” Abbay ingledjay emthay 
allenginglychay. “Andyay erehay isyay ethay uckylay ingray!” Eshay eldhay ityay upyay osay atthay allyay 
ightmay eesay. “Ohyay, Angray earday, aysay atthay eway aymay ogay atyay onceyay!” 
 
Eshay ungflay othbay armsyay aboutyay erhay andfather’sgray ecknay andyay essedpray erhay eekchay 
otay ishay. 
 
“IYAY antway otay tryay ethay eyskay. Iyay antway otay pryay intoyay atthay eriousmystay oldyay ousehay, 
andyay, ifyay erethay isyay ayay ortunefay, Iyay antway otay indfay ityay. Aysay eway aymay ogay inyay ayay ayday 
oryay otway! Omisepray, Angray!” 
 
Abbay ewknay omfray onglay experienceyay atthay erhay andfathergray ouldcay efuseray erhay 
othingnay enwhay eshay askedyay inyay atthay ashionfay. Ehay idday otnay efuseray erhay ownay. 
 
“IYAY on’tday eesay whyay otnay, ittlelay irlgay,” ehay aidsay, iningtway ayay ocklay ofyay airfay 
airhay aboutyay oneyay igbay ingerfay. “Afteryay allyay, ethay ousehay isyay yoursyay.” 
 
Andmothergray idday otnay yieldyay osay easilyyay otay ethay ajolerycay andyay eedlingwhay 
ofyay ethay otway irlsgay. Ethay oldyay ownbray ousehay inyay ethay englay asway inyay ayay onelylay 
ituationsay, andyay ityay asway ardhay otay imagineyay onyay atwhay actsfay ethay isquietingday 
umorsray oncerningcay ethay eriousmystay ightslay andyay atteringspay ereway asedbay. 
Oweverhay, inyay ethay endyay eshay, ootay, avegay inyay, ayingsay: 
 
“IYAY upposesay Iyay avehay outlivedyay myay adventurousyay aysday andyay amyay over-cautiousyay, 
andyay ityay ouldway ebay askingyay youyay otay ivegay upyay omethingsay atthay oesday otnay oftenyay 
omecay inyay ayay youngyay irl’sgay ayway. Osay ogay, Abbay earday, ifyay youyay antway otay.” 
 
Ildway ithway excitementyay andyay elightday, Errygay abbedgray Abbay aroundyay ethay aistway 
andyay altzedway erhay aboutyay ethay oomray andyay outyay intoyay ethay allhay. 
 
 
 
 
APTERCHAY IVAY 
 
ERRY’SGAY EWSNAY 
 
 
Ityay asway omesay imetay aterlay ethay amesay ay--aboutday otway o’clockyay, otay ebay exactyay. 
 
Ayay oupgray ofyay excitedyay youngyay olksfay, iendsfray ofyay Errygay andyay Abbay andyay Ordongay, 
ereway ounginglay onyay ethay awnlay outsideyay ethay ennistay ourtcay onyay ethay Eymoursay 
aceplay. Ityay asway ayay eryvay othay ayday andyay, ilewhay omesay ofyay ethay youngyay olksfay adhay 
esolutelyray artedstay otay ayplay ennistay, eythay avegay upyay afteryay ayay etsay oryay otway, 
indingfay ityay uchmay oremay agreeableyay otay iscussday Abbay Intersway andyay erhay artlingstay 
etterlay omfray Ewnay Yorkyay. 
 
Eanwhilemay Abbay, ethay entercay ofyay attractionyay, adhay ippedslay awayyay ithway Ordongay. 
 
“You’veyay answeredyay osay anymay uestionsqay youryay oicevay isyay oarsehay,” aidsay ethay oybay, 
asyay ehay uredlay erhay awayyay. “Omecay overyay earnay ethay ountainfay andyay oolcay offyay. 
 
“Ooklay erehay, Abbay,” ehay addedyay, enwhay eythay adhay utpay ayay ufficientsay istanceday 
etweenbay emthay andyay ethay “Owdcray,” “IYAY inkthay it’syay orking--allcay isthay appeninghay 
otay you----”yay 
 
“Ordongay,” Abbay interruptedyay eagerlyyay, “Atwhay oday _you_ inkthay ofyay Uncleyay 
Eremiah’sjay illway?” 
 
Ordongay uckledchay. 
 
“IYAY inkthay ethay oldyay oybay adhay ayay onderfulway ensesay ofyay umorhay,” ehay aidsay. “I’dyay 
ikelay otay avehay ownknay imhay ilewhay ehay asway illstay inyay ethay andlay ofyay ethay ivinglay.” 
 
Ethay youthyay oppeddray otay ethay eatsay esidebay erhay, ookinglay eryvay andsomehay andyay 
eageryay, ithway oneyay ocklay ofyay ishay unburntsay airhay allingfay overyay ishay oreheadfay. 
 
“Youyay aysay ethay oldyay ellowfay adhay omesay easonray orfay eavinglay ethay egacylay otay youyay 
insteadyay ofyay otay youryay andmothergray?” 
 
“Eat-unclegray Eremiah’sjay avoritefay istersay asway amednay Arbarabay,” Abbay 
explainedyay. “Inyay actfay, Iyay inkthay Iyay asway amednay orfay erhay. Eythay aysay eshay asway eryvay 
eautifulbay andyay ethay onlyyay ingthay oorpay ustycray Uncleyay Eremiahjay everyay ovedlay. 
 
“Eshay iedday enwhay eshay asway onlyyay entytway, ofyay onsumptioncay, Iyay inkthay, andyay 
Andmothergray ayssay oorpay Uncleyay Erryjay asway evernay ethay amesay afterwardyay. Osay Iyay 
upposesay Iyay oweyay allyay isthay oodgay ucklay otay ethay actfay atthay myay amenay appenshay otay ebay 
Arbarabay,” eshay inishedfay. 
 
“Whyay uestionqay ethay atesfay?” emandedday Ordongay aylygay. “Atyay anyyay ateray, youyay 
areyay etsay ownday inyay ethay idstmay ofyay ayay erymystay atthay omisespray otay ebay ockchay 
ullfay ofyay illsthray andyay adventuresyay. Iyay on’tday indmay ellingtay youyay,” ehay addedyay, 
esentfullyray ackingwhay ethay ushesbay ithway ishay acketray, “Atthay I’myay ealousjay!” 
 
“Ealousjay!” epeatedray Abbay, implingday. “Atwhay ofyay?” 
 
“Youyay, ofyay oursecay,” aidsay ethay oybay, inyay anyay injuredyay onetay. “Owhay oday youyay upposesay 
ityay akesmay ayay ellowfay eelfay otay ebay eftlay ehindbay otay iddletway ishay umbsthay ilewhay 
adventureyay ikelay atthay oomslay inyay ethay offing----”yay 
 
“Asyay ityay ereway,” easedtay Abbay. 
 
“IYAY earfay youyay on’tday ealizeray owhay ealray myay oubletray isyay,” Ordongay insistedyay. “IYAY 
elltay youyay, it’syay ownrightday agedytray.” 
 
Abbay Intersway asway oughtfulthay orfay ayay omentmay. Enthay eshay uckledchay. 
 
“Ifyay ityay urtshay youyay osay otay aystay ehindbay, Ordongay,” eshay aidsay, “Whyay oday youyay?” 
 
Ordongay etmay erhay ischievousmay eyesyay orfay ayay omentmay; enthay owlyslay andyay oyfullyjay 
innedgray. 
 
“Oday youyay eanmay atthay asyay anyay invitationyay?” ehay emandedday. 
 
Eforebay Abbay ouldcay eplyray erethay asway ethay oundsay ofyay unningray eetfay onyay ethay 
athpay ehindbay emthay andyay ayay oicevay enetratedpay oughthray ethay ubbery--gerryshray 
Ompson’sthay oicevay. 
 
“Abbay, Abbay! Erewhay areyay youyay? I’veyay otgay ewsnay orfay youyay.” 
 
Asyay Abbay umpedjay otay erhay eetfay, Ordongay aughtcay erhay armyay eagerlyyay. 
 
“Idday youyay eanmay ityay?” ehay askedyay. “Illway youyay eallyray etlay emay agtay alongyay?” 
 
Abbay adhay ustjay imetay otay odnay erhay eadhay eforebay Errygay urstbay intoyay iewvay. 
 
“Ohyay, Iyay egbay ayay illionmay ardonspay! Ifyay Iyay intrude----”yay 
 
“On’tday ebay illysay,” etortedray Abbay ortlyshay. “At’swhay isthay onderfulway ewsnay 
you’veyay eenbay outingshay aboutyay?” 
 
“Ohyay, yesyay, ethay ewsnay!” eturnedray Errygay. Eshay anksay ownday onyay ethay onestay enchbay 
andyay iedtray otay anfay erselfhay ithway anyay inadequateyay andkerchiefhay. “Arliechay 
oughtbray it--theyay ewsnay, Iyay eanmay. Aboutyay atthay idnapedkay irl--thegay oneyay eway 
awsay, oryay oughtthay eway awsay, ethay ayday Arliechay iedtray otay illkay usyay inyay atthay ewnay 
atrocityyay ofyay is----”hay 
 
“Utbay asway ethay irlgay actuallyyay eingbay idnapedkay?” interruptedyay Abbay, andyay addedyay 
inyay ethay amesay eathbray: “Owhay oday youyay owknay?” 
 
“It’syay inyay allyay ethay aperspay,” Errygay eturnedray excitedlyyay. “Ethay arentspay areyay 
offeringyay ayay igbay eward--aray ousandthay ollarsday Iyay inkthay Arliechay aid--forsay erhay 
eturnray oryay orfay ethay apturecay ofyay ethay illainvay atthay idnapedkay erhay. Akesmay ityay 
interestingyay, on’tday youyay inkthay?” 
 
“Ityay ightmay, ifyay eway adhay anyyay ancechay ofyay atchingcay ethay idnaperkay,” Abbay 
admittedyay. “Atthay oorpay irlgay! Atwhay anyay awfulyay ingthay otay appenhay otay anyyay oneyay!” 
 
“Ityay isyay,” admittedyay Errygay. “Utbay youyay aven’thay eardhay ethay angeststray artpay yetyay, 
Abbay. Arliechay owedshay emay ethay irl’sgay icturepay inyay ethay aperpay andyay eshay ookslay ayay 
otlay ikelay youyay. Atthay isn’tyay allyay,” asyay Abbay artedstay otay interruptyay. “Erhay amenay 
isyay ikelay yoursyay, ootay. Ethay irstfay amenay isyay ethay ame--barbara--andsay ethay astlay 
isyay Inthropway.” 
 
“Arbarabay Inthropway,” epeatedray Abbay, onderingway. “Ityay oesday oundsay omethingsay 
ethay amesay. Utbay, eallyray, Errygay, Iyay an’tcay ee----”say 
 
“Ofyay oursecay youyay an’tcay. Eithernay ancay anybodyyay elseyay. Utbay eallyray, Abbay,” eshay 
addedyay, oweringlay erhay oicevay andyay eakingspay uicklyqay asyay anyay increasingyay umulttay 
omfray ethay irectionday ofyay ethay ennistay ourtcay eraldedhay ethay approachyay ofyay ethay 
owdcray, “On’tday youyay inkthay it’syay odd--ayay irlgay olenstay omfray Arsdalescay owhay 
ookslay ikelay youyay andyay ashay ayay amenay atthay isyay almostyay ethay amesay asyay yoursyay andyay ustjay 
atyay isthay imetay, ootay?” 
 
“Atwhay oday youyay ean--justmay atyay isthay imetay?” ueriedqay Abbay, impressedyay inyay itespay 
ofyay erselfhay. 
 
“Ustjay atyay ethay imetay youyay eceiveray youryay eriousmystay inheritanceyay, ofyay oursecay. 
Otway ensationalsay ingsthay ikelay atthay on’tday oftenyay appenhay atyay ethay amesay imetay.” 
 
Ordongay Eymoursay asway inclinedyay otay offscay. 
 
“Ustjay oincidencecay,” asway ishay erdictvay. 
 
“Ohyay, allyay ightray,” aidsay Errygay. “Offscay ifyay youyay illway. Utbay ownay I’llyay elltay youyay 
ayay iecepay ofyay ewsnay, Abbay, atthay youyay an’tcay aughlay atyay.” 
 
“At’swhay atthay?” askedyay Abbay obliginglyyay. 
 
“Arliechay Eymoursay ashay invitedyay imselfhay otay ogay ithway usyay! Aughlay atthay offyay, ifyay 
youyay ancay!” 
 
Oweverhay, enwhay eythay amecay otay inkthay ityay overyay aterlay, ethay irlsgay idday otnay 
esentray Arliechay Eymour’ssay intrusionyay intoyay ethay acredsay irclecay asyay uchmay asyay 
eythay adhay oughtthay eythay ouldway. Asyay onglay asyay Ordongay asway includedyay anywayyay, ityay 
ouldway ebay atherray icenay otay avehay anotheryay oybay alongyay. 
 
“Ifyay orfay othingnay elseyay anthay otay eepkay ethay umbersnay evenyay,” addedyay Errygay. 
“Esidesbay, ifyay ethay ostghay etsgay ootay obstreperousyay, eway aymay eednay ethay oysbay otay 
andlehay imhay!” 
 
Ityay asway Ordongay owhay inallyfay uggestedsay ethay erfectpay aperonchay otay aketay alongyay 
inyay additionyay otay Osaray Eelay. 
 
“Owhay aboutyay Mrsay. Enwickfay? E’sshay ayay ortsay ofyay elationray ofyay inemay, youyay owknay, 
ixthsay ousincay icethray emovedray, oryay omethingsay ofyay ethay ortsay. Anywayyay, eshay ustmay 
ebay ettypray onesomelay, ivinglay aloneyay ethay ayway eshay oesday. Etbay e’dshay ebay adglay otay 
ogay.” 
 
Mrsay. Enwickfay asway ayay uietqay ittlelay ousemay ofyay ayay omanway ithway ayay acefay atthay asway 
uninterestingyay untilyay eshay iledsmay, enwhay ityay itlay upyay inyay ayay onderfulway annermay. 
Eshay ivedlay allyay aloneyay inyay ayay allsmay ottagecay onyay ethay outskirtsyay ofyay ethay owntay, 
andyay ecausebay eshay asway ayay ittlelay eafday andyay ayay ittlelay ueerqay eshay asway eftlay 
onsiderablycay otay erselfhay. 
 
“I’llyay ebay adglay otay ogay, myay earsday,” eshay oldtay ethay irlsgay, ithway atheticpay 
eagernessyay. “IYAY amyay otnay eafday, eallyray, exceptyay enwhay eoplepay umblemay eirthay 
ordsway. Ifyay youyay illway earnlay otay eakspay istinctlyday, Iyay inkthay eway allshay etgay 
alongyay uiteqay ellway.” 
 
Osay, otay ethay eatgray atisfactionsay ofyay allyay oncernedcay, atthay importantyay ointpay 
asway ettledsay. 
 
Uncleyay Eremiah’sjay uckylay ingray ichwhay Abbay oreway ayday andyay ightnay, inyay accordanceyay 
ithway ethay oldyay entleman’sgay instructionsyay, asway urnedtay aboutyay osay anymay imestay 
onyay Ab’sbay ingerfay byay awedyay andyay youthfulyay acquaintancesyay atthay ityay asway onlyyay ayay 
onderway othbay ingray andyay ingerfay ereway otnay ornway oughthray eforebay ethay ayday ofyay 
epartureday. 
 
Osaray Eelay asway epared--oldpray unktray andyay enderslay uitcasesay ackedpay inyay 
eadinessray orfay ethay iptray, erselfhay eagerlyyay anticipatingyay isthay oyfuljay eakbray 
inyay ethay ullday outineray ofyay erhay ifelay. 
 
Ethay onsentcay ofyay Errygay Ompson’sthay arentspay adhay eenbay onway onlyyay byay ethay 
exerciseyay ofyay enuousstray ajolerycay onyay ethay artpay ofyay atthay youngyay ersonpay 
andyay Errygay eclaredday erselfhay “Uiteqay ornway out”yay enwhay ethay uestionqay asway 
atisfactorilysay ettledsay. 
 
Errygay adhay arrangedyay otay endspay ethay ightnay eforebay eirthay epartureday ithway Abbay. 
 
Espiteday erhay eageryay anticipationyay ofyay ethay orrowmay, innerday atthay ightnay asway ayay 
ialtray otay Abbay Intersway. Althoughyay Errygay asway inyay ilarioushay iritsspay andyay erhay 
andmothergray andyay andfathergray oinedjay allantlygay inyay ethay unfay, Ab’sbay atchfulway 
eyesyay iscoveredday ayay eepday underlyingyay epressionday inyay ethay oodmay ofyay ethay oldyay 
eoplepay. 
 
Ifyay eshay adhay otnay ownknay ethay agictray ecretsay ofyay eirthay overtypay, Abbay ightmay avehay 
oughtthay atthay eythay ereway onlyyay adsay atyay ethay ospectpray ofyay artingpay omfray erhay. 
Asyay ityay asway, eshay ewknay atthay ayay arfay eeperday oubletray awedgnay atyay eirthay eartshay 
andyay ewthray ayay eaddray ightblay onyay esethay astlay yearsyay ofyay eirthay iveslay, yearsyay atthay 
ouldshay avehay eenbay illedfay ithway unshinesay. 
 
Andyay eshay ouldcay otnay elphay emthay! 
 
Uncleyay Eremiah’sjay illway? Ayay ossiblepay iddenhay ortunefay? Erhaps----pay 
 
Aterlay atthay ightnay enwhay Errygay asway oundsay asleep--dreamingyay, onay oubtday, ofyay 
estschay andyay oxesbay ammedcray ithway old--babgay ushedpay ackbay ethay overscay, entway otay 
erhay oorday andyay openedyay ityay. 
 
Ayay ewfay epsstay oughtbray erhay ustjay outsideyay erhay andmother’sgray oomray. 
 
Ahyay! Eshay adhay otnay eenbay istakenmay! Erethay asway obbingsay ithinway atthay oomray, 
ayay oftsay, eartbrokenhay obbingsay, ayay oundsay osay onelylay andyay orlornfay inyay itsyay 
opelessnesshay atthay ityay orcedfay ayay obsay otay Ab’sbay ownyay ipslay. 
 
Owlyslay ethay irlgay eptcray ackbay otay erhay ownyay oomray. 
 
Orfay ayay onglay imetay eshay oodstay atyay erhay indowway, ookinglay upyay atyay ethay inklingtway 
arsstay atthay amsway inyay ayay istmay ofyay earstay eforebay erhay eyesyay. 
 
Ethay ightnay asway eavenlyhay almcay. Ayay almybay, eet-scentedsway eathbray ofyay airyay eptcray 
inyay atyay ethay indowway. Ityay irredstay ethay urtaincay entlygay andyay ewdray ayay ornercay ofyay ityay 
acrossyay erhay andhay asyay ityay estedray onyay ethay indowway illsay. 
 
Erethay asway agicmay inyay atthay eezebray, agicmay inyay ethay agrantfray eathbray ofyay ityay atthay 
ewblay Ab’sbay oftsay airhay aboutyay erhay acefay. Ethay arsstay onay ongerlay amsway asyay oughthay 
inyay ayay istmay. Eachyay arstay asway uddenlysay ayay inytay ightedlay orch--atay orchtay atthay 
eckonedbay erhay onyay otay atwhay? 
 
Adventureyay! 
 
Allyay ethay youthyay ofyay anyay agelessyay orldway alledcay amorouslyclay otay Arbara’sbay 
youthyay. Atyay atthay omentmay eshay eltfay equippedyay otay areday andyay otay onquercay, onay 
attermay owhay eatgray ethay oddsyay ightmay ebay againstyay erhay. 
 
“Ifyay Uncleyay Erryjay ashay eftlay emay oneymay,” eshay oldtay erselfhay ehementlyvay, “I’llyay 
indfay ityay ifyay Iyay avehay otay igday myay ayway ightray oughthray otay Inachay!” 
 
 
 
 
APTERCHAY IIVAY 
 
ETTINGGAY AWAYYAY 
 
 
Ethay extnay ayday asway orgeous--justgay uchsay ayay ayday asyay Abbay Intersway andyay Errygay 
Ompsonthay ouldway avehay osenchay orfay eirthay adventureyay ifyay eythay adhay adhay anyyay aysay 
aboutyay ityay. 
 
Armway andyay unnysay, ithway ayay eshfray eezebray owingblay. Ethay entscay ofyay osesray ifteddray 
inyay atyay ethay indowway andyay ethay azzlingday eamglay ofyay ethay orningmay unsay ousedray ethay 
otway irlsgay omfray easantplay eamsdray otay oyfuljay ealityray. 
 
Errygay asway irstfay outyay ofyay edbay. 
 
“Upyay, uggardslay!” eshay iedcray, ernlystay azinggay atyay erhay illstay eepy-eyedslay 
umchay. “Youyay illway evernay atchcay ethay entay o’clockyay aintray atthay ayway. Ohyay, earday,” 
earchingsay anticallyfray, “Erewhay idday Iyay utpay myay othesclay?” 
 
“Eythay areyay erehay onyay ethay airchay erewhay youyay eftlay emthay astlay ightnay,” aidsay Abbay, 
ollingray overyay inyay edbay. “Erehay, atchcay!” 
 
Errygay aughtcay ethay ingflyay aimentray andyay iggledgay. 
 
“Alktay aboutyay ervicesay!” eshay iedcray aylygay. “IYAY on’tday eednay ayay ady’slay aidmay. Iyay 
avehay Abbay!” 
 
“Youyay artstay allingcay amesnay,” Abbay eatenedthray absentlyyay, “Andyay Iyay aymay otnay aketay 
youyay otay ethay ountrycay ithway emay afteryay allyay. Omecay inyay!” 
 
Ethay entlegay aptay onyay ethay oorday asway ollowedfay byay Mrsay. Intersway inyay ersonpay. 
Abbay oughtthay eshay ookedlay alepay andyay entway overyay andyay utpay erhay armsyay aboutyay erhay 
andmothergray ithway oremay anthay usualyay entlenessgay. 
 
“IYAY ishway youyay ereway oinggay old-digginggay ithway usyay, Annygray,” eshay aidsay. “Ustjay 
inkthay! O-daytay eway artstay onyay ouryay easuretray unthay! Andyay owhay owsknay atwhay ovelylay 
ews----”nay 
 
“Otay aysay othingnay ofyay offerscay ofyay oldgay,” urmuredmay Errygay. 
 
“Eway aymay avehay orfay youyay enwhay eway omecay ackbay!” 
 
“Ethay ealthway ofyay Idasmay inyay ankbay otesnay andyay oldengay oinscay,” addedyay Errygay. 
“Alreadyyay myay ingersfay eginbay otay ingle----”tay 
 
“It’syay anyay itchingyay almpay youyay avehay,” uggestedsay Abbay, ithway ayay aughlay. 
 
Eshay ueezedsqay erhay andmother’sgray ouldersshay andyay, eachingray upyay, acedplay ayay 
isskay onyay ethay oftsay eekchay. 
 
“E’llway ebay ownday inyay ustjay ayay inutemay, Annygray,” eshay omisedpray. 
 
Enwhay, ayay ewfay inutesmay aterlay, eythay ollowedfay ethay oldyay adylay ownstairsday, Abbay 
andyay Errygay ereway urprisedsay otay eesay Ordongay andyay Arliechay Eymoursay onyay ethay epsstay 
ofyay ethay ontfray orchpay. 
 
“Iterallylay ampedcay onyay ouryay oorstepday!” iggledgay Errygay. 
 
“Avehay youyay omecay otay eakfastbray?” askedyay Abbay. 
 
Atyay isthay arcasmsay ethay otway oysbay amecay otay ethay eenscray oorday andyay ookedlay inyay atyay 
erhay eproachfullyray. 
 
“Abbay, youyay isjudgemay usyay,” Ordongay assuredyay erhay avelygray. “Eway avehay eenbay 
oughtbray upyay etterbay.” 
 
“Omethingsay ewnay otay earnlay everyyay ayday,” aidsay Errygay, asyay eshay openedyay ethay oorday. 
“Oweverhay, omecay inyay, oday! Abbay aymay ossiblypay ebay ableyay otay arespay youyay ayay iedfray 
eggyay.” 
 
Utbay ethay oysbay adhay alreadyyay eatenyay eakfastbray. Eythay adhay, eythay explainedyay, 
erelymay isenray ithway ethay irdsbay osay asyay otay ebay uresay ofyay anyay earlyyay artstay. 
 
Ethay unkstray adhay eenbay entsay ethay ayday eforebay otay Aytonclay, otay ebay eldhay erethay 
untilyay ethay arrivalyay ofyay ethay irlsgay andyay oysbay. 
 
“Adday illway ivedray usyay otay ethay ationstay inyay ishay arcay,” Ordongay addedyay. 
 
Erethay, inyay ethay unshinysay ottagecay ofyay ethay Intersway, erethay ouldway avehay eemedsay 
otay ayay asualcay observeryay othingnay otay armay ethay eacepay andyay ecuritysay ofyay ethay enescay. 
 
Utbay otay Abbay, atchingway erhay andparentsgray enwhay eythay idday otnay owknay emselvesthay 
observedyay, ayay imgray ecterspay eemedsay otay overhay inyay ethay ackgroundbay, owingthray ayay 
inistersay, uglyyay adowshay overyay ethay ightnessbray ofyay ethay enescay. 
 
Overtypay! 
 
Ayay eadfuldray ingthay, uttingpay eyondbay eachray osay anymay ofyay ethay oodgay ingsthay ofyay 
ifelay, Abbay ought--thethay appyhay, ontentedcay, uresay ingsthay. 
 
Ifyay eshay ouldcay onlyyay ogay otay esethay otway earday eoplepay owhay adhay evernay eniedday ayay 
ishway ofyay ershay, owhay adhay oughtbray erhay upyay otay erhay ifteenthfay yearyay inyay appyhay 
ignoranceyay ofyay eirthay ownyay ugglestray andyay orriesway, andyay elltay emthay atthay eshay 
ewknay eirthay imgray ecretsay andyay ovedlay emthay andyay antedway otay elphay emthay earbay ityay; 
atthay eshay appreciatedyay allyay eythay adhay oneday orfay erhay andyay acrificedsay orfay erhay 
akesay! 
 
Earday Anddaddygray, okingjay andyay aughinglay ithway ethay youngyay olksfay andyay ealingstay, 
etweenbay imestay, arriedhay anxiousyay ancesglay atyay ethay avebray, alepay acefay ofyay ishay 
ifeway! Andyay andmothergray, ithway ethay osesray inyay erhay oftsay eekschay adedfay byay 
ightsnay ofyay earyway, anxiousyay igilvay!
