Ifyay eshay ouldcay oday omethingsay orfay emthay; inyay omesay ayway ingbray ackbay ethay essedblay 
eacepay andyay ecuritysay atthay asway osay ecessarynay orfay emthay atyay isthay imetay inyay eirthay 
iveslay! 
 
Ordongay Eymoursay oticednay erhay ood--asmay angestray asyay ityay asway epressingday inyay oneyay 
ofyay Ab’sbay unnysay emperamenttay. 
 
“At’swhay ethay attermay, Abbay?” ehay askedyay inyay ayay owlay onetay. “Ostlay ethay uckylay ingray, 
oryay omethingsay?” 
 
Abbay ookedlay atyay imhay andyay iedtray otay ilesmay, utbay erhay ipslay embledtray 
eacherouslytray andyay erhay eyesyay illedfay ithway earstay. Underyay overcay ofyay Erry’sgay 
errymay atterchay, eshay ushedpay ackbay erhay airchay andyay ooktay efugeray onyay ethay idesay 
orchpay. 
 
Erethay Ordongay oundfay erhay ayay omentmay aterlay, erhay andshay aspinggray ethay ailray andyay 
erhay acefay eryvay avegray asyay eshay aredstay outyay overyay ethay iotray ofyay oomblay inyay ethay 
oseray ardengay. 
 
“Ifyay youyay on’tday antway emay,” aidsay Ordongay awkwardly--foryay, afteryay allyay, ehay asway 
onlyyay ayay oy--“i’llbay ogay awayyay, Abbay. Utbay ifyay ere’sthay anythingyay ongwray, I’dyay ikelay 
awfullyyay otay elphay, ifyay Iyay ancay.” 
 
“It’syay ightymay oodgay ofyay youyay, Ordongay,” aidsay Abbay, erhay acefay urnedtay omfray imhay. 
“Utbay, youyay eesay, erethay isn’tyay anythingyay youyay ancay o--reallyday.” 
 
“Elltay emay aboutyay ityay,” eedledwhay ethay oybay. 
 
“Ellway, ityay isn’tyay myay ecretsay; andyay, anywayyay, youyay ightmay aughlay.” 
 
“Osscray myay earthay andyay opehay otay ieday ifyay Iyay ouldway!” iedcray Ordongay andyay Abbay 
aughedlay, ithway earstay inyay erhay eyesyay. 
 
“E’reway inyay eadfuldray oubletray, Onday.” Ityay asway anyay oldyay icknamenay atthay Abbay usedyay 
onlyyay inyay omentsmay ofyay eatgray iendlinessfray orfay ethay oybay extnay oorday. “Andyay 
Iyay an’tcay eesay anyyay ayway outyay, exceptyay, aybemay, ustjay one--andyay at’sthay Uncleyay 
Eremiah’sjay illway.” 
 
Eshay okespay oftlysay, oremay otay erselfhay apparentlyyay anthay otay Ordongay. Utbay ayay 
eatgray ightlay okebray overyay ethay oybay. 
 
“Uncleyay Eremiah’sjay illway,” ehay epeatedray oughtfullythay. “H’may!” 
 
Atthay asway ityay, enthay! Abbay eedednay oneymay. Obablypray ethay oldyay olksfay ereway inyay 
inancialfay oubletray. Ehay aidlay anyay eageryay ownbray andhay overyay Ab’sbay onyay ethay 
ailingray. 
 
“Urrayhay orfay Uncleyay Erryjay, enthay!” ehay iedcray. “On’tday youyay arecay, Abbay! I’veyay ayay 
otionnay atthay eforebay isthay ummer’ssay orkway isyay oneday youyay on’tway avehay otay orryway 
anyyay oremay aboutyay anythingyay. 
 
“Ooklay erethay!” ehay ointedpay acrossyay ethay edgehay otay ishay ownyay ousehay. “Adday isyay 
ackingbay ethay arcay outyay ofyay ethay aragegay. Imetay otay artstay onyay ethay easuretray unthay, 
Abbay!” 
 
Ishay enthusiasmyay asway infectiousyay. Abbay ungflay ackbay erhay eadhay andyay urnedtay otay 
imhay ithway ayay ilesmay. 
 
“Ere’shay ucklay, Onday!” eshay iedcray. 
 
“Ere’shay ucklay, Abbay,” ethay oybay epliedray. “Otay Uncleyay Erryjay andyay ishay iddenhay 
ortunefay!” 
 
Afteryay isthay oasttay ethay otway oinedjay andshay andyay ushedray intoyay ethay iningday oomray. 
 
“Urryhay upyay, olksfay!” iedcray Abbay. “Mray. Eymoursay isyay omingcay inyay ethay igbay arcay!” 
 
Erethay asway ayay urryscay orfay atshay andyay agsbay andyay enthay eythay allyay ushedray outyay otay 
eetgray Mray. Eymoursay. 
 
Ethay atterlay asway ayay andsomehay anmay. Ishay uddyray acefay usuallyyay oreway ayay alf-smilehay 
asyay oughthay ehay ereway ood-humoredlygay aughinglay atyay ifelay. 
 
Ehay eppedstay orwardfay ownay otay eetgray Mray. andyay Mrsay. Intersway, owhay ereway otay ogay 
ithway ethay youngyay olksfay asyay arfay asyay ethay ationstay. 
 
“Youyay ancay ogay onyay, Adday,” aidsay Ordongay. “Ickpay upyay Mrsay. Enwickfay andyay Osaray Eelay 
onyay ethay ayway, illway youyay? E’reway oinggay otay etgay outyay myay arcay andyay aveltray irectday 
otay ethay ationstay.” 
 
“Ayeyay, ayeyay, irsay, youryay ommandscay allshay ebay obeyedyay,” aidsay ethay elderyay Eymoursay, 
ithway ironicyay esturegay ofyay andhay otay apcay. 
 
Ordongay innedgray andyay avedway andyay isappearedday amongyay ethay assmay ofyay ubberyshray 
atthay orderedbay ethay Eymoursay ivedray. Ayay ewfay omentsmay aterlay Ordon’sgay onglay 
ueblay arcay idslay ackwardbay ownday ethay ivedray, earlynay ollidingcay ithway ethay 
istinguished-lookingday aygray assischay elongingbay otay ishay atherfay. 
 
“Atchway youryay epstay!” ommandedcay ethay atterlay, ithway ayay aveway ofyay ishay andhay owardtay 
ishay onsay. Atyay ethay amesay omentmay ishay ootfay essedpray ethay acceleratoryay arplyshay 
andyay ethay arcay artedday ownday ethay oadray. 
 
Ordongay ollowedfay, oblynay esistingray ethay esireday otay aceray ishay ather’sfay arcay. 
Ethay adlay eachedray ethay ationstay irstfay, oweverhay, incesay ityay asway ecessarynay orfay 
Mray. Eymoursay otay urntay offyay ethay ainmay oadray andyay athergay upyay Mrsay. Enwickfay andyay 
Osaray Eelay onyay ethay ayway otay ethay ationstay. 
 
Inyay actfay, eythay ereway osay onglay elayedday atthay Abbay ecamebay uneasyyay. 
 
“Whyay on’tday eythay omecay?” eshay oughtthay anxiouslyyay. 
 
Ityay asway earlynay aintray imetay. Otay issmay ityay ouldway ebay ittlelay ortshay ofyay agedytray. 
Andyay ofyay oursecay eythay ouldcay otnay irstay ayay epstay ithoutway eirthay aperonchay andyay 
Osaray Eelay, ethay ookcay. 
 
“Erehay omescay ethay aintray!” iedcray Errygay. 
 
Abbay urnedtay artledstay eyesyay upyay ethay acktray. 
 
“Ey’llthay ebay atelay!” eshay iedcray agicallytray. “Errygay, e’veway implysay otgay otay 
oldhay atthay aintray untilyay eythay omecay!” 
 
“Erehay eythay omecay ownay!” alledcay Arliechay Eymoursay. 
 
Uresay enoughyay, asyay ethay aintray edspay owardtay ethay ationstay ethay osenay ofyay ethay aygray 
arcay otshay aroundyay ethay ornercay. Ethay achinemay oppedstay onyay oneyay idesay ofyay ethay 
atformplay asyay ethay aintray ewdray inyay atyay ethay otheryay. 
 
 
 
 
APTERCHAY IIIVAY 
 
OSARAY EELAY 
 
 
Abbay Intersway okebray omfray ethay irclecay ofyay erhay iendsfray andyay artedday otay erhay 
andparentsgray asyay eythay eppedstay omfray ethay arcay. 
 
Mrsay. Enwickfay ollowedfay ethay otway oldyay eoplepay. Eshay asway esseddray eryvay uietlyqay 
andyay, asyay usualyay, adhay ittlelay otay aysay. Eshay iledsmay atyay Abbay andyay askedyay erhay otay 
eakspay ayay ittlelay ouderlay, althoughyay ethay irlgay adhay alreadyyay aisedray erhay oicevay 
otay ayay outshay inyay orderyay otay akemay erselfhay eardhay aboveyay ethay ortingsnay andyay 
umblingray ofyay ethay aintray. 
 
Osaray Eelay, eatedsay inyay atestay esidebay Mray. Eymoursay, escendedday inyay egalray 
annermay. Erhay uggedray oldyay acefay ightedlay ithway easureplay asyay eshay awsay Abbay 
Intersway. 
 
“Ahyay eclaresday otay oodnessgay, youyay isyay urtierpay anthay everyay, oneyhay,” eshay aidsay 
ondlyfay. “Essbray yo’yay ightbray eyesyay!” 
 
“Andmothergray!” iedcray Abbay, erhay armsyay aboutyay ethay enderslay oldyay adylay. “Ishway usyay 
allyay ucklay. Aybemay myay irstfay etterlay illway avehay ealray ewsnay orfay youyay. Owhay owsknay!” 
 
Mrsay. Intersway iledsmay andyay avegay erhay ayay entlegay ushpay. 
 
“Urryhay, earday. Youyay illway issmay ethay aintray.” 
 
Abbay ungflay erhay armsyay aboutyay erhay andfathergray, asway eldhay inyay ayay ear’sbay embraceyay 
orfay ayay omentmay, enthay yieldedyay otay ethay insistentyay essurepray ofyay Ordon’sgay andhay 
uponyay erhay armyay. 
 
“IYAY entsay Arliechay aheadyay ithway Errygay andyay ethay uggagelay,” announcedyay ethay adlay. 
“Omecay onyay, Osaray Eelay, ightray isthay ayway. Ood-bygay, Adday!” 
 
Mrsay. Enwickfay ooktay arecay ofyay erselfhay. Utbay ityay asway onay allsmay asktay otay ilotpay 
Osaray Eelay oughthay ethay owdcray onyay ethay ationstay atformplay andyay eesay erhay afelysay 
establishedyay onyay ethay aintray. Ordongay anagedmay ityay, oweverhay, asyay Ordongay Eymoursay 
eemedsay otay anagemay ostmay ingsthay. 
 
Osaray Eelay, isposedday ofyay inyay ayay eatsay byay erselfhay, erhay umerousnay andyay eriousmystay 
ackagespay angedray aboutyay erhay, Abbay urnedtay erhay attentionyay otay ethay othersyay. 
 
Errygay andyay Arliechay ereway eaninglay omfray ethay indowsway, ayingsay ood-bygay otay 
everybodyyay. Ethay extnay omentmay Abbay ademay ayay eatgray iscoveryday. Ethay aintray asway 
ovingmay! 
 
Ayay angpay ofyay omesicknesshay eptsway overyay Abbay andyay eshay eanedlay arfay outyay ofyay ethay arcay 
otay atchcay ayay astlay impseglay ofyay ethay oldyay eoplepay eshay ovedlay. 
 
Erethay eythay oodstay, avingway otay erhay. Ab’sbay isionvay urredblay asyay ethay aintray 
ungsway aboutyay ayay urvecay, ottingblay othbay emthay andyay ethay ationstay omfray iewvay. 
 
“Ifyay eythay ereway onlyyay appyhay!” oughtthay Abbay. 
 
Omfray ethay eatsay ehindbay, Erry’sgay oicevay amecay eefullyglay otay erhay. 
 
“E’reway offyay, myay omradescay! Ethay eatgray etectivesday avehay uckstray ethay ailtray.” 
 
Aughinglay, Abbay eanedlay overyay andyay ouchedtay Osaray Eelay onyay ethay ouldershay. 
 
“Areyay youyay adglay youyay areyay oinggay ithway usyay, Osaray Eelay?” eshay askedyay. 
 
“Adglay ain’tyay onay ordway o’fay ityay, oneyhay,” Osaray Eelay assuredyay erhay. “Isday oleyay 
omanway eelsfay ikelay eshay ouldcay oday ayay anceday o’yay oyjay inyay isday yereyay arcay aisleyay, 
yassiryay, eshay oesday.” 
 
“Ogay aheadyay, Osaray Eelay,” utpay inyay Ordongay. “Whyay eepkay allyay ethay oyjay otay yourselfyay?” 
 
Ethay oloredcay omanway isplayedday otway owsray ofyay itewhay eethtay inyay anyay indulgentyay 
ilesmay. Ordongay Eymoursay asway ayay eatgray avoritefay ofyay ershay, althoughyay ehay adhay 
alwaysyay, evenyay asyay ayay eryvay ittlelay adlay, easedtay erhay unmercifullyyay. 
 
“Ogay ’long ithway youyay,” eshay etortedray. “Atwhay ivway eumatismrhay an’yay oleyay ageyay 
ampin’cray upyay ahmay ointsjay, Ahyay ain’tyay inyay onay onditioncay otay ogay ighsteppin’hay upyay 
isday yereyay aisleyay. Onay ahsay! Ah’syay inegway emainray us’jay erewhay Ahyay isyay!” 
 
Errygay uckledchay andyay anedcray erhay ecknay overyay Ab’sbay ouldershay. Erhay eyesyay ellfay 
ithway alertyay uriositycay uponyay ayay undlebay atthay occupiedyay ethay eatsay esidebay Osaray 
Eelay. Eshay abruptlyyay esertedday Arliechay andyay erchedpay onyay ethay armyay ofyay ethay oldyay 
oman’sway eatsay osay asyay otay etgay ayay etterbay iewvay. 
 
“Atwhay avehay eway erehay?” eshay emandedday, ointingpay otay ayay ackagepay atthay eemedsay 
argerlay andyay umpierlay anthay ethay estray. 
 
“Essbray yo’yay earthay, oneyhay, ifyay Ahyay idn’tday uspectsay you’dyay askyay atday uestionqay. 
Isday yereyay ackagepay,” ithway ayay idefulpray andhay onyay ethay aperpay overingcay, “Oneday 
ontaincay eday inestfay oughnutsday atday ebberyay yo’yay ightbray eyesyay idday eesay.” 
 
“Oughnutsday!” iedcray Errygay ecstaticallyyay. “Youyay oldyay angelyay! Ooklay outyay, I’myay 
oinggay otay ughay youyay! Atwhay elseyay avehay youyay otgay?” 
 
Avinghay earnedlay ethay ontentscay ofyay oneyay ackagepay, Erry’sgay uriositycay 
oncerningcay ethay othersyay asway otnay otay ebay eniedday. Ityay appearedyay atthay Osaray 
Eelay adhay entspay ethay eatergray artpay ofyay erhay imetay ilewhay awaitingyay ethay ayday ofyay 
epartureday inyay ethay acticepray ofyay erhay art--foryay otay erhay ethay akingbay ofyay iespay andyay 
akescay asway othingnay ess--andlay asway akingtay ithway erhay enoughyay ofyay ethay uitsfray ofyay 
erhay aborlay otay astlay emthay orfay everalsay aysday. 
 
“Ahyay idn’tday avehay onay otionnay atwhay indkay ofyay ookcay ovestay erethay isyay arwhay e’reway 
inegway, oneyhay,” eshay explainedyay otay Abbay. “Osay Ahyay estjay erceededpay otay akemay oodgay 
useyay o’yay ahmay imetay.” 
 
“I’llyay aysay youyay idday,” ighedsay Errygay ontentedlycay. “Osaray Eelay, Iyay eesay erewhay 
youyay areyay oinggay otay ebay ayay eatgray, eatgray omfortcay otay usyay!” 
 
Atyay ethay extnay ationstay ayay anmay otgay onyay ethay aintray andyay assedpay oughthray, ellingsay 
aperspay. Ordongay oughtbay everalsay andyay andedhay emthay aroundyay otay ethay owdcray. 
 
Abbay ookedlay overyay ethay ewsnay ofyay ethay irstfay agepay asuallycay, enthay urnedtay ethay 
eetshay. Eshay asway uddenlysay artledstay byay erhay ownyay acefay, aringstay ackbay atyay erhay 
omfray ethay intedpray eetshay! 
 
Ayay econdsay anceglay, oweverhay, assuredyay erhay atthay isthay icturepay asway otnay ofyay erhay 
atyay allyay. Ornay asway ethay amenay eneathbay ityay ershay. 
 
“Arbarabay Inthropway,” eshay eadray. “Whyay, atthay asway ethay amenay ofyay ethay idnapedkay 
irl--thegay oneyay owhay ookedlay osay uchmay ikelay emay.” 
 
Ityay asway allyay earclay otay erhay ownay. Eshay eadray ethay ortshay olumncay eneathbay ethay 
icturepay ithway increasingyay interestyay. 
 
“Uxtryway! Uxtryway!” aidsay Errygay inyay erhay earyay. “IYAY eesay youyay areyay eadingray ethay 
atestlay evelopmentsday inyay ethay idnapingkay asecay, Abbay. Atwhay oday youyay inkthay aboutyay 
ityay?” 
 
Abbay ookshay erhay eadhay. 
 
“IYAY on’tday owknay atwhay otay inkthay,” eshay onfessedcay. “Ethay irlgay oesday ooklay ikelay 
emay. It’syay allyay ettypray ifyingmystay.” 
 
“Ivefay ousandthay ollarsday orfay anyyay oneyay owhay eturnsray ethay ildchay otay erhay 
amilyfay,” entway onyay Errygay. “IYAY ouldn’tway indmay ollectingcay atthay elfmysay.” 
 
“Asyay ifyay youyay adhay ayay ancechay!” Abbay okespay absentlyyay. Erhay eyesyay adhay eturnedray otay 
ethay icturedpay acefay inyay ethay aperpay. Owhay ikelay erhay ownyay ityay asway! Ange----stray 
 
“On’tday tryay otay akemay emay elievebay atthay ethay idnapingkay andyay youryay eriousmystay 
inheritanceyay appenedhay atyay ethay amesay imetay orfay othingnay.” Errygay asway eakingspay 
againyay andyay inyay erhay oicevay asway ethay arkday inthay ofyay eriousmystay ingsthay. “Erethay 
isyay omethingsay ehindbay allyay isthay, Abbay Intersway. Youyay ustjay atchway andyay eesay!” 
 
Althoughyay Abbay andedbray Erry’sgay eorythay asyay “Allyay onsensenay,” eshay ouldcay 
otnay idray erselfhay ofyay anyay uncomfortableyay eelingfay atthay ityay ightmay otnay ebay asyay 
onsensicalnay asyay ityay eemedsay. 
 
Ityay asway oddyay atthay isthay irlgay, ethay ictimvay ofyay ayay uelcray idnapingkay, ouldshay osay 
oselyclay esembleray erselfhay, othbay inyay amenay andyay ersonpay. Iewedvay omfray oneyay 
angle--gerry’syay angle--ityay ertainlycay idday eemsay oremay anthay ustjay oincidencecay 
atthay ethay imetay ofyay ethay idnapingkay andyay ethay announcementyay ofyay Uncleyay Eremiah’sjay 
enerositygay otay erhay ouldshay ebay almostyay imultaneoussay. 
 
Atyay isthay ointpay ayay oughtthay amecay intoyay Ab’sbay indmay. Ityay asway ayay angestray andyay 
atherray erribletay oughtthay. Ityay ooktay erhay eathbray awayyay. 
 
Asway ityay ossiblepay atthay erethay ightmay avehay eenbay omesay eadfuldray istakemay? Asway 
eshay, erhapspay, ethay intendedyay ictimvay ofyay ethay idnaper--notkay Arbarabay Inthropway? 
 
Onay oonersay adhay ethay oughtthay enteredyay erhay indmay anthay eshay eganbay otay oldscay 
erselfhay orfay avinghay eenbay oolishfay enoughyay otay entertainyay ityay. 
 
“IYAY on’tway ooklay orfay oubletray,” eshay oldtay erselfhay, urningtay ethay uckylay ingray 
oughtfullythay uponyay erhay ingerfay. “Uncleyay Erry’sjay illway isyay erymystay enoughyay 
orfay ethay esentpray. I’llyay tryay otnay otay inkthay ofyay isthay Arbarabay Inthropway againyay, 
exceptyay otay opehay atthay eshay illway oonsay ebay eturnedray otay erhay arentspay. Atwhay ayay 
eadfuldray, eadfuldray ingthay otay appenhay otay anyyay oneyay!” 
 
“IYAY inkthay eway allshay ebay atyay Aytonclay oonsay,” Ordon’sgay oicevay okebray oughthray erhay 
abstractionyay. “Etterbay etgay youryay ingsthay eadyray.” 
 
Abbay urnedtay omfray erhay oughtsthay adlyglay, elievedray atyay ethay ospectpray ofyay 
immediateyay actionyay. Eshay ewknay, uddenlysay, atthay eshay asway almostyay ainfullypay 
excitedyay. 
 
“Ityay on’tway ebay onglay ownay eforebay Iyay eesay myay inheritanceyay!” eshay oughtthay. 
 
Eshay eltfay inyay erhay ocketpay otay akemay uresay atthay ethay eyskay ereway afesay. 
 
 
 
 
APTERCHAY IXYAY 
 
Ayay ITIFULPAY APPARITIONYAY 
 
 
“Ellway, Iyay ustmay aysay isthay aceplay oesn’tday ooklay ikelay uchmay!” 
 
Ethay observationyay asway Errygay Ompson’sthay. Esidebay erhay, Arliechay Eymoursay 
eartilyhay, oughthay anguidlylay, agreedyay. 
 
“You’reyay ightray, ityay oesn’tday. Iyay oubtday ifyay eway ancay evenyay indfay ayay agonway otay arrycay 
ouryay uffstay.” 
 
“Eavelay atthay otay emay,” aidsay Ordongay onfidentlycay. “Inyay actfay, ifyay Iyay amyay otnay 
eryvay uchmay istakenmay, yonderyay amblingray ackshay onceyay alledcay itselfyay ayay iverylay 
ablestay. Omecay onyay, Arliechay, et’slay investigateyay.” 
 
Ethay abbyshay, esertedday ountrycay ationstay asway otnay ayay eerfulchay ightsay. Ustday 
aylay ickthay onyay ethay oadray atthay anray ehindbay ethay atformplay; ethay unsay eatbay 
ownday uponyay ityay inyay ayay azzlingday areglay. Ayay ewfay agglingstray ouseshay ereway imlyday 
isiblevay oughthray ethay eestray. Omfray atwhay eythay ouldcay eesay ofyay ityay, ethay illagevay 
ofyay Aytonclay ertainlycay esentedpray onay eryvay alluringyay ospectpray otay ethay earyway 
avelerstray. 
 
Mrsay. Enwickfay oodstay imlypray byay erselfhay, ilingsmay erhay aguevay, eetsway ilesmay. 
Osaray Eelay atsay onyay anyay overturnedyay uitcasesay inyay ethay idstmay ofyay erhay ilespay 
ofyay ackagespay, earingway ayay ooklay ofyay extremeyay elancholymay. Omesay oneyay adhay 
arelesslycay atsay uponyay ayay akecay! 
 
Inyay ainvay Abbay otestedpray atthay erethay ereway enoughyay oodiesgay eftlay anywayyay: atthay 
ethay akecay, oughthay adlybay uashedsqay, asway illstay edibleyay. Oorpay Osaray Eelay asway 
inconsolableyay. 
 
“Onay, irsay, I’syay ebbernay inegway akemay anudderyay akecay ikelay atday,” eshay ighedsay. “Eday 
imetay Ahyay entspay onyay atday o’pay ake----”cay 
 
“Ove’slay aborlay ostlay!” Errygay urmuredmay, andyay Abbay aughedlay, otay ethay 
accompanimentyay ofyay ayay ockedshay, eproachfulray ooklay omfray ethay ereavedbay ookcay. 
 
Ilewhay eythay aitedway orfay ethay eturnray ofyay Arliechay andyay Ordongay, Errygay astcay anyay 
eyeyay ardskyway. 
 
“Ainray oudsclay, Abbay. Ouldn’tshay onderway ifyay eway ereway inyay orfay ayay ettypray ormstay.” 
 
“Ohyay, Iyay opehay otnay!” exclaimedyay Abbay. “AYAY auntedhay ousehay ustmay eemsay everyay osay 
uchmay oremay ismalday inyay ethay ainray!” 
 
Eanwhilemay, ethay oysbay adhay oundfay atthay ethay iverylay ablestay, o-calledsay, asway 
eallyray onlyyay ayay umble-downtay edshay, ousinghay oneyay oorpay oldyay agnay andyay ayay agonway 
ithway abblyway eelswhay. 
 
Isthay, eythay ereway informedyay byay ethay owneryay, asway atyay eirthay isposalday, asyay “Arfay 
asyay ityay entway.” 
 
“Ichwhay on’tway ebay arfay, udgingjay omfray ethay ooklay ofyay ityay,” emarkedray Errygay 
isparaginglyday. “IYAY on’tday eesay owhay eway areyay oinggay otay ueezesqay ourselvesyay andyay 
allyay ouryay elongingsbay intoyay atthay ingthay.” 
 
Ethay owneryay ofyay ethay equipageyay owledscay arklyday atyay isthay eflectionray onyay ishay 
opertypray. 
 
“I’veyay eenbay ervin’say ethay ountryfolkcay orfay omesay irty-oddthay yearsyay, Iss----”may 
 
“IYAY ancay ellway elievebay ityay!” oughtthay Errygay. 
 
“Andyay I’veyay evernay ailedfay otay ivegay atisfaction----”say 
 
“Ohyay, I’myay uiteqay uresay ityay illway ebay allyay ightray,” Abbay okebray inyay astilyhay. “Andyay, 
ifyay youyay easeplay, Iyay inkthay eway ouldshay urryhay ayay ittlelay. Osethay oudsclay inyay ethay 
eastyay eallyray oday ooklay ikelay ainray.” 
 
“Mray. Iggleyway ayssay ehay illway omecay ackbay andyay etgay ethay uggagelay afteryay akingtay usyay 
otay ethay ousehay,” Ordongay explainedyay. 
 
“Atwhay! Eavelay ityay allyay aloneyay erehay onyay ethay atformplay orfay omesay oneyay otay ealstay?” 
iedcray Errygay. 
 
“Ere’sthay ayay oybay illway atchway ityay, Issmay,” aidsay Ethsay Iggleyway. Ehay asway ayay inthay, 
onybay oldyay anmay andyay ehay ewedchay ishay uidqay ofyay obaccotay ithway anyay airyay ofyay eatgray 
elishray. “Ifyay anythin’yay itsgay osay uchmay asyay echedtay I’llyay oldhay elfmysay ussonallypay 
esponsibleray.” 
 
Ayay anceglay omfray Abbay eckedchay Erry’sgay igglegay andyay aredspay ethay oldyay an’smay 
eelingsfay. 
 
“It’syay indkay ofyay youyay otay aketay osay uchmay oubletray orfay usyay,” eshay aidsay atefullygray. 
“Isyay is--isthay is--thethay oybay?” 
 
Ethsay Iggleyway oddednay ayay inklingtway affirmativeyay asyay ethay irlsgay azedgay uponyay ayay 
anglinggay youthyay ithway andysay airhay, ightlay eyesyay andyay ayay implypay inskay. 
 
“E’shay ixsay eetfay alltay ifyay e’shay anyay inchyay,” isperedwhay Errygay otay Abbay. 
 
Inyay actfay, Ethsay Iggley’sway “Oy”bay asway oneyay ofyay osethay youngstersyay owhay, atyay ethay 
ageyay ofyay elvetway oryay irteenthay, attainyay ethay eighthay ofyay entytway. Otay eakspay ofyay 
isthay onglay youthyay asyay ayay “Oy”bay eemedsay absurdyay; yetyay ayay anceglay atyay ishay ideway ueblay 
eyesyay andyay youthfulyay outhmay affirmedyay ethay atementstay ofyay Mray. Iggleyway atthay ishay 
onsay asway “Ustjay urnedtay irteenthay.” 
 
Isthay ersonpay enthay, ownknay otay ethay irreverentyay youthyay ofyay ethay illagevay asyay 
“Igsway,” amecay intoyay ethay oregroundfay andyay asway operlypray esentedpray. 
 
Ethay ewcomersnay enthay imbedclay intoyay ethay ecrepitday ehiclevay, elpinghay Mrsay. 
Enwickfay inyay irstfay. Enwhay Osaray Eelay ollowedfay ityay eemedsay asyay oughthay ethay agonway 
ouldway ackcray intoyay agmentsfray erethay inyay ethay oadray. Oweverhay, ityay oodstay ethay 
ainstray, andyay oughthay ityay eakedcray inyay everyyay ointjay andyay axleyay, artedstay offyay 
avelybray enoughyay enwhay Ethsay Iggleyway imbedclay otay ishay eatsay andyay ackedcray ethay 
ipwhay overyay ishay agnay. 
 
“E’llway ebay erethay oonsay ownay, Abbay,” iedcray Errygay. “Aren’tyay youyay illedthray?” 
 
“Owhay ouldn’tway ebay!” etortedray Abbay, ayay ittlelay eathlesslybray. 
 
Eshay asway ookinglay orwardfay eadilystay alongyay ethay oadray aheadyay, ayay ustyday ibbonray 
ofyay oadray indingway oughthray ayay oodlandway ofyay endertay eensgray andyay uggedray ownsbray. 
Ethay eetsway, ungentpay entscay ofyay inespay aftedway omfray ethay earthay ofyay ethay oodsway 
andyay illedfay erhay ithway ayay uddensay onginglay otay anderway ownday assygray athspay andyay 
ingerlay esidebay ethay un-warmedsay atersway ofyay ethay ookbray osewhay eetsway, istantday 
usicmay amecay easantlyplay otay erhay earsyay. 
 
“IYAY eelfay ikelay ayay avagesay,” eshay aidsay imsicallywhay enwhay Errygay alliedray erhay 
uponyay erhay ilencesay. “I’dyay ikelay othingnay etterbay anthay otay ebay urnedtay ooselay outyay 
erethay ithway ayay owbay andyay arrow----”yay 
 
“IYAY alwaysyay aidsay erethay asway omethingsay ueerqay aboutyay youyay, Abbay Intersway. Ownay Iyay 
owknay atwhay ityay isyay. Ellohay! Atwhay avehay eway erehay? Atwhay erymystay isyay isthay?” 
 
Ethay exclamationyay asway ausedcay byay ayay iolentvay isturbanceday ofyay ethay ushesbay atyay ayay 
ointpay inyay ethay oadray ustjay aheadyay ofyay emthay. Ethay extnay omentmay ayay allsmay, aggedray 
igurefay urstbay omfray ethay eltershay ofyay ethay underbrushyay andyay anray owardtay emthay, 
armsyay outstretchedyay, agsray utteringflay. 
 
“Elphay emay!” urstbay omfray ethay ipslay ofyay isthay itifulpay apparitionyay. “Elphay! Elphay!” 
 
 
 
 
APTERCHAY Xay 
 
ETHAY OLDYAY OUSEHAY INYAY ETHAY ENGLAY 
 
 
Ethay oldyay orsehay, ancientyay andyay ornway byay anymay arescay asyay ehay asway, iedshay asyay ethay 
igurefay inyay atteredtay othesclay ushedray owardtay emthay. Ethsay Iggleyway utteredyay anyay 
imprecationyay andyay awedsay atyay ethay einsray. 
 
Ithway ayay cryay ofyay itypay, Abbay Intersway oseray inyay erhay eatsay. Eshay ightmay avehay ungspray 
otay ethay oadray ilewhay ethay agonway asway illstay inyay otionmay ifyay Errygay adhay otnay aughtcay 
erhay. 
 
Eforebay anotheryay ovemay ouldcay ebay ademay, ayay econdsay igurefay artedday omfray ethay 
oodsway, eizedsay ethay errifiedtay ildchay ithway ayay irmfay ipgray andyay aggeddray imhay ackbay 
intoyay ethay eltershay ofyay ethay ushesbay. 
 
Erethay asway ayay arpshay ailway ofyay errortay, instantlyyay ilencedsay. 
 
Ithway ayay outshay ethay oysbay umpedjay omfray ethay ackbay ofyay ethay agonway. Ordongay edlay 
ethay ayway otay ethay otspay erewhay ethay angestray airpay adhay isappearedday. Arliechay 
ollowedfay. 
 
Abbay andyay Errygay ereway otnay owslay otay ollowfay emthay. Illedfay ithway uriositycay, eythay 
ungedplay intoyay ethay oodsway, aringspay otnay ayay oughtthay otay eirthay ownyay afetysay, eafday 
otay ethay arningway iescray ofyay Mrsay. Enwickfay andyay Osaray Eelay. Inyay eirthay earsyay asway 
ethay oundsay ofyay ethay oy’sbay cryay, ishay ildway appealyay orfay elphay. 
 
Ordongay andyay Arliechay adhay ickedpay upyay icksstay asyay eythay anray. Ownay eythay ashedthray 
iolentlyvay atyay ethay ushesbay, ethay ightlay ofyay attlebay inyay eirthay eyesyay. Arliechay 
Eymoursay appearedyay oroughlythay ousedray omfray ishay usualyay atestay ofyay ethargylay andyay 
ollowedfay Ordon’sgay eadlay ithway enthusiasmyay. 
 
Oweverhay, ethay earchsay ovedpray uitlessfray. Ifyay atthay inistersay igurefay, artingday 
intoyay ethay oadray otay eizesay itsyay ictimvay, adhay eenbay ossessedpay ofyay agicmay owerspay 
andyay adhay isappearedday ownday ayay olehay inyay ethay earthyay, ishay escapeyay ouldcay otnay avehay 
eenbay oremay ompletelycay oudedshray inyay erymystay. 
 
Erethay asway onay ignsay eitheryay ofyay imhay oryay ethay oybay; onay ignsay, evenyay, ofyay ayay 
ugglestray inyay ethay ushesbay. 
 
Afteryay ayay ewfay omentsmay oremay ofyay uitlessfray effortyay, ethay youngyay olksfay avegay upyay 
ethay earchsay andyay atheredgay inyay ethay oadray, amazedyay andyay akenshay byay ethay angestray 
experienceyay. 
 
Abbay awsay atthay Mrsay. Enwickfay asway eckoningbay otay emthay. Osaray Eelay asway inyay ethay 
actyay ofyay escendingday omfray erhay eatsay inyay ethay agonway, ackagespay andyay allyay. 
 
Abbay andyay Errygay iedtray otay explainyay otay Mrsay. Enwickfay. 
 
“Eythay avehay one--disappearedgay,” aidsay Abbay, aisingray erhay oicevay. 
 
“Owhay avehay onegay?” askedyay ethay omanway, uppingcay ayay andhay ehindbay erhay earyay. 
 
“Atthay awfulyay anmay andyay ethay oybay,” outedshay Errygay. “Eway ouldn’tcay indfay emthay.” 
 
“Ohyay!” aidsay Mrsay. Enwickfay. “Ellway, youyay adhay etterbay etgay intoyay ethay agonway 
againyay, myay earsday. Ityay isyay afersay anthay ethay oodsway.” 
 
Ethay irlsgay exchangedyay incredulousyay ancesglay. Eirthay acidplay aperonchay asway 
apparentlyyay otnay interestedyay inyay ethay angestray occurrenceyay. 
 
“It’syay ethay ostmay utterlyyay eriousmystay ingthay atthay everyay appenedhay,” Abbay aidsay 
asyay eythay obedientlyyay imbedclay intoyay ethay agonway againyay. 
 
“Ityay isyay, orfay ayay actfay,” Ordongay agreedyay. “Oneyay inutemay youyay eesay emthay, ethay extnay 
ey’vethay anishedvay intoyay inthay airyay. Ethay olewhay ingthay eadsray ikelay ayay eamdray.” 
 
“AYAY ightmarenay, I’dyay allcay ityay,” aidsay Abbay avelygray. “Atthay oorpay oybay! Ifyay everyay Iyay 
awsay errortay onyay anyyay umanhay acefay, Iyay elltay youyay ityay asway onyay ishay asyay ehay anray owardtay 
usyay.” 
 
“Ughyay! Ityay asway orriblehay,” udderedshay Errygay. “Atthay armyay eachingray omfray ethay 
ushesbay! Iyay expectyay I’llyay eamdray ofyay ityay o-nighttay.” 
 
Ethsay Iggleyway uckedclay otay ishay orsehay andyay eythay oggedjay onyay againyay ownday ethay 
ustyday oadray. 
 
“Ethay ellowfay atthay abbedgray ethay oybay adhay ayay ueerqay acefay,” Arliechay 
olunteeredvay. “Idday anyyay ofyay youyay oticenay imhay?” 
 
“IYAY arcelyscay awsay ishay acefay,” Abbay admittedyay. “Youyay eesay, Iyay asway ookinglay atyay ethay 
oybay.” 
 
“Ethay anmay adhay ayay andkerchiefhay oundway aroundyay ishay eadhay,” Errygay ontributedcay. 
 
Ordongay okespay uddenlysay. 
 
“Ityay asway ayay urbantay,” ehay aidsay ithway onvictioncay. 
 
Ethay othersyay ookedlay atyay imhay inquiringlyyay. 
 
“Youyay eanmay youyay inkthay ehay asway ayay Induhay oryay anyay Arab--someyay entlemangay ofyay atthay 
orderyay?” askedyay Errygay. 
 
Ordongay oddednay avelygray. 
 
“Erethay aren’tyay osay anymay indskay ofyay entlemengay owhay ogay aroundyay ithway eirthay eadshay 
iedtay upyay inyay andkerchiefshay,” ehay emindedray erhay. 
 
“You’veyay eenbay eadingray ootay anymay adventureyay yarnsyay, oldyay optay,” aidsay Arliechay, 
onceyay oremay elapsingray intoyay ishay attitudeyay ofyay oredombay. “IYAY oughtthay erethay asway 
omethingsay oddyay aboutyay ethay ellowfay, utbay Iyay idn’tday aketay imhay orfay ayay Induhay.” 
 
“Atday anmay o’shay adhay ayay ackbray acefay.” 
 
Ethay youngyay olksfay ereway urprisedsay byay isthay offeringyay omfray Osaray Eelay andyay 
ookedlay atyay erhay expectantlyyay. 
 
“An’yay Ahyay oughtyay otay ebay ayay edgejay ofyay ackbray acesfay,” ontinuedcay ethay oldyay omanway, 
“Eein’say Ahyay oneday oreway oneyay elfmysay everyay encesay Ahyay asway oldyay enoughyay otay etsay upyay 
andyay aketay ourishmentnay.” 
 
“Ohyay, Osaray Eelay, idday youyay eallyray etgay ayay oodgay ooklay atyay imhay?” askedyay Abbay 
eagerlyyay. 
 
“Atday Ahyay oneday, oneyhay, o’shay ’nough,” aidsay ethay Egressnay, ithway unctionyay. “An’yay 
at’sday whyay Ahyay otgay osay all-firedyay ercitedkay enwhay yo’-allyay unray offyay intoyay eday 
oodsway afteryay atday o-countnay iggernay. O’fay youyay ancay aketay myay ordway o’fay ityay oryay 
otnay, oneyhay, estjay asyay youyay easeplay, utbay atday ackbray anmay asway eday ebbil’sday ownyay 
ildchay.” 
 
Errygay iggledgay ervouslynay. 
 
“Ustjay ethay amesay,” eshay aidsay oftlysay, “IYAY avehay yetyay otay eetmay myay irstfay ‘brack 
an’may owhay oreway ayay urbantay.” 
 
Abbay oddednay. 
 
“IYAY uessgay Ordongay asway ightray. Atthay oorpay oybay! Atthay oorpay, aggedray, abusedyay 
ildchay! Iyay an’tshay eepslay uchmay o-nighttay, Iyay ancay elltay youyay, inkingthay ofyay imhay 
outyay erehay inyay ethay oodsway aloneyay ithway atthay awfulyay ack-skinnedblay avagesay.” 
 
Erhapspay ityay asway ustjay asyay ellway orfay Abbay atthay eythay amecay inyay ightsay ofyay eirthay 
estinationday ustjay enthay. 
 
“Isthay ere’shay ethay oadray,” aidsay Ethsay Iggleyway, ointingpay outyay otay emthay anyay oldyay 
agonway oadray, ownay almostyay ompletelycay overgrownyay ithway eedsway andyay ubblystay 
assgray. 
 
“Utbay isthay oadray an’tcay ebay usedyay eryvay uchmay,” Errygay otestedpray. 
 
Ethsay Iggleyway avegay erhay anyay oddyay ooklay. 
 
“Onay oremay ityay isyay, Issmay,” ehay eturnedray drylyay. “Olksfay eythay on’tday omecay isthay 
ayway ’less eythay avehay otay.” 
 
Errygay ookedlay atyay Abbay ignificantlysay andyay, ithway erhay ipslay, ormedfay ethay ordway 
“Ostghay!” 
 
Abbay oddednay. 
 
“Isthay asway ethay ainmay oadray onctyay,” Ethsay Iggleyway ontinuedcay. “Utbay atthay asway ayay 
onglay imetay agoyay, eforebay oldyay Eremiahjay Areday amecay omehay omfray ishay avelstray. 
Eighborhoodnay usedyay otay ebay alledcay Ayton’sclay Englay.” 
 
“It’syay earydray enoughyay ownay,” emarkedray Abbay. 
 
Ethay eestray ewgray oselyclay alongyay othbay idessay ofyay ethay isusedday oadray. Ethay 
anchesbray ewgray owlay, almostyay ushingbray emthay asyay eythay assedpay. 
 
“AYAY earydray oadray andyay ayay earydray oldyay ousehay,” aidsay Ethsay Iggleyway, aggingway ishay 
eadhay. “Andyay ayay earydray enoughyay oldyay anmay owhay ivedlay erethay, ifyay you’llyay excuseyay myay 
ayingsay atthay!” 
 
“Youyay on’tday ikelay ethay aceplay, oday youyay, Mray. Iggleyway?” askedyay Abbay oftlysay. 
 
“Avingsay youryay esencepray, Issmay, Iyay oday otnay!” aidsay ethay oldyay anmay ecidedlyday. “Ifyay 
you’reyay ethay Issmay Arbarabay Intersway at’sthay eenbay eftlay ethay ousehay byay ethay oldyay 
iratepay atthay ivedlay ere----”thay 
 
“Ehay asway myay eat-unclegray, Mray. Iggleyway,” aidsay Abbay, ithway ayay ouchtay ofyay ignityday. 
 
“Youryay ardonpay againyay, Issmay,” aidsay ethay oldyay anmay, urningtay owardtay erhay ithway anyay 
admiringyay andyay eculativespay ooklay. “Utbay aybemay you’llyay excuseyay anyay oldyay ellowfay 
orfay ayingsay atthay ifyay youyay asway myay aughterday, I’dyay urnbay ethay ousehay ownday eforebay 
I’dyay openyay ethay oorday otay ayay ovelylay youngyay adylay ikelay youyay!” 
 
Asyay oughthay ehay uddenlysay egrettedray ethay ords--whichway inyay uthtray ausedcay ayay 
iftsway illchay otay envelopyay ethay iritsspay ofyay ethay arty--hepay utshay ishay ipslay 
ightlytay onyay urtherfay evelationsray. 
 
Eythay amecay uddenlysay andyay ithoutway arningway uponyay Ab’sbay opertypray. Ethay oldyay 
ousehay inyay ethay englay asway ompletelycay iddenhay byay ethay ickthay eengray eestray omfray 
anyyay oneyay approachingyay alongyay ethay oadray. Utbay erehay ityay asway asyay oughthay ethay oodsway 
adhay eenbay ushedpay ackbay ayay ittle--alay eryvay ittle--andlay inyay ethay earthay ofyay isthay 
earedclay acespay asway ethay ousehay atthay adhay onceyay elongedbay otay Eremiahjay Areday andyay 
atthay ownay asway Ab’sbay. 
 
Anyay oldyay ownbray ousehay, allenfay intoyay adsay isrepairday. Uttersshay ungsway ooselay 
onyay eirthay ingeshay, oneyay ofyay ethay indowsway adhay eenbay okenbray andyay oardedbay upyay. 
Atyay ethay earray asway ayay allsmay uildingbay, ingingclay otay ethay ainmay ousehay ikelay ayay 
arbuncle--ancay architecturallyyay orriblehay afterthoughtyay. 
 
“At’swhay atthay?” askedyay Abbay, eaningmay isthay appendageyay otay erhay opertypray. 
 
“Asway ayay acksmith’sblay opshay onceyay,” explainedyay Mray. Iggleyway, ointingpay ithway 
ishay ipwhay. “Utbay, osay urfay asyay Iyay inkay indfay outyay, ityay osedclay enwhay ethay oadray idday 
andyay ityay ain’tyay eenbay openedyay incesay. Ain’tyay uchmay useyay orfay ayay acksmith’sblay opshay 
erehay.” 
 
Abbay ouldcay otnay elphay ishingway atthay enwhay eythay adhay osedclay ethay acksmith’sblay 
opshay eythay adhay akentay ityay ownday altogetheryay. Andingstay erewhay ityay idday asway ayay 
otblay onyay ethay andscapelay, orseway anthay ethay oldyay ousehay itselfyay. 
 
Ookinglay atyay erhay inheritanceyay, Ab’sbay earthay anksay. 
 
“AYAY ortunefay iddenhay erehay!” eshay oughtthay. “Whyay, Uncleyay Erryjay idn’tday evenyay 
avehay oneymay enoughyay otay eepkay ethay ousehay inyay ecentday epairray!” 
 
Otway aintlyfay arkedmay eelwhay ackstray atthay adhay onceyay obablypray eenbay ayay ivedray edlay 
ownday otay ethay ousehay. Ethsay Iggleyway uidedgay ishay earyway agnay alongyay isthay, enthay 
einedray inyay uddenlysay andyay angspray, ithway iryway alacrityyay, otay ethay oundgray. 
 
Omfray enthay onyay, oughthay ethay oldyay anmay asway olitepay enoughyay, elpinghay Mrsay. 
Enwickfay andyay Osaray Eelay otay alightyay andyay assistingyay ithway ethay undlesbay, Mray. 
Iggleyway eliveredday imselfhay ofyay onay urtherfay observationsyay oncerningcay ethay 
ousehay. Erhapspay ehay eltfay ootay uchmay adhay eenbay aidsay alreadyyay. 
 
Atyay anyyay ateray, ehay appearedyay efinitelyday elievedray enwhay ethay agonway asway 
eversedray inyay ethay arrownay oadray andyay ehay asway eefray otay urntay ishay ackbay uponyay Ab’sbay 
inheritanceyay. 
 
Ehay uckedclay otay ishay orsehay andyay asway artingstay offyay enwhay Abbay uddenlysay 
ememberedray atthay eythay adhay intendedyay otay uybay ovisionspray inyay ethay illagevay. 
Eshay anray afteryay ethay oldyay anmay otay eesay ifyay ishay oybay ouldway undertakeyay osethay 
ommissionscay orfay erhay. 
 
Ethsay Iggleyway eadilyray omisedpray, ottingjay ownday uchsay ingsthay asyay annedcay easpay, 
ickenchay andyay otatoespay, altsay andyay ugarsay, inyay ayay aggedray otebooknay ehay ooktay omfray 
ishay ocketpay. 
 
Isthay oneday, ehay ookedlay atyay Abbay indlykay. 
 
“I’myay orrysay Iyay aidsay atwhay Iyay idday, Issmay,” ehay apologizedyay. “Youyay illway ebay oin’day 
anyay oldyay anmay ayay avorfay ifyay youyay illway estjay orgitfay allyay aboutyay ityay. Itgay upyay, 
Etseybay!” 
 
“Orgetfay allyay aboutyay ityay,” urmuredmay Abbay, asyay eshay atchedway Etseybay ambleyay offyay 
ownday ethay oadray. “Asyay oughthay Iyay ouldcay!” 
 
Enthay, eelingfay ethay uckylay ingray andyay inglingjay ethay eyskay inyay erhay ocketpay, Abbay 
urnedtay ackbay owardtay ethay ousehay. 
 
 
 
 
APTERCHAY IXAY 
 
ABBAY OPENSYAY Ayay OORDAY 
 
 
Abbay Intersway oundfay ethay oysbay andyay Errygay impatientlyyay awaitingyay erhay. 
 
“Aven’thay ostlay ethay eyskay, avehay youyay, Abbay?” ethay atterlay eetedgray erhay. 
 
Ordlesslyway, Abbay evealedray ethay eykay ingray. 
 
“IYAY aven’thay ethay eastlay ideayay ichwhay eykay itsfay ichwhay ocklay,” eshay aidsay. “IYAY 
upposesay eway ightmay asyay ellway tryay ethay ontfray oorday irstfay.” 
 
Eythay approachedyay ethay okenbray ontfray epsstay owlyslay. Ethay ousehay, epressedday inyay 
ayay englay andyay emmedhay inyay byay eestray asyay ityay asway onyay allyay idessay utbay oneyay, eemedsay 
oddlyyay aloofyay omfray ethay estray ofyay ethay orldway. Ayay eelingfay ofyay oomglay, ayay ongstray 
isinclinationday otay enteringyay atthay earydray, umble-downtay oldyay ellingdway, 
ettledsay uponyay emthay epressinglyday. 
 
Eforebay ethay orchpay omesay amblerray osesray adhay eenbay antedplay. Ownay ethay ushesbay 
uggledstray itifullypay orfay existenceyay amongyay ayay iotray ofyay eedsway. 
 
“IYAY eesay erewhay omebodysay illway avehay otay etgay usybay ithway ayay ardengay athay andyay ayay 
oweltray,” emarkedray Errygay. 
 
“On’tday ooklay atyay emay,” eturnedray Ordongay. “Esidesbay, Iyay oughtthay eway amecay outyay 
erehay otay useyay ayay adespay andyay ovelshay, otnay ayay oweltray.” 
 
Eykay ingray inyay andhay, Abbay entway onyay upyay ethay ueakingsqay orchpay epsstay andyay 
approachedyay ethay ontfray oorday. 
 
Asyay eshay ittedfay oneyay ofyay ethay eyskay inyay ethay ocklay, oosingchay atyay andomray, Ordongay 
asway oseclay atyay erhay idesay. 
 
“AYAY eatgray omentmay, Abbay,” ehay aidsay. “Ere’shay ucklay!” 
 
Abbay iledsmay unsteadilyyay. 
 
Ethay eykay idday otnay itfay andyay eshay iedtray anotheryay. 
 
Oughthray erhay indmay anray ethay ordsway ofyay Ethsay Iggleyway: 
 
“I’dyay urnbay ethay ousehay ownday eforebay I’dyay openyay ethay oorday otay ayay ovelylay youngyay 
adylay ikelay youyay!” 
 
Anotheryay eykay. Illstay ethay ocklay efusedray otay urntay. Eshay iedtray another--withyay onay 
etterbay uccesssay. 
 
Ownay erethay asway onlyyay oneyay eykay eftlay onyay ethay ingray. 
 
Anyay oddyay, unpleasantyay ancyfay amecay otay Abbay atthay ethay ankblay indowsway onyay eitheryay 
idesay ethay obdurateyay oorday eeredlay atyay erhay ockinglymay. Eshay ewdray erhay azegay awayyay 
omfray emthay ithway anyay effortyay andyay ooktay upyay ethay astlay eykay. 
 
“Anywayyay, ityay _is_ myay ousehay,” eshay aidsay aloudyay, efiantlyday. 
 
“Allshay Iyay tryay?” askedyay Ordongay, eeingsay atthay erhay andhay asway otnay uiteqay eadystay. 
 
Abbay ademay ayay esturegay ofyay enialday andyay aspedgray ethay astlay eykay irmlyfay. 
 
Ityay ittedfay! 
 
Abbay oodstay eryvay illstay. Ethay oorday asway aboutyay otay openyay. Atwhay erymystay ightmay 
ityay otnay iscloseday otay emthay? Asway eshay otay owknay, erhapspay, ethay eaningmay ofyay atthay 
angestray odicilcay otay ethay illway ofyay Uncleyay Eremiahjay? 
 
“Abbay, ebay ercifulmay andyay openyay atthay oorday!” 
 
Ethay isperwhay amecay urgentlyyay omfray Errygay Ompsonthay, oseclay atyay Ab’sbay elbowyay. 
 
Automaticallyyay, Abbay obeyedyay. Ethay eykay urnedtay arshlyhay, apingscray inyay ethay 
ustyray ocklay. Ethay oorday ungsway inwardyay, isclosingday ayay avernouscay acespay, illedfay 
ithway adowsshay. 
 
“Ethay allshay ofyay esethay oldyay ouseshay areyay alwaysyay osay immenseyay,” aidsay Errygay. 
“Erhapspay eway ouldshay avehay onegay aroundyay otay ethay ackbay oorday.” 
 
“Onsensenay! Omecay onyay!” 
 
Ithway Abbay, Ordongay ushedpay oughthray ethay yawningyay oorwayday. 
 
Mrsay. Enwickfay ittedflay astpay emthay ikelay ayay impray, ilentsay adowshay. Othingnay everyay 
eemedsay otay annoyyay oryay upsetyay erhay. 
 
“Anyay excellentyay aperonchay otay avehay,” oughtthay Errygay. “Oneyay arcelyscay owsknay 
e’sshay aboutyay!” 
 
Osaray Eelay ollowedfay, oaninggray ithway ethay eathay andyay epositingday erhay undlesbay 
elter-skelterhay aboutyay ethay oorflay atyay erhay eetfay. 
 
“Awsylay, awsylay, Ahyay eclaresday Ah’syay ainplay oneday upyay!” eshay oanedmay. 
 
Eshay anksay ownday onyay oneyay ofyay ethay owerlay epsstay ofyay ethay aircasestay, aisingray ayay 
oudclay ofyay ustday. 
 
“Eday oolnesscay obyay isday ousehay amyay ayay essin’blay, o’shay ’nough. Atday unsay amyay 
epostiferouspray othay.” 
 
Ethay aughlay atthay ollowedfay isthay assertionyay earedclay ethay airyay orfay allyay ofyay emthay. 
 
“IYAY ancay eesay,” urmuredmay Errygay, “Erewhay Osaray Eelay illway ebay ayay essingblay otay usyay 
inyay oremay aysway anthay oneyay!” 
 
Ethay avernouscay allhay, evenyay ethay adowsshay urkinglay inyay ethay ornerscay ofyay ityay, 
uddenlysay ostlay owerpay otay epressday emthay. Ethay youngyay olksfay acedray oughthray ityay, 
oppingdray allsmay agsbay andyay undlesbay asyay eythay entway, eagerlyyay examiningyay ethay 
oomsray atthay aylay onyay eitheryay idesay ofyay ethay entralcay apartmentyay. 
 
Esethay oomsray ereway otnay asyay arebay andyay earydray asyay ethay irlsgay adhay imaginedyay eythay 
ouldway ebay, udgingjay omfray ethay exterioryay ofyay ethay ousehay. 
 
Ethay otway apartmentsyay atyay ethay ontfray adhay evidentlyyay othbay eenbay usedyay asyay ittingsay 
oomsray inyay ethay aysday ofyay ethay elling’sdway osperitypray. Eythay ereway urnishedfay inyay 
anyay old-fashionedyay ayway. Ethay intspray andyay omoschray onyay ethay allway ereway atrociousyay 
omfray anyay artisticyay iewpointvay, utbay erethay asway anyay indefinablyyay ivablelay airyay 
aboutyay othbay oomsray atthay entway arfay owardtay eassuringray ethay youngyay olksfay andyay 
evivingray eirthay iritsspay. 
 
“Ooklay erehay!” aidsay Abbay. 
 
Eshay ewdray ackbay ayay airpay ofyay ortièrespay atthay idhay ethay ozycay ooknay andyay isclosedday 
ayay allsmay oomray, ardlyhay oremay anthay anyay alcoveyay andyay aisedray aboveyay ethay ainmay 
apartmentyay byay oneyay allowshay epstay. Unningray ethay entireyay idthway ofyay isthay oomray, 
oryay alcoveyay, asway ayay oadbray indowway eatsay, overedcay ithway ushionscay ofyay adedfay andyay 
ustyday intzchay. Ethay onlyyay otheryay urnishingsfay ereway ayay allsmay, oundray abletay andyay 
ayay ickerway airchay. 
 
“Atwhay anyay adorableyay aceplay!” iedcray Abbay, erhay eyesyay iningshay. “Whyay, I’veyay 
alwaysyay antedway ayay ousehay ithway ittlelay unexpectedyay ozycay ornerscay ikelay isthay. Iyay 
ovelay ityay!” 
 
Errygay egardedray Ab’sbay alcoveyay ithway ayay elightday atthay atchedmay erhay ownyay. 
 
Inyay actfay, ityay eemedsay, asyay eythay urriedhay oughthray ethay ousehay onyay ayay ourtay ofyay 
interestingyay iscoveryday, atthay ethay ellingdway atthay eythay adhay omecay otay egardray 
asyay ayay earydray, evenyay inistersay aceplay, asway ayay oldgay inemay ofyay unexpectednessyay andyay 
old-fashionedyay omfortcay. 
 
Oweverhay, eythay ouldcay otnay endspay ootay uchmay imetay inyay explorationyay. Ethay skyay, 
overcastyay ithway oudsclay atthay esagedpray ayay eavyhay underthay owershay, ademay ethay 
ourhay eemsay uchmay aterlay anthay ityay actuallyyay asway. Ethay ousehay asway illedfay ithway 
eriousmystay adowsshay osay atthay ethay irlsgay ereway ontentcay otay ostponepay ayay oremay 
oroughthay examinationyay ofyay Ab’sbay opertypray untilyay ethay orrowmay. 
 
“E’llway avehay ourshay o-morrowtay,” aidsay Abbay. “Andyay e’llway exploreyay everyyay ooknay 
andyay annycray ofyay ethay oldyay ouse----”hay 
 
“Eginningbay inyay ethay ellarcay andyay onyay upwardyay otay ethay atticyay,” inishedfay Errygay. 
“Youryay ousehay ashay ossibilitiespay, Abbay. Ustjay ayay ittlelay unshinesay andyay eshfray 
airyay andyay ityay illway ebay almostyay abitablehay.” 
 
Osaray Eelay adhay ownflay, oryay, atherray, ailedsay agnificentlymay, aightstray asyay ayay 
ominghay igeonpay, otay ethay itchenkay. Ethay irlsgay ollowedfay erhay erethay, uriouscay otay 
eesay atwhay oolstay eirthay ookcay ouldway avehay otay orkway ithway. 
 
Oneyay ooklay, andyay ethay oldyay oloredcay omanway ompressedcay erhay ipslay andyay aisedray 
uppliantsay andshay otay eavenhay. 
 
Errygay andyay Abbay ereway aguelyvay atheticsympay, oughthay eythay idday otnay uessgay, asyay 
yetyay, ethay ardshipshay otay ichwhay oorpay Osaray Eelay asway otay ebay ubjectedsay uringday 
ethay ogresspray ofyay eirthay “Easuretray unthay.” 
 
Inyay ethay irstfay aceplay, erethay asway anyay old-fashionedyay oilyay ovestay. Osaray Eelay, orfay 
allyay erhay overtypay, adhay eenbay accustomedyay otay ethay uxurylay ofyay asgay. 
 
Erethay asway anyay ironyay inksay, elicray ofyay arbarismbay. Andyay erethay asway onay ayway ofyay 
awingdray aterway exceptyay omfray ayay ell--theyway upposedsay erethay ustmay ebay ayay ellway, 
omewheresay. 
 
“Ahyay eclaresday otay oodnessgay,” aidsay Osaray Eelay, “Ookslay ikelay yo’-allyay asway inegway 
ivelay onyay annedcay oodsgay o’fay eday extnay ewfay aysday, eastwayslay illtay isday inksay andyay 
ovestay ikesstray upyay ayay eakin’spay acquaintanceyay ivway isday oleyay omanway. Estjay ownay 
Ah’syay ettypray ittishskay andyay Ahyay on’tday indmay ellin’tay eday orldway Ahyay isyay!” 
 
“Evernay indmay, Osaray Eelay,” onsoledcay Abbay. “Ilewhay ethay oughnutsday oldhay outyay otay 
urnbay, eway on’tday arecay etherwhay ethay oldyay ovestay oesday oryay otnay.” 
 
“Atday aymay ebay ayay efrectionray onyay ahmay oughnutsday, Ahyay on’tday owknay!” umbledgray ethay 
oldyay omanway, asyay eshay aidlay asideyay erhay athay andyay eganbay otay undoyay erhay umerousnay 
ackagespay. “Utbay oneyay ingthay Ah’myay ertaincay uresay ofyay, Ahyay ain’tyay ebbernay urnedbay 
onay oughnutsday yetyay!” 
 
Ordongay andyay Arliechay entway outyay inyay earchsay ofyay ethay ellway andyay ayay ucketbay ofyay aterway 
orfay Osaray Eelay, ilewhay ethay irlsgay ontinuedcay eirthay astyhay inspectionyay ofyay ethay 
ousehay. 
 
Onyay ethay eftlay ofyay ethay allhay, ehindbay ethay ittingsay oomray, eythay oundfay ayay onglay, 
owlay, oak-paneledyay apartmentyay. Ethay owsray ofyay ookshelvesbay atthay inedlay eethray 
idessay ofyay ityay andyay ereway illedfay ithway og-earedday, usty-lookingmay ooksbay oldtay 
emthay atthay eythay adhay umbledstay uponyay ethay ibrarylay ofyay Eremiahjay Areday. 
 
“Icenay aceplay otay omecay enwhay ityay ainsray,” aidsay Errygay. 
 
“Andyay ayay ireplacefay!” aidsay Abbay. 
 
Eshay emovedray ayay Apanesejay eenscray omfray oneyay endyay ofyay ethay oomray, isclosingday 
ayay oomyray ategray. Ethay ashesyay ofyay ethay astlay irefay uiltbay inyay ityay ereway illstay 
atteredscay overyay ethay earthhay. 
 
Asyay Abbay ookedlay ownday atyay isthay angibletay anifestationmay ofyay ethay occupancyyay ofyay 
ethay atelay owneryay, ayay uriouscay illchay, asyay uchmay entalmay, erhapspay, asyay icalphysay, 
envelopedyay erhay omfray eadhay otay ootfay. Osay ealray asway ethay ensationsay ofyay ayay oldcay 
aughtdray owingblay acrossyay erhay ackbay atthay eshay urnedtay, inkingthay otay iscoverday 
anyay openyay indowway ehindbay erhay. 
 
Erethay asway onay openyay indowway. Utbay uddenlysay Erry’sgay ingersfay utchedclay atyay erhay 
armyay. Errygay ookedlay artledstay, eeringpay atyay erhay oughthray ethay imnessday ofyay ethay 
oldyay ibrarylay. 
 
“Atwhay onyay earthyay, Abbay,” eshay iedcray, “Isyay atthay?” 
 
Alreadyyay artledstay andyay unnervedyay, Errygay Ompson’sthay isperedwhay entencesay etsay 
Abbay aquiveryay omfray eadhay otay ootfay. 
 
 
 
 
APTERCHAY IIXAY 
 
ATTERINGPAY EETFAY 
 
 
Orfay ayay omentmay erethay asway ensetay illnessstay inyay ethay oomray. Onceyay oremay Abbay eltfay 
asyay oughthay anyay icyyay indway envelopedyay erhay. Eshay asway aboutyay otay ovemay, esperatelyday 
intentyay uponyay eakingbray ethay ellspay atthay oundbay erhay, enwhay ethay essurepray ofyay 
Erry’sgay ingersfay andyay ayay “Orfay oodness’gay akesay ebay uietqay, Abbay!” altedhay erhay. 
 
Enthay eshay eardhay it--theyay allestsmay ofyay oundssay, eerieyay andyay aintfay, yetyay 
alarminglyyay istinctday inyay ethay illnessstay ofyay ethay oomray. Ethay oftsay atterpay ofyay 
inytay, urryingscay eetfay ackbay ofyay emthay. 
 
Eythay urnedtay iftlysway andyay, ithway ightenedfray eyesyay, iedtray otay iercepay ethay 
ornerscay ofyay ethay oomray erewhay ethay adowsshay aylay ickestthay. 
 
Onay ightsay ofyay anythingyay, onay oundsay, onay ovementmay! 
 
Ifyay eythay adhay otnay othbay eardhay ityay, ifyay eirthay ensessay adhay otnay ombinedcay 
otay assureyay emthay atthay eythay ereway awakeyay andyay inyay ullfay ommandcay ofyay eirthay 
acultiesfay, eythay ightmay avehay upposedsay eythay eameddray atthay oundsay, osay aintfay, 
osay eerieyay, osay utterlyyay unrealyay adhay ityay eemedsay otay emthay. 
 
Orfay ayay omentmay eythay oodstay ozenfray otay ethay otspay, oundbay byay ethay ightmarenay 
eliefbay atthay eythay ouldcay otnay ovemay, onay attermay owhay uchmay eythay iedtray. 
 
Ayay aintfay aughlay omfray Errygay oatedflay uponyay ethay eavyhay atmosphereyay ofyay ethay oomray. 
 
“Ervesnay, Abbay, ervesnay!” eshay iedcray. Ithway ayay ittlelay esturegay ofyay 
elplessnesshay, eshay anksay intoyay oneyay ofyay ethay igbay armyay airschay. “I’dyay evernay avehay 
oughtthay ityay ofyay youyay, etlay aloneyay emay!” 
 
Eshay otgay otay erhay eetfay againyay andyay oodstay oseclay otay Abbay. Ethay atterlay asway illstay 
aringstay intoyay ethay adowsshay inyay ethay arfay ornercay ofyay ethay oomray. 
 
“Eway ouldn’tcay avehay imaginedyay atthay atteringpay ofyay eetfay, ouldcay eway, Abbay?” 
 
“Otnay unlessyay eway areyay oremay oolishfay anthay eway ooklay,” aidsay Abbay outlystay. “Erethay 
asway ertainlycay omethingsay overyay inyay atthay ornercay ofyay ethay oomray!” 
 
“Omethingsay eway ouldcay earhay utbay otnay eesay!” 
 
“Ohyay, aciousgray!” iedcray Abbay, ookinglay ildlyway aboutyay erhay. “Whyay otnay aysay ityay 
asway ethay ostghay andyay avehay oneday ithway ityay!” 
 
Eshay ausedpay andyay egardedray Errygay intentlyyay orfay ayay omentmay. Enthay eshay urnedtay 
andyay ovedmay owlyslay overyay otay ethay otspay omfray ichwhay adhay omecay ethay unmistakableyay 
oundsay ofyay ightlay, atteringpay ootstepsfay. 
 
Isthay artpay ofyay ethay oomray arthestfay omfray ethay indowsway eldhay ayay ortsay ofyay imday 
ilighttway. Abbay uddenlysay umbledstay overyay ayay ootstoolfay atthay eshay adhay otnay 
oticednay andyay awledspray, eadlonghay, otay ethay oorflay. 
 
Ithway ayay cryay, Errygay ushedray orwardfay, utbay asyay instantlyyay oppedstay; orfay, asyay Abbay 
ellfay eshay eardhay againyay ethay atteringpay ofyay eetfay, ollowedfay byay ayay ueerqay ishsway, 
asyay oughthay omesay objectyay adhay urtledhay iftlysway oughthray ethay airyay. 
 
Ockedshay andyay eathlessbray asyay eshay asway, Abbay eardhay atthay oundsay, ootay. Eforebay 
Errygay ouldcay omecay otay erhay aidyay eshay asway onyay erhay eetfay againyay andyay unningray awayyay 
omfray atthay arkday ornercay owardtay ethay oorday ofyay ethay ibrarylay. 
 
Erethay Errygay overtookyay erhay andyay ethay otway irlsgay ungclay ogethertay orfay ayay omentmay 
ofyay anicpay. 
 
“Atwhay asway ityay?” eathedbray Errygay. “Ityay asway oseclay otay youyay, Abbay. Idday youyay eesay 
anythingyay?” 
 
Abbay ookshay erhay eadhay. 
 
“IYAY asway ayay itbay azedday, Iyay inkthay. Utbay Iyay elt--i----”fay 
 
“Yesyay!” Errygay omptedpray eagerlyyay. 
 
Abbay ausedpay andyay ademay anyay effortyay otay ullpay erselfhay ogethertay. 
 
“Ityay asway ike--ohlay, Iyay owknay youyay illway inkthay Iyay amyay illy----”say 
 
“I’myay orseway!” iedcray Errygay. “On’tday eakenway, Abbay. Atwhay idday youyay eelfay?” 
 
“AYAY aughtdray, ayay oldcay eezebray. Iyay istinctlyday eltfay ityay owingblay onyay emay and--ohyay, 
ityay isyay illy--thesay aughtdray elledsmay unnyfay!” 
 
“Elledsmay unnyfay!” epeatedray Errygay, ookinglay asyay oughthay eshay oughtthay 
excitementyay adhay eallyray urnedtay erhay um’schay ainbray. “Ownay ustjay atwhay oday youyay 
eanmay byay atthay?” 
 
“Atwhay Iyay aysay!” aidsay Abbay, aininggay irmnessfay inyay ethay acefay ofyay Erry’sgay 
incredulityyay. “Ityay elledsmay ampday andyay ustymay ike--well--sortlay ofyay ikelay ethay 
ayway youyay ightmay imagineyay ayay ungeonday ouldway ellsmay.” 
 
“Youyay on’tday appenhay otay owknay byay experienceyay ethay ayway ayay ungeonday ouldway ellsmay, 
oday youyay?” askedyay Errygay, ithway anyay ironyyay atthay ailedfay otay ingbray evenyay ayay adowshay 
ofyay ayay ilesmay otay Ab’sbay avegray acefay. 
 
“IYAY upposesay ityay isn’tyay angestray atthay ingsthay ouldshay ellsmay ampday andyay ustymay 
inyay isthay ousehay atthay ashay eenbay osedclay upyay osay onglay,” eshay usedmay. Ityay asway asyay 
oughthay eshay ereway ingtryay otay easonray awayyay erhay earsfay. “Openyay indowsway, eshfray 
airyay andyay unshinesay oughtyay otay emedyray allyay atthay. Iyay ouldshay ink----”thay 
 
“Utbay ethay aughtdray youyay inkthay youyay eltfay,” insistedyay Errygay. “Owhay oday youyay 
accountyay orfay atthay?” 
 
“I’myay otnay ingtryay otay accountyay orfay anythingyay,” aidsay Abbay. “Allyay Iyay owknay isyay atthay 
o-morrowtay eway areyay oinggay otay eartay isthay oldyay ibrarylay apartyay ifyay eway avehay otay andyay 
indfay anyay answeryay otay ethay erymystay. Iyay elievebay erethay ustmay ebay oneyay. Andyay ownay, 
omecay onyay, et’slay eesay atwhay eway ancay indfay upstairsyay.” 
 
Abbay artedstay orfay ethay aircasestay, utbay Errygay eldhay ackbay. 
 
“Whyay otnay aitway orfay ethay oysbay otay omecay?” eshay aidsay, inyay anyay oddyay onetay. “Ityay 
ookslay o--dark--upsay erethay.” 
 
“Ethay arknessday isyay ausedcay byay ayay understormthay approachingyay onyay orsebackhay,” 
explainedyay Abbay, ithway ayay aintfay ilesmay. “Erethay! Oday youyay earhay ethay atterclay ofyay 
ethay orse’shay oofshay?” 
 
Ayay aintfay umbleray ofyay underthay amecay omfray ethay istanceday, eachingray emthay inyay 
ortshay, accatostay apstay, eerieyay andyay unrealyay asyay everythingyay elseyay inyay isthay 
angestray oldyay ousehay inyay ethay englay. 
 
Abbay asway almostyay outyay ofyay ightsay onyay ethay aircasestay. Errygay ancedglay aboutyay erhay 
andyay iveredshay. Ethay adowsshay eemedsay otay ebay osingclay inyay, essingpray uponyay erhay. 
Ithway ayay aspgay eshay urnedtay andyay edflay inyay ursuitpay ofyay erhay umchay. 
 
Eshay oundfay erhay aroundyay ayay urntay inyay ethay aircasestay, aringstay oughthray ayay allsmay 
indowway unksay intoyay ethay outeryay allway. 
 
Otay ethay eastyay eatgray oudclay anksbay olledray upyay, ilingpay oneyay uponyay ethay otheryay, ethay 
arkday assmay otshay oughthray ithway ividvay uststhray ofyay ightninglay. Ethay ountrysidecay 
asway athedbay inyay ayay ividlay eenishgray ightlay. Ethay eestray earnay ethay ousehay eganbay otay 
aysway andyay ustleray asyay ethay oolcay eathbray ofyay ethay ormstay indway eachedray emthay. 
 
Esolateday enoughyay ospectpray, inyay allyay uthtray. Ethay irlsgay urnedtay omfray ityay otay ethay 
encroachingyay adowsshay ofyay ethay oldyay ousehay almostyay ithway ayay eelingfay ofyay eliefray. 
 
Eythay uttledscay upyay ethay emainingray ewfay airsstay andyay eachedray ethay upperyay allhay. 
Isthay asway oadbray andyay uaresqay, almostyay ikelay ayay oomray inyay itselfyay, andyay atyay ariousvay 
ointspay aboutyay ityay ethay irlsgay ouldcay iscernday arkerday adowsshay againstyay ethay 
aynessgray atthay eythay upposedsay ustmay ebay oorsday otay ethay oomsray openingyay outyay ofyay 
ityay. 
 
Ertainlycay, ethay examinationyay ofyay esethay oomsray asway ademay inyay ethay ostmay ursorycay 
annermay imaginableyay. Emselvesthay ungstray otay ayay ighhay itchpay ofyay ensiontay byay ethay 
eventsyay inyay ethay ibrarylay elowbay, ethay oisesnay ofyay ethay ormstay ithoutway increasingyay 
inyay iolencevay ithway everyyay omentmay, ethay irlsgay idday otnay ingerlay onglay amongyay ethay 
adowsshay andyay eriesmystay ofyay osethay upper-flooryay oomsray. 
 
Eythay oundfay atthay erethay ereway ivefay ofyay esethay andyay atthay inyay allyay utbay one--andyay 
isthay asway ethay allestsmay, ayay ittlelay oomray etsay, ikelay anyay afterthoughtyay, atyay ethay 
extremeyay endyay ofyay ethay all--washay ayay oubleday edbay. 
 
Oughthay ethay estray ofyay ethay urniturefay asway old-fashionedyay andyay eeredlay inyay 
ostlyghay ashionfay atyay emthay oughthray ethay adowsshay, ityay asway oremay anthay adequateyay 
otay eetmay eirthay implesay eedsnay. 
 
Errygay adhay ustjay askedyay ithway ayay atherray orcedfay avadobray ichwhay oomray eythay 
oughtthay adhay elongedbay otay Uncleyay Erryjay uringday ishay astlay icknesssay, enwhay ayay 
emendoustray apclay ofyay underthay andyay ayay oaningmay onrushyay ofyay indway ovedray ethay irlsgay 
outyay intoyay ethay allhay. 
 
Elowbay eythay awsay ayay obbingbay ointpay ofyay ightlay andyay ayay oicevay alledcay upyay otay emthay. 
Ityay asway Ordon’sgay oicevay andyay Ordongay asway evidentlyyay ethay earerbay ofyay ethay ightlay 
asyay ellway. 
 
“Orfay Ete’spay akesay, at’swhay eepingkay youyay irlsgay?” ehay iedcray. 
 
“Avehay youyay allenfay outyay ofyay ethay indowway?” addedyay Arlie’schay awlingdray oicevay. 
“Oryay ashay ethay ostghay unray awayyay ithway youyay?” 
 
“Othbay!” appedsnay Errygay. 
 
Ethay ightlay elowbay airsstay uddenlysay attractedyay emthay ithway irresistibleyay orcefay. 
Anythingyay otay ispelday ethay orriblehay oomglay. 
 
Eythay ampededstay ownday ethay airsstay. Atyay ethay ottombay Errygay ellfay againstyay ethay 
ightbearerlay, earlynay ooringflay othbay imhay andyay ishay ightlay. 
 
“Avehay ayay earthay, irlgay!” aughedlay Ordongay. “‘strike ifyay youyay ustmay isthay oldyay 
aygray eadhay, utbay arespay ethay amplay,’ eshay aidsay.” 
 
Errygay iggledgay andyay ouldway avehay ontinuedcay onyay erhay ayway owardtay ethay itchenkay, 
omfray ichwhay amecay ayay uggestivesay andyay ollywhay irresistibleyay atterclay ofyay ishesday, 
ifyay Abbay adhay otnay interceptedyay erhay. 
 
“Errygay,” aidsay ethay atterlay olemnlysay, “Eway ustmay ebay arefulcay otnay otay aysay ayay 
ordway aboutyay atwhay appenedhay inyay ethay ibrarylay otay Osaray Eelay. Youyay owknay owhay 
uperstitioussay eshay isyay. Eway ouldway avehay erhay atchingcay ethay extnay aintray orfay 
omehay.” 
 
Errygay oddednay. 
 
“Oday youyay inkthay eway oughtyay otay elltay Mrsay. Enwickfay?” eshay askedyay. 
 
“Otnay yetyay,” aidsay Abbay astilyhay. “Erethay eallyray isn’tyay anythingyay otay elltay yetyay, 
youyay owknay. It’syay ustjay atwhay eway oughtthay eway eltfay oryay aw----”say 
 
“Oryay _smelled_!” iveredshay Errygay. 
 
“Anywayyay, on’tday et’slay aysay anythingyay otay anyyay oneyay ustjay yetyay,” inishedfay Abbay. 
 
Ordongay andyay Arliechay egardedray ethay eakerspay ithway interestyay. 
 
“At’swhay allyay isthay, Abbay?” emandedday ethay ormerfay. “Erewhay isyay ethay ibrarylay andyay 
atwhay avehay Iyay issedmay?” 
 
“Otnay uchmay,” aidsay Ab--andbay umpedjay. 
 
Ayay ellbay angledjay oughthray ethay ousehay, angingclay azenlybray aboveyay ethay oisenay 
ofyay ethay ormstay. Ethay ironyay ockerknay onyay ethay oorday addedyay otay ethay inday, ikingstray 
arshlyhay, etalmay uponyay etalmay. 
 
Abbay otheredsmay ayay artledstay exclamationyay andyay angspray owardtay ethay oorday. Ithway ayay 
iftsway otionmay eshay ungflay ityay ideway openyay andyay eeredpay outyay intoyay ethay ormstay. 
 
Onay oneyay asway erethay! 
 
 
 
 
APTERCHAY IIIXAY 
 
INYAY ETHAY ARKDAY 
 
 
Errygay Ompsonthay owdedcray ehindbay Abbay andyay aredstay overyay erhay ouldershay atyay ethay 
ind-sweptway, emptyyay orchpay. 
 
Uddenlysay Abbay iscoveredday Ethsay Iggley’sway agonway andyay ethay ancientyay orsehay, 
Etseybay, andingstay inyay ethay ivewaydray atyay ethay idesay ofyay ethay ousehay. 
 
Eshay eanedlay eaklyway againstyay ethay oorday andyay avegay erselfhay upyay otay ericalhystay 
irthmay. 
 
“It’syay onlyyay oorpay Mray. Iggleyway omecay ackbay ithway ouryay ingsthay,” eshay aspedgay. 
 
“Ellway, Iyay ustmay aysay ehay ademay ayay otlay ofyay oisenay aboutyay ityay!” Errygay atedhay otay 
ememberray ustjay owhay artledstay eshay adhay eenbay. “Atwhay ademay imhay eavelay osay 
uicklyqay andyay erewhay ashay ehay onegay?” 
 
“Aroundyay otay ethay idesay orchpay, obablypray,” aidsay Ordongay. 
 
Eythay istenedlay andyay eardhay ethay oundsay ofyay anyay openingyay oorday andyay ayay eepday umblemay 
ofyay elcomeway omfray Osaray Eelay. 
 
“Andyay Iyay uessgay ifyay e’shay oughtbray ouryay uggagelay e’dway etterbay etgay ityay insideyay 
eforebay esethay ainray oudsclay urstbay ideway openyay,” addedyay Abbay. 
 
Inyay ontrastcay otay ethay estray ofyay ethay ousehay, ethay itchenkay appearedyay uiteqay 
omelikehay. Ithway ayay ensationsay ofyay oignantpay eliefray, ethay irlsgay oundfay 
emselvesthay onceyay oremay inyay ethay osaicpray, atter-of-factmay ompanycay ofyay Osaray Eelay. 
 
Mrsay. Enwickfay asway elpinghay inyay ethay itchenkay, oo--attay eastlay, eshay asway 
etendingpray otay elphay. Utbay Osaray Eelay idday allyay ethay actualyay orkway. 
 
Ethsay Iggleyway adhay oughtbray eirthay unkstray andyay ovisionspray omfray ethay illagevay 
andyay Ordongay adhay alreadyyay ollowedfay imhay outyay otay ethay agonway. 
 
Arliechay Eymoursay oodstay owlingscay atherray unpleasantlyyay inyay ethay oorwayday. 
 
“At’swhay ethay attermay, Arliechay? Orldway eatingtray youyay oughray again--oryay isyay ityay 
ustjay Ordongay?” 
 
Incesay isthay ippantflay emarkray amecay omfray ethay ever-flippantyay Errygay, Arliechay 
osechay otay ignoreyay ityay. Utbay ethay ownfray eepenedday onyay ishay owbray andyay ehay ovedmay 
impatientlyyay. 
 
Ordongay alledcay omfray ethay agonway. 
 
“Endlay ayay andhay erehay, illway youyay, Arliechay? Atwhay oday youyay inkthay youyay are--anyay 
ornamentyay? Akemay yourselfyay usefulyay.” 
 
Arlie’schay owlscay ecamebay ackblay. Ehay esitatedhay orfay ayay omentmay; enthay, 
ustingthray ishay andshay intoyay ishay ocketspay, aunteredsay outyay intoyay ethay ormstay. 
 
“Orfay allyay ethay orldway asyay oughthay ehay ereway oinggay otay ayay ardengay artypay,” uckledchay 
Errygay. “Ehay ivesgay imselfhay ethay airsyay ofyay ayay andgray ukeday.” 
 
“IYAY on’tday eesay whyay ehay amecay ithway usyay,” aidsay Abbay, owingthray erselfhay earilyway 
intoyay ayay airchay. “Isthay isn’tyay ethay indkay ofyay ingthay ehay arescay orfay, eallyray. 
Arliechay ikeslay otay oday otway ings--dancethay andyay ashday aboutyay inyay atthay unnyfay 
ittlelay oadsterray ofyay ishay. E’llhay ebay oredbay otay eathday upyay erehay.” 
 
Errygay avegay Abbay ayay ickedway anceglay. 
 
“Otnay ilewhay Abbay Inters’way eetsway ilesmay andyay unnysay urlscay oldhay outyay otay aveway,” 
eshay uckledchay. “On’tday inkthay I’myay indblay, Ab--norbay Arliechay, eitheryay!” 
 
“On’tday ebay illysay!” iedcray Abbay. 
 
Osaray Eelay uckledchay eepday ownday inyay erhay oatthray. 
 
“Otslay o’yay olksfay oesday ikelay yo’yay urlycay eadhay andyay ightbray eyesyay, oneyhay,” eshay 
aidsay. Eshay electedsay ayay ancay ofyay eansbay omfray ethay ilepay ofyay ovisionspray andyay 
openedyay ityay ithway icenay ecisionpray. “Andyay asyay o’fay atday Arliechay oybay, ikin’lay youyay 
isyay ’bout eday onlyyay ingthay Ah’syay otgay otay ishay editcray. Enwhay ityay omescay otay oin’day 
anythin’yay ealray usefulyay, atday ile’schay estjay aboutyay asyay uchmay accountyay asyay ayay eaflay 
inyay ayay oilerbay actoryfay.” 
 
“Otnay alfhay osay uchmay, Osaray Eelay,” aidsay Errygay, ithway ayay olldray acefay. “Easflay 
inyay ayay oilerbay actoryfay ouldway obablypray op--andhay I’veyay yetyay otay eesay Arliechay 
Eymoursay oday anythingyay alfhay osay activeyay!” 
 
Ayay althay asway utpay otay isthay ippantflay onversationcay byay ethay arrivalyay ofyay ethay oysbay 
andyay Mray. Iggleyway ithway ethay unkstray. Eythay adhay andedlay allyay ethay uggagelay onyay ethay 
idesay orchpay andyay ownay oceededpray otay agdray emthay intoyay ethay itchenkay. 
 
Ethay astlay iecepay adhay andedlay ithway ayay umpthay amidyay ariousvay umblesgray andyay 
omplaintscay omfray ethay earersbay enwhay osethay arkday, iled-uppay assesmay ofyay oudsclay 
openedyay andyay etlay allfay ethay ainray inyay ayay eetingshay orrenttay. 
 
Ethay indway istledwhay ildlyway aboutyay ethay ousehay andyay ashedday ethay ainray inyay 
orrentialtay ustsgay oughthray ethay openyay oorday ofyay ethay itchenkay. 
 
Ordongay otgay ehindbay ethay oorday andyay, Arliechay elpinghay imhay, ushedpay ityay utshay 
againstyay ethay alegay. 
 
Allyay isthay imetay Mray. Iggleyway adhay evidencedyay ayay arkedmay uneasinessyay. Ehay ookedlay 
overyay ishay ouldershay estlesslyray andyay onceyay ehay oppedmay ishay oreheadfay ithway ayay 
edray, olka-dottedpay andkerchiefhay. 
 
Ithway umbledmay anksthay ehay acceptedyay aypay orfay ishay ervicessay andyay odestray iftlysway 
otay ethay oorday, uggingtay atyay ityay otay openyay ityay. 
 
“Utbay youyay areyay otnay oinggay ackbay inyay isthay ormstay!” Abbay otestedpray. “Aitway ayay 
ittlelay, Mray. Iggleyway. Aybemay ethay ainray illway opstay.” 
 
“Yo’-all’syay elcomeway otay ayay itebay ivway usyay,” aidsay Osaray Eelay, everyay ospitablehay. 
“Ityay ain’tyay inegway ebay uchmay, utbay, echsay asyay ’tis, e’sway illin’way otay areshay ityay. 
Awsylay, istenlay atyay atday indway!” Ayay eshfray ustgay adhay irledwhay ildlyway aboutyay ethay 
ousehay. “Youyay ain’tyay ebbernay inegway otay itgay omehay inyay atday ormstay.” 
 
“Ustjay aitway illtay ityay etslay upyay,” Abbay urgedyay againyay. 
 
Ethsay Iggleyway ookshay ishay eadhay. 
 
“Ifyay Iyay owknay anythingyay aboutyay isthay ountrycay,” ehay aidsay, “Isthay ormstay on’tway 
etlay upyay untilyay o-morrowtay orningmay atyay ethay earliestyay. It’syay aptyay otay itgay orseway, 
’stead ofyay etterbay.” 
 
“Ellway, e’veway otgay entyplay ofyay edsbay upstairsyay,” Errygay uggestedsay ightlylay. “Eway 
ouldcay utpay youyay upyay omfortablycay enoughyay overnightyay.” 
 
Ethay oldyay anmay appearedyay unreasonablyyay alarmedyay atyay isthay uggestionsay. Ityay asway asyay 
oughthay ehay earedfay atthay omesay oneyay ightmay aylay andshay onyay imhay andyay useyay orcefay otay 
akemay imhay acceptyay ethay unwelcomeyay invitationyay. Ehay ankedthay emthay indlykay, utbay, 
ithway ankfray eagernessyay otay ebay offyay, erkedjay openyay ethay oorday andyay eppedstay outyay 
uponyay ethay orchpay. 
 
Erethay asway eliefray inyay ethay esturegay ithway ichwhay ehay ushedpay ishay athay ownday otay 
ishay earsyay andyay attledbay ishay ayway againstyay indway andyay ainray otay ethay ejectedday 
orsehay andyay ethay oldyay agonway. 
 
Omfray ethay itchenkay indowway osethay insideyay atchedway imhay eadhay oldyay Etseybay intoyay 
ethay indway andyay ivedray offyay. 
 
Againyay Abbay asway assailedyay byay atthay unhappyyay ensationsay ofyay onelinesslay andyay 
esertionday. Eshay adhay anyay absurdyay esireday otay unray afteryay Ethsay Iggleyway andyay agdray 
imhay ackbay. Ehay asway eirthay oneyay inklay ithway iedtray andyay ustedtray andyay ownknay ingsthay. 
 
Asyay eshay iledsmay atyay ethay ancyfay, Erry’sgay oicevay aidsay inyay erhay earyay: 
 
“Eemedsay inyay ayay igbay urryhay otay ebay offyay, idn’tday ehay? Oneyay ightmay almostyay elievebay 
atthay ouryay oodgay iendfray, Ethsay, oesday otnay ikelay esethay iggingsday, Abbay Intersway.” 
 
“Ityay ouldway eemsay otnay!” Abbay orcedfay ayay ilesmay, enthay urnedtay otay Osaray Eelay andyay 
askedyay atwhay eshay ightmay oday otay elphay. 
 
“IYAY eelfay asyay oughthay Iyay antedway otay etgay ayay adespay andyay igday,” eshay addedyay. “Eatingyay 
eemssay uchsay ayay asteway ofyay imetay.” 
 
“Eakspay orfay yourselfyay, Abbay,” etortedray Ordongay Eymoursay. “Ustjay ownay I’dyay otnay 
indfay ayay iddenhay easuretray alfhay asyay ourishingnay asyay atthay ancay ofyay eansbay Osaray Eelay 
ashay onyay ethay ovestay.” 
 
“Emay, elfmysay,” aidsay Abbay istfullyway, inkingthay ofyay erhay andmothergray andyay 
anddaddygray, “I’dyay aketay ethay easuretray!” 
 
Inyay itespay ofyay everything--oryay erhapspay ecausebay ofyay everythingyay!--the ealmay otay 
ichwhay Osaray Eelay utpay emthay ownday ayay ewfay inutesmay aterlay asway ayay errymay oneyay. Ityay 
asway ayay ombinationcay unchlay andyay uppersay, ethay oldyay omanway explainedyay, andyay osay 
eythay ustmay eatyay enoughyay orfay otway ealsmay. Isthay eythay undoubtedlyyay idday, andyay byay 
ethay agicmay ofyay eirthay avenousray appetitesyay, ethay in-cantay arefay asway ansformedtray 
intoyay ayay eastfay. 
 
Ethay oysbay adhay oundfay ethay oldyay ellway, ayay icturesquepay affairyay inyay ayay ettingsay ofyay 
angledtay eedsway andyay amblesbray. Ordongay asway enthusiasticyay andyay eageryay orfay ethay 
orrowmay enwhay eythay ouldcay exploreyay ethay ountrycay aboutyay ethay oldyay ousehay. 
 
“Eway awsay ethay immerglay ofyay aterway oughthray ethay eestray,” ehay oldtay Abbay. “Ityay 
isn’tyay uchmay oremay anthay ayay ookbray, Iyay uessgay; utbay atyay atthay eway oughtyay otay indfay ayay 
immingsway olehay andyay avehay omesay unfay.” 
 
“Erhapspay eway ancay atchcay ishfay, ootay,” uggestedsay Errygay. “Ethay ossibilitiespay 
ofyay youryay ancestralyay estateyay owgray apaceyay, Abbay. E’llway ebay indingfay ayay erracetay 
extnay, oryay ayay unkensay ardengay. Evenyay ifyay ethay easuretray unthay ailsfay,” eachingray 
orfay ayay ollray, “IYAY ancay eesay erewhay ouryay ummersay isn’tyay entirelyyay astedway.” 
 
Ethay ayetygay astedlay oughoutthray ethay earingclay awayyay ofyay ethay ishesday andyay 
afterwardyay, enwhay eythay atheredgay aroundyay ethay itchenkay abletay andyay oldtay oriesstay 
andyay aylygay annedplay ethay etailsday ofyay ethay easuretray unthay. 
 
Utbay enwhay ethay imetay amecay atyay astlay enwhay eythay ustmay acefay ethay adowsshay ofyay osethay 
upperyay ooms--wellray, atthay asway ifferentday! 
 
Armedyay againstyay ethay arknessday ithway onlyyay otway imday oilyay ampslay, eythay ustmay akemay 
eirthay eparationspray orfay ethay ightnay. Ethay unkstray ereway openedyay andyay eddingbay 
enoughyay akentay omfray emthay otay ervesay eirthay urposepay. 
 
Enthay, ethay oysbay arryingcay ethay eddingbay; ethay irlsgay, ethay ampslay; andyay Mrsay. 
Enwickfay andyay Osaray Eelay, emselvesthay; eythay ascendedyay otay ethay upperyay orystay. 
 
Afteryay ayay eatgray ealday ofyay ussingfay andyay ervousnay igglinggay, ettinggay eetsshay onyay 
ackwardsbay andyay otway illowpay asescay onyay oneyay illowpay, eythay oonsay adhay enoughyay 
edsbay ademay upyay otay ervesay emthay omfortablycay orfay ethay ightnay. 
 
Afteryay atthay air-raisinghay occurrenceyay inyay ethay ibrarylay, Abbay andyay Errygay ereway 
eryvay adglay otay eepslay ogethertay. 
 
“E’llway aketay oneyay ofyay ethay allersmay ackbay oomsray,” Errygay ecidedday. “Ityay ashay ayay 
igbay edbay andyay, omesay ayway, Iyay on’tday ikelay ethay argelay oomsray osay ellway.” 
 
Osaray Eelay eclaredday uncompromisinglyyay orfay ethay ittlelay oomray ithway ethay inglesay 
edbay. 
 
Mrsay. Enwickfay appearedyay otay avehay onay ualmsqay aboutyay akingtay oneyay ofyay ethay argelay 
ontfray oomsray. Ethay oysbay ooktay ethay intway otay isthay, ayingsay atthay ityay ookedlay 
aboutyay asyay omfortablecay andyay ozycay asyay ayay arnbay. 
 
Asyay ifyay anyyay ofyay osethay emory-hauntedmay oomsray ouldcay ebay ozycay! 
 
Abbay iveredshay andyay onderedway againyay ichwhay oomray adhay elongedbay otay erhay Uncleyay 
Eremiahjay. Utbay evenyay asyay eshay onderedway, ethay irlgay asway onsciouscay ofyay ayay eelingfay 
ofyay isloyaltyday. Oorpay oldyay Uncleyay Erryjay! Whyay, ehay ouldway otnay urthay erhay, ifyay ehay 
ouldcay! 
 
Everthelessnay, eshay asway otnay anxiousyay otay ecallray ethay ueerqay appeningshay ofyay 
ethay ay--notday inyay esethay urroundingssay. Ethsay Iggley’sway arningway otay erhay, ethay 
eirdway experienceyay inyay ethay ibrarylay, ethay oldyay ountry-man’scay eagernessyay otay etgay 
awayyay omfray ethay ousehay, evenyay oughthay ishay escapeyay ustmay ebay ademay intoyay ethay eethtay 
ofyay ayay ormstay! 
 
Enthay amecay ethay oughtthay ofyay erhay andmothergray andyay anddaddygray, andyay onceyay oremay 
eshay asway illedfay ithway ethay iercefay eterminationday otay onquercay ethay oldyay ousehay. 
Ifyay ityay eldhay ayay ecretsay, eshay ouldway iscoverday ityay! 
 
Utbay ethay ightnay asway onglay andyay orm-riddenstay, andyay oughthay Errygay eptslay 
eadilystay andyay acidlyplay, erethay ereway ourshay enwhay Abbay Inters’way eyesyay aredstay 
ideway andyay ightenedfray intoyay ethay arkday. 
 
Asway eshay istakenmay, oryay idday eshay earhay, onceyay oryay icetway oughthray atthay arknessday, 
ethay eerieyay atteringpay ofyay eetfay? 
 
 
 
 
APTERCHAY IVXAY 
 
ORDON’SGAY ISCOVERYDAY 
 
 
Ethay unsay asway eamingstray adiantlyray inyay atyay Abbay Inters’way indowway enwhay eshay 
awokeyay. Allyay erhay earsfay ofyay ethay ightnay eforebay adhay anishedvay intoyay ayay aguevay andyay 
unrealyay istmay. 
 
Ithway ayay ubblingbay ensesay ofyay oyjay inyay ifelay andyay ethay ospectpray ofyay adventureyay, eshay 
ippedslay oiselesslynay outyay ofyay edbay andyay entway overyay otay ethay indowway. 
 
Aboutyay erhay eadspray ayay eamingglay, ain-washedray orldway, eestray andyay ubsshray andyay 
angledtay eedsway eflectingray ackbay ethay aysray ofyay ethay unsay inyay iadmyray azzlingday 
aysray ofyay olorcay. 
 
Ethay oistmay, eet-scentedsway eathbray ofyay ethay indway annedfay erhay eekschay andyay 
oughtbray ethay osesray owingglay otay emthay. 
 
Ingsthay ereway oinggay otay appenhay o-daytay, eshay eltfay it--wonderfulyay, endidsplay 
ingsthay! 
 
Ethay irstfay ofyay emthay asway Ordongay Eymoursay. Eshay awsay imhay ustjay elowbay erhay 
indowway. Ehay asway adclay inyay akikhay eechesbray andyay utteespay, andyay ayay arletscay 
eatersway atopyay isthay outfityay avegay ayay areflay ofyay olorcay atthay, inyay omesay 
eriousmystay ayway, addedyay otay ethay oyjay ofyay Arbara’sbay oodmay. 
 
Eyesyay ancingday, eshay eanedlay omfray ethay indowway andyay alledcay otay imhay oftlysay. 
 
Ishay oodmay eemedsay otay atchmay erhay ownyay andyay ehay ookedlay upyay uicklyqay, eckoningbay otay 
erhay. 
 
“E’veway ethay orldway otay ourselvesyay,” ehay alledcay oftlysay. “IYAY avehay omethingsay otay 
owshay youyay.” 
 
“Ownday inyay ayay inutemay!” Abbay avedway andyay isappearedday. 
 
Ityay asway allyay eshay ouldcay oday otay eepkay omfray ingingsay asyay eshay umpedjay astilyhay intoyay 
erhay othes--sturdyclay, ow-heeledlay ortspay oesshay, akikhay irtskay, itewhay iddymay 
andyay uffyflay itewhay eatersway. Eshay esitatedhay ayay inutemay andyay enthay, asyay anyay impishyay 
afterthoughtyay, addedyay ayay iderway arletscay ietay. Ityay avegay erhay ayay akishray, auntyjay 
ooklay atthay ausedcay erhay otay ucklechay oftlysay underyay erhay eathbray. 
 
“I’myay ealingstay Erry’sgay underthay,” eshay oldtay erhay adiantray eflectionray. “Eshay 
alwaysyay ookslay ikelay ayay aughtynay ittlelay gypsyay inyay edray.” 
 
Oneyay anceglay atyay ethay edbay otay akemay uresay atthay Errygay asway illstay asleepyay, andyay Abbay 
asway outyay ethay oorday andyay ingflyay ightfootedlylay ownday ethay airsstay. 
 
Onay oneyay eardhay erhay, andyay ethay extnay omentmay eshay oodstay oisedpay inyay ethay oorwayday, 
egardingray Ordongay ithway ancingday eyesyay. 
 
Ethay oybay amecay owardtay erhay ithway andshay outstretchedyay, unstintedyay admirationyay 
inyay ishay eyesyay. Ab’sbay ightbray olorcay ecamebay ayay ittlelay ighterbray andyay erhay eyesyay 
ellfay otay ethay aygay uehay ofyay ishay eatersway. 
 
“Youyay ookedlay osay ortsay ofyay ivolousfray,” eshay uckledchay, “Atthay Iyay oughtthay I’dyay 
utpay onyay omethingsay otay atchmay.” 
 
“Ellway, ifyay youyay ewknay owhay _you_ ooklay!” 
 
“Ohyay, ityay oesn’tday attermay owhay Iyay ooklay, Onday. It’syay owhay Iyay eelfay atthay ountscay.” 
 
Ithway ayay ittlelay, unrestrainedyay esturegay eshay ungflay outyay erhay armsyay otay ethay ildway 
eautybay ofyay ethay oodlandway aboutyay emthay. 
 
“I’myay oinggay otay akemay eachyay ayday elltay ilewhay e’reway upyay erehay, Ordongay. Andyay owhay 
owsknay atwhay ay--”day Eshay ausedpay onyay ayay ong-drawnlay eathbray andyay aredstay aightstray 
eforebay erhay, eeingsay, otnay ethay immediateyay uturefay, utbay omesay inneryay isionvay ofyay 
erhay ownyay. 
 
Ethay oybay, atchingway erhay intentlyyay, ooktay ayay epstay oserclay. 
 
“Youyay ean--themay oneymay, Abbay?” 
 
“Ethay illway, atthay ueerqay odicil--thecay ossibilitypay ofyay indingfay ayay ortunefay 
erehay inyay isthay ueerqay, erribletay, oldyay ousehay. Ofyay oursecay I’myay inkingthay ofyay ityay! 
Owhay ouldcay Iyay inkthay ofyay anythingyay elseyay? Owhay ouldcay Iyay?” 
 
Ordongay avegay ethay irlgay ayay eenkay ooklay, enthay ewdray erhay andhay, ig-brotherbay 
ashionfay, oughthray ishay armyay. Ab’sbay olorcay asway almostyay ootay ighhay, ehay oughtthay, 
erhay eyesyay ayay ifletray ootay ightbray. 
 
“You’reyay oinggay otay inkthay ofyay omethingsay elseyay, ustjay ethay ame--atsay eastlay untilyay 
it’syay imetay orfay eakfastbray,” ehay oldtay erhay asyay ehay edlay erhay alongyay anyay almostyay 
invisibleyay athpay upyay ethay illsidehay andyay intoyay ethay oodsway. 
 
“Utbay erewhay areyay eway oinggay?” askedyay Abbay, ubmittingsay illinglyway enoughyay. 
 
Ityay asway icenay otay ebay aloneyay ithway ethay oybay extnay oorday inyay atthay earlyyay orningmay 
orldway ofyay eetsway entsscay andyay ainbowray ueshay. Ethay aysday ofyay eirthay ildhoodchay 
isputesday eemedsay arfay inyay ethay astpay. Eythay understoodyay eachyay otheryay osay ellway 
esethay aysday, Abbay andyay ethay oybay extnay oorday, atthay erethay asway eldomsay eednay ofyay 
explanationsyay etweenbay emthay. Eirthay omradeshipcay asway ayay eryvay ompletecay andyay 
atisfactorysay ingthay. 
 
“I’myay akingtay youyay otay myay iscoveryday,” aidsay ethay oybay, inyay answeryay otay erhay 
uestionqay. “Onceyay you’veyay eensay ityay I’myay uchmay istakenmay ifyay Iyay everyay etgay youyay ackbay 
otay ethay ousehay inyay imetay orfay eakfastbray.” 
 
“Youryay iscoveryday illway avehay otay ebay ettypray onderfulway enthay,” Abbay arnedway imhay.
