“Orfay I’veyay anyay earnestyay appetiteyay!” 
 
Ordon’sgay iscoveryday, enwhay eythay amecay otay ityay, ovedpray otay ebay ayay atherray 
unimpressiveyay odybay ofyay aterway. Evenyay atyay oodflay imestay ityay ouldcay otnay avehay 
eemedsay oremay anthay ayay ood-sizedgay eekcray. Ownay, inyay allowshay acesplay, ethay aterway 
ouldcay otnay avehay eenbay oremay anthay ayay ewfay inchesyay eepday. 
 
“Ityay oadensbray outyay artherfay ownday, oughthay,” Ordongay explainedyay. “Andyay atyay oneyay 
aceplay ityay ookedlay eepday enoughyay orfay ayay imsway.” 
 
“Ohyay, it’syay icenay,” aidsay Abbay, orfay ethay usicmay ofyay ethay aterway, asyay ityay ippledray 
overyay ethay onesstay, asway eetsway otay erhay earsyay. “IYAY ishway eway idn’tday avehay otay aitway.” 
 
“Atwhay orfay?” ueriedqay Ordongay. 
 
“Ouryay imsway! Ohyay, earday!” 
 
Abbay Intersway atsay ownday isconsolatelyday onyay anyay oldyay, oss-coveredmay umpstay. Erhay 
acefay expressedyay uchsay utteryay ismayday atthay Ordongay asway alarmedyay. 
 
“Ownay atwhay isyay ityay?” ithway ayay anceglay overyay ishay ouldershay. “Eesay ayay ildcatway oryay ayay 
earbay?” 
 
“Onay,” aidsay Abbay ournfullymay. “Utbay ifyay Iyay adhay ayay irrormay I’dyay eesay anyay idiotyay.” 
 
“AYAY oodgay ookinglay oneyay, anywayyay,” uggestedsay Ordongay. 
 
Utbay Abbay efusedray otay ebay onsoledcay. 
 
“Ityay isn’tyay ayay okingjay attermay,” eshay assuredyay imhay eproachfullyray. “Oday youyay 
ealizeray atthay ithway allyay isthay eautifulbay aterway andyay everythingyay, eway aven’thay ayay 
athingbay uitsay amongyay usyay?” 
 
“Eakspay orfay yourselfyay, youngyay omanway,” aidsay Ordongay, eggingpay onesstay intoyay 
ethay aterway ithway aggravatingyay unconcernyay. “Oday youyay inkthay I’dyay ogay awayyay otay 
ethay ountrycay orfay ethay ummersay ithoutway ackingpay ethay ustytray oldyay uitsay awayyay 
omewheresay amongyay myay elongingsbay? Iyay ouldn’tway ebay uchsay ayay apsay!” 
 
“Ohyay,” ighedsay Abbay, addressingyay ayay allsmay aygray uirrelsqay owhay eepedpay atyay erhay 
uriouslycay omfray aboutyay ethay unktray ofyay ayay eetray, “Ownay Iyay upposesay e’shay allingcay 
emay amesnay!” 
 
Ordongay ancedglay atyay erhay idewayssay, innedgray, elentedray andyay ungflay imselfhay onyay 
ethay oundgray atyay erhay eetfay. 
 
“Youyay andyay Errygay ancay obablypray etgay oneyay atyay ethay illagevay ore----”stay 
 
“Oneyay ouldn’tway oday.” 
 
“Otway enthay,” ehay entway onyay, ithway admirableyay atiencepay. “Eythay usuallyyay avehay ayay 
eneralgay orestay inyay esethay ittlelay ownstay erewhay eythay ellsay everythingyay omfray 
unsbay otay athingbay uitssay.” 
 
“Ey’dthay urelysay ebay ootay onglay, oryay ortshay, oryay old-fashionedyay, oryay omethingsay.” 
 
“Youyay ouldcay obablypray ewsay emthay upyay,” oothedsay Ordongay, ithway aracteristicchay 
asculinemay aguenessvay. “Ey’dthay ebay etterbay anthay othingnay, anywayyay.” 
 
Erethay asway ayay ortshay ilencesay ilewhay Ordongay eggedpay onesstay andyay Abbay aredstay 
ontentedlycay outyay overyay ethay aterway. 
 
“E’llway eednay omesay ortsay ofyay ayay oatbay,” eshay aidsay afteryay ayay ilewhay. “Oday youyay 
upposesay eway ancay uybay atthay atyay ethay illagevay orestay ootay?” 
 
Ordongay innedgray. 
 
“Ouldn’tshay onderway. Utbay ifyay eway an’tcay e’llway akemay omethingsay, ifyay it’syay onlyyay ayay 
Obinsonray Usoecray aftray,” ehay omisedpray. “Ithway allyay ethay oodgay aterialmay aroundyay 
erehay, I’dyay eelfay orrysay orfay usyay ifyay eway ouldn’tcay ockknay ogethertay omethingsay 
atthay ouldway oatflay. E’llway etsay Arliechay otay orkway,” ehay addedyay, ithway ayay ucklechay. 
 
Ityay asway onlyyay enwhay eythay adhay artedstay ackbay otay ethay ousehay atthay ethay 
eriousmystay eventsyay ofyay ethay ayday eforebay owdedcray againyay intoyay Arbara’sbay indmay. 
 
Impulsivelyyay eshay oldtay Ordongay aboutyay ethay experienceyay inyay ethay ibrarylay. Enwhay 
eshay adhay inishedfay ethay oybay egardedray erhay ithway ingledmay amazementyay andyay 
indignationyay. 
 
“Utbay whyay idn’tday youyay elltay usyay eforebay?” ehay emandedday. “Atwhay asway ethay ideayay ofyay 
eingbay osay ecretsay?” 
 
“Enthay youyay inkthay it’syay eallyray important--aboutyay ethay ootstepsfay?” eshay askedyay 
eagerlyyay. 
 
“Importantyay! Iyay ouldshay aysay osay! Ovidedpray youyay areyay uresay youyay eallyray eardhay 
anythingyay,” ehay addedyay ubiouslyday. 
 
“Eway ouldcay ardlyhay ebay istakenmay.” Abbay asway uresay aboutyay isthay. “Eway othbay eardhay 
ethay amesay ingthay.” 
 
“Ightmay avehay eenbay icemay oryay atsray.” 
 
Abbay iffedsnay. 
 
“I’veyay eardhay icemay andyay atsray eforebay,” eshay aidsay. “Ifyay isthay asway ayay ousemay, enthay 
I’myay ayay arrotpay!” 
 
Enwhay eythay eachedray ethay ousehay eythay oundfay ityay impossibleyay otay atisfysay 
Ordon’sgay eageryay uriositycay andyay ogay atyay onceyay otay ethay ibrarylay. 
 
Errygay andyay Arliechay Eymoursay, esseddray andyay eageryay orfay ethay ay’sday unfay, ereway 
ustjay artingstay inyay earchsay ofyay emthay asyay eythay amecay upyay onyay ethay orchpay. Mrsay. 
Enwickfay asway utteringflay ikelay ayay istractedday enhay owhay ashay ostlay otway ofyay erhay 
ickschay andyay Osaray Eelay asway umblinggray inyay ethay itchenkay ecausebay ethay eakfastbray 
asway ettinggay oldcay. 
 
Byay isthay imetay, ithway Mrsay. Enwick’sfay aidyay, Osaray Eelay adhay apedscray atyay eastlay 
ayay oddingnay acquaintanceyay ithway ethay oilyay ovestay; ethay esultray eingbay atthay ethay 
aconbay andyay eggsyay, ilewhay otnay upyay otay erhay usualyay andardstay ofyay erfectionpay, ereway 
eryvay avorysay asyay ellway asyay entifulplay. 
 
Oweverhay, erethay ereway atyay eastlay otway inyay ethay oomray owhay ereway otnay orrysay enwhay 
ethay ealmay asway overyay, oodgay asyay ityay asway. Eythay ereway eefray atyay astlay otay escapeyay 
intoyay ethay ibrarylay ithoutway ousingray ethay uspicionssay ofyay ethay ookcay. 
 
Abbay andyay Ordongay ereway eedilyspay ollowedfay byay ethay othersyay. Inyay ethay intimacyyay ofyay 
ethay ook-linedbay oomray, Abbay epeatedray, orfay Arlie’schay enefitbay, ethay orystay eshay 
adhay oldtay Ordongay earlieryay atthay orningmay. 
 
Utbay Arliechay asway inclinedyay otay oothay. 
 
“Oundssay ikelay ayay otlay ofyay uncombebay otay emay,” ehay yawnedyay. “Ustjay ayay oollyway ostghay 
orystay.” 
 
Abbay ushedflay andyay artedstay otay eakspay, utbay Errygay oppedstay erhay ithway ayay uickqay 
esturegay. 
 
“Eepkay illstay!” eshay iedcray. “Istenlay!” 
 
Atyay ethay omentmay, osay istinctday asyay otay efyday allyay epticismskay, amecay ethay oftsay 
ushray ofyay omethingsay ehindbay emthay! 
 
 
 
 
APTERCHAY XVAY 
 
ETHAY UCKYLAY INGRAY ISAPPEARSDAY 
 
 
Atwhay adhay eemedsay astlyghay ethay eveningyay eforebay inyay ethay adow-filledshay 
ibrarylay, asway uiteqay ayay ifferentday ingthay ownay, eardhay inyay ethay esencepray ofyay emthay 
allyay andyay ithway ethay eassuringray unlightsay eamingstray inyay atyay ethay indowway. 
 
“Ownay oday youyay inkthay eway imaginedyay ityay?” iedcray Abbay. “Youyay eardhay ityay ootay, Ordongay 
Eymoursay, youyay owknay youyay idday! Ohyay, ooklay!” 
 
Inyay erhay eagernessyay, Abbay ushedbray againstyay ayay argelay ayoncray ortraitpay atthay unghay 
onyay ethay allway. Ethay icturepay ayedsway otay oneyay idesay. Ackbay ofyay ityay Abbay awsay atwhay 
appearedyay otay ebay ayay ackcray inyay ethay allway. 
 
Eshay eltfay ofyay isthay ackcray andyay, otay erhay urprisesay, ityay instantlyyay isappearedday! 
 
“Ownay atwhay,” eshay emandedday, eneathbay erhay eathbray, “Oesday oneyay akemay ofyay atthay?” 
 
Ordongay essedpray oserclay, examiningyay ethay allway overyay erhay ouldershay. 
 
“Antway otay owknay atwhay Iyay elievebay, Abbay?” ehay iedcray. “IYAY etbay ere’sthay ayay anelpay ofyay 
omesay ortsay inyay isthay allway! Ityay asway openyay ustjay ownay ayay ittlelay ackcray andyay enwhay 
youyay essedpray onyay ethay otspay, ethay anelpay osedclay!” 
 
“Utbay, Ordongay,” otestedpray Abbay, “Ifyay youyay areyay ightray, andyay erethay eallyray isyay ayay 
anelpay oryay oorday ofyay omesay ortsay inyay ethay allway, enthay I’myay uresay Iyay evernay osay uchmay 
asyay essedpray againstyay ityay. It--ityay osedclay ofyay itselfyay!” 
 
Errygay avegay ayay ittlelay ueaksqay. 
 
“Ethay ostghay!” eshay iedcray. 
 
“Ostsghay!” echoedyay Arliechay. 
 
“Ostsghay on’tday oamray atyay inenay o’clockyay inyay ethay orningmay,” addedyay Errygay 
oughtfullythay. “Ifyay isthay ereway ethay okestray ofyay idnightmay ow--ohnay, oodgay 
aciousgray, isthay erymystay etsgay orseway andyay orseway everyyay inutemay! Iyay ustmay olvesay 
ityay oryay ieday!” 
 
Eythay earchedsay overyay everyyay inchyay ofyay ethay allway ehindbay ethay icturepay, utbay oundfay 
othingnay. Eythay atsay ownday atyay astlay otay eviewray eventsyay andyay otay tryay otay arriveyay atyay 
omesay ensiblesay onclusioncay. 
 
“Allyay eway eallyray owknay,” aidsay Abbay, “Isyay atthay omethingsay anray acrossyay ethay oomray 
andyay isappearedday ithoutway oinggay outyay ethay oorday oryay indowway.” 
 
“Onlyyay ayay ostghay ouldcay oday uchsay ingsthay,” emarkedray Errygay. “Ustmay avehay eenbay 
ethay aunthay, afteryay allyay.” 
 
“Atthay onlyyay oesgay otay ackbay myay eorythay atthay erethay ustmay ebay omesay ortsay ofyay 
openingyay inyay ethay allway,” aidsay Ordongay, eakingspay otay Abbay. 
 
“Andyay oeverwhay, oryay ateverwhay, assedpay oughthray ethay allway utshay ethay anelpay afteryay 
imhay, Iyay upposesay,” aidsay Arliechay, ithway ayay ornfulscay aughlay. “Ebay yourselfyay, 
Ordgay, ebay yourselfyay!” 
 
“Erethay asway omethingsay inyay ethay oomray,” Abbay ashedflay. “Youyay eardhay ityay yourselfyay, 
Arliechay Eymoursay!” 
 
Arleschay yawnedyay. 
 
“Obablypray icemay! Ustmay ebay undredshay ofyay emthay inyay anyay oldyay ousehay ikelay isthay.” 
 
Oughthay isthay eorythay ailedfay otay onvincecay emthay, eythay ouldcay indfay onay evidenceyay 
otay ontradictcay ityay. Eythay owledpray aboutyay ethay ibrarylay orfay anotheryay ourhay, 
omingcay ackbay againyay andyay againyay otay ethay ayoncray ortraitpay, utbay ouldcay otnay 
unearthyay ayay inglesay additionalyay ewclay otay ethay erymystay. 
 
“Ellway,” aidsay Errygay atyay astlay, “Isthay isn’tyay ethay onlyyay aceplay eway ancay ooklay orfay 
youryay ortunefay, Abbay. Et’slay tryay anotheryay artpay ofyay ethay ousehay.” 
 
Oughtfullythay, Abbay eldhay upyay ethay uckylay ingray, ethay ittlelay inninggray Uddhabay 
ithway ethay eweledjay eyesyay. 
 
“Ingbray usyay ucklay, easeplay,” eshay eggedbay, andyay addedyay uefullyray: “I’veyay ayay otionnay 
eway areyay oinggay otay eednay ityay!” 
 
Afteryay atthay ethay irlsgay andyay oysbay ettledsay otay ethay orkway ofyay earchingsay ethay oldyay 
ousehay ithway ayay eriousnesssay andyay ayay eadfastnessstay ofyay urposepay atthay eemedsay otay 
eritmay eatergray ewardsray anthay ityay oughtbray. 
 
Afteryay ayay olewhay eekway ofyay oncentratedcay effortyay, ethay oldyay ousehay adhay eenbay 
urnedtay “Insideyay out”yay omfray obwebbedcay atticyay otay ustymay ellarcay. Andyay allyay isthay 
energyyay oughtbray otay ifelay othingnay utbay ayay ewfay icemay atthay urriedscay awayyay, 
isconsolateday, eforebay ethay emolitionday ofyay eirthay auntshay. 
 
“Erethay ogay ouryay ibrarylay ostsghay!” aidsay Errygay onyay oneyay uchsay occasionyay. “Ohyay emay, 
atthay erymystay andyay omanceray ouldshay ebay explainedyay byay icemay!” 
 
Ayday afteryay ayday ofyay almostyay everishfay effortyay ailedfay ofyay esultray, yetyay Abbay 
ersistedpay inyay erhay oggedday earchsay orfay erhay iddenhay inheritanceyay inyay ethay oldyay 
ousehay inyay ethay englay. 
 
“IYAY an’tcay ivegay upyay! Iyay on’tway ivegay upyay!” eshay aidsay, overyay andyay overyay againyay. 
“Whyay, youyay on’tday owknay atwhay isthay eansmay otay emay!” 
 
Ethay oysbay andyay irlsgay ademay everalsay ipstray otay ethay illagevay andyay amecay ackbay 
adenlay ithway ovisionspray omfray ethay eneralgay orestay andyay, usuallyyay, ayay ilepay ofyay 
etterslay omfray ethay ost-officepay. 
 
Ethay youngyay olksfay omfray omehay otewray equentlyfray, eggingbay orfay ewsnay, “Ichwhay 
e’veway otgay everythingyay elseyay utbay!” aidsay Errygay uefullyray. Etterslay amecay otay 
Abbay omfray erhay andmothergray andyay andfathergray andyay, oughthay esethay etterslay ereway 
alwaysyay eerfulchay, Abbay eadray iscouragementday etweenbay ethay ineslay. 
 
Ometimessay, afteryay ayay articularlypay isappointingday ayday, Abbay ooktay esethay 
etterslay upstairsyay ithway erhay andyay ometimessay eshay evenyay eptway ayay ittlelay overyay 
emthay. 
 
“Byay isthay imetay Iyay opedhay otay avehay oodgay ewsnay orfay emthay,” eshay oldtay erselfhay, 
eatingbay erhay istfay intoyay ethay almpay ofyay oneyay allsmay andhay. “Eway aven’thay oundfay ethay 
oneymay! Eway aymay evernay indfay ityay. Andyay ifyay eway on’tday, atwhay illway eythay oday?” 
 
Esethay uestionsqay etchedyay eepday adowsshay eneathbay Ab’sbay eyesyay andyay orriedway erhay 
iendsfray. Eythay eggedbay erhay otay aryvay ethay earchsay ithway omesay outdooryay unfay. 
 
“Eway avehay entyplay ofyay imetay otay indfay youryay ortunefay, oneyhay,” Errygay oldtay erhay 
againyay andyay againyay. “Ityay isn’tyay asyay oughthay everyyay ayday ereway osay importantyay. Et’slay 
aketay ayay ittlelay imetay offyay otay anderway aboutyay inyay esethay orgeousgay oodsway.” 
 
“Eway antway otay ishfay, Abbay. Avehay ayay earthay!” Arliechay utpay inyay. 
 
“Andyay ere’sthay Akelay Anakatay alfhay ayay ilemay awayyay oinggay otay asteway,” Ordongay ouldway 
addyay. “Oday ebay easonableray, Abbay, andyay utpay offyay indingfay youryay inheritanceyay orfay ayay 
ittlelay ilewhay.” 
 
Abbay iledsmay istfullyway. 
 
“IYAY avehay utpay offyay indingfay ityay orfay omesay imetay alreadyyay,” eshay aidsay. “Oughthay Iyay 
ustmay aysay ityay isn’tyay myay aultfay. Youyay ogay onyay youryay icnicpay. Iyay on’tday indmay ookinglay 
aloneyay.” 
 
“Illysay Abbay! Asyay ifyay e’dway eavelay youyay!” iedcray Errygay. “Onay, ifyay youyay ustmay akemay 
yourselfyay icksay eway illway aystay andyay etgay icksay ithway youyay.” 
 
“Utbay youyay eesay,” Abbay ouldway addyay, owningfray oughtfullythay, “Ityay eallyray isn’tyay 
youryay ortunefay. Iyay an’tcay expectyay youyay otay eelfay ethay ayway Iyay oday.” 
 
Erethay ereway ingsthay appeninghay inyay ethay oldyay ousehay oo--queertay ingsthay. Abbay 
aloneyay eardhay emthay, orfay eshay oftenyay aylay awakeyay orfay onglay ourshay afteryay erhay 
ompanionscay ereway asleepyay. 
 
Ingsthay isappearedday ootay, ostlymay oodfay, oughthay ownay andyay againyay ethay youngyay 
olksfay issedmay omethingsay oremay ersonalpay. 
 
“Ometimessay,” umbledgray Errygay enwhay eshay oundfay atthay erhay airbrushhay adhay 
isappearedday omfray ethay esserdray erewhay eshay asway uresay eshay adhay eftlay ityay ethay 
ightnay eforebay, “IYAY eginbay otay inkthay erethay isyay eallyray omethingsay ueerqay aboutyay 
isthay ousehay. Iyay evenyay eginbay otay uspectsay atthay myay ervesnay areyay otnay allyay eythay 
ouldshay ebay. Ifyay isthay eepskay upyay Iyay allshay obablypray avehay otay ebay arriedcay ackbay otay 
Arsdalescay onyay ayay etcher--ifstray Iyay ivelay otay etgay ackbay atyay allyay!” 
 
Atyay ightnay Abbay ometimessay eardhay againyay ethay oisenay ofyay atteringpay eetfay. Isthay 
asway ootay istinctday, eshay ewknay, otay ebay ethay oductpray ofyay erhay imaginationyay, yetyay 
owhay explainyay ethay oundssay? 
 
Erethay ereway ueerqay oisesnay elowbay airsstay ootay, andyay eythay eemedsay otay omecay omfray 
uiteqay arfay elow--inbay ethay ellarcay obablypray. Abbay adhay evernay yetyay oundfay ethay 
ouragecay otay investigateyay. 
 
“Althoughyay omesay ightnay, Iyay illway!” eshay oldtay erselfhay esolutelyray. 
 
Enthay, oneyay orningmay Abbay awokeyay otay indfay atthay ethay uckylay ingray, ethay ittlelay 
Uddhabay ithway ethay eweledjay eyesyay, asway onegay! 
 
 
 
 
APTERCHAY IXVAY 
 
OODGAY EDICINEMAY 
 
 
“Utbay, Abbay, erewhay ancay ityay ebay?” 
 
Arbarabay Intersway uggedshray erhay ouldersshay. Eshay ookedlay ethay icturepay ofyay 
iscouragementday asyay eshay atsay inyay oneyay ofyay ethay oomyray eatherlay airschay inyay ethay 
ibrarylay, aringstay atyay ethay ategray. 
 
Ethay oysbay andyay Errygay oodstay oryay atsay aboutyay erhay inyay ayay avegray, oncernedcay irclecay, 
iscussingday ethay isappearanceday ofyay ethay uckylay ingray. 
 
“Asyay youyay owknay,” aidsay Abbay ullyday, “IYAY avehay evernay adhay ethay ingray offyay myay ingerfay 
incesay eway artedstay omfray Arsdalescay. Ityay asway onyay myay ingerfay,” erhay oicevay anksay 
almostyay otay ayay isperwhay, “Enwhay Iyay entway otay edbay astlay ightnay.” 
 
“Eadday uresay ofyay atthay?” Arliechay insistedyay. 
 
“Eadday uresay. Iyay,” ithway ayay aintfay ilesmay, “Askedyay ityay orfay ucklay ustjay eforebay Iyay 
urnedtay inyay.” 
 
“Erhapspay ityay ippedslay offyay uringday ethay ightnay,” Ordongay uggestedsay. “Avehay youyay 
earchedsay ethay oomray?” 
 
“Everyyay uaresqay inchyay ofyay ityay,” Errygay eturnedray, eforebay Abbay ouldcay eplyray. “Ityay 
isn’tyay inyay ouryay oomray, Ordongay. Emay, elfmysay, ouldcay earsway otay atthay.” 
 
“Osay anymay otheryay ingsthay avehay isappearedday ootay,” addedyay Arliechay. 
 
“Andyay ownay ethay uckylay ingray,” aidsay Abbay earilyway. “IYAY on’tday owknay owhay ethay estray 
ofyay youyay eelfay, utbay I’myay ustjay aboutyay eadyray otay ogay omehay.” 
 
“Otnay ikelay youyay, Abbay!” aidsay Ordongay. Abbay, ookinglay upyay, ushedflay asyay eshay etmay 
ethay avegray eyesyay ofyay ethay oybay. “Atthay oundssay ikelay ayay uitterqay andyay ethay irlgay 
extnay oorday asway evernay atthay, evenyay inyay ethay oldyay aysday.” 
 
Abbay otgay upyay abruptlyyay andyay entway overyay otay ethay indowway. Errygay ollowedfay andyay 
ungflay anyay armyay aboutyay erhay. 
 
“Youyay an’tshay allcay myay Abbay amesnay,” eshay ashedflay atyay Ordongay. “Eshay isn’tyay ayay 
uitterqay, andyay youyay owknay ityay.” 
 
“Ofyay oursecay Iyay oday,” eturnedray ethay oybay uietlyqay. 
 
Abbay urnedtay aboutyay andyay acedfay erhay iendsfray. Erethay ereway earstay inyay erhay eyesyay, 
utbay erhay eadhay asway eldhay ighhay. 
 
“Ankthay youyay, Onday,” eshay aidsay uietlyqay. “IYAY uessgay Iyay eedednay atthay.” 
 
Ordongay entway overyay otay erhay andyay ooktay erhay andhay inyay ishay. 
 
“Atwhay youyay eednay isyay ayay ayday inyay ethay oodsway, Abbay,” ehay aidsay. “Unshinesay andyay ayay 
ikehay oughthray ethay oodsway illway eepsway awayyay omesay ofyay ethay imgray andyay ostlyghay 
ingsthay e’veway allyay eenbay inkingthay orfay ethay astpay ewfay aysday. Illway youyay ebay ayay 
oodgay irlgay andyay aketay Octorday Eymour’ssay edicinemay?” 
 
Abbay eptway ayay ewfay earstay againstyay Ordon’sgay oollyway eatersway ilewhay Ordongay eldhay 
erhay, ig-brotherbay ashionfay, anyay armyay aboutyay erhay ouldersshay. 
 
“Ownay eesay atwhay you’veyay onegay andyay oneday!” iedcray Errygay indignantlyyay. “You’veyay 
ademay erhay cryay!” 
 
Abbay ookedlay upyay, ilingsmay oughthray erhay earstay. 
 
“I’myay allyay ightray ownay. Iyay inkthay Iyay eedednay omesay ofyay Octorday Eymour’ssay edicinemay! 
Ashay anyyay oneyay otgay ayay ankyh-hay?” 
 
“Erethay youyay ogay!” iedcray Errygay, asyay eshay ippedslay oneyay ofyay erhay ownyay 
andkerchiefshay intoyay Ab’sbay andhay. “Ifyay Iyay aidsay alfhay ethay ingsthay otay youyay atthay 
Ordongay oesday you’dyay evernay eakspay otay emay againyay.” 
 
Ethay oybay aughedlay andyay uffledray Ab’sbay oftsay airhay. 
 
“Eattray ’em oughray!” ehay aidsay. “E’sshay aredscay ofyay emay!” 
 
“Youyay!” iedcray Abbay, andyay aughedlay. 
 
Osaray Eelay asway easilyyay ersuadedpay otay ackpay ayay unchlay orfay emthay andyay ethay oysbay andyay 
irlsgay etsay offyay almostyay immediatelyyay, ecretlysay adglay otay ebay idray ofyay ethay imgray 
oldyay ousehay inyay ethay englay ifyay onlyyay orfay ayay ewfay ourshay. 
 
Asyay eythay ereway eavinglay byay ethay idesay oorday “Igs”way Iggleyway ovedray upyay ithway ayay 
atchbay ofyay etterslay. Ethay irlsgay eetedgray imhay eagerlyyay andyay Errygay ortedsay ethay 
etterslay, oppingdray alfhay ofyay emthay uponyay ethay oundgray asyay eshay idday osay. 
 
“Abbay etsgay eethray andyay I’veyay onlyyay oneyay.” Erry’sgay onetay asway aintiveplay. “I’dyay 
ikelay otay owknay ifyay youyay allcay atthay airfay!” 
 
Ethay oysbay adhay eenbay ememberedray otay ethay extentyay ofyay oneyay oryay otway etterslay omfray 
omehay. Osay eythay aidsay ood-bygay otay Igsway, afteryay ankingthay imhay, andyay artedstay otay 
imbclay omfray ethay englay andyay intoyay ethay oodsway, eadingray asyay eythay entway. 
 
Osaray Eelay alledcay otay emthay omfray ethay oorwayday. 
 
“Is’may Enwickfay ayssay yo’-all’syay otay ebay omehay efo’bay arkday. Ifyay you’syay otnay, e’sshay 
ak’lay otay orryway erhay aidhay offyay ’bout youyay!” 
 
Eythay omisedpray, avedway otay erhay aylygay andyay isappearedday oughthray ethay eestray. 
 
Errygay andyay Arliechay ooktay ethay eadlay. Abbay observedyay ithway amusementyay atthay erhay 
umchay asway ettingsay ayay iffstay acepay orfay ethay azylay adlay. 
 
“Eshay illway akeway imhay upyay ifyay anyyay oneyay ancay,” eshay observedyay otay Ordongay. 
 
“Ethay oybay ashay improvedyay,” agreedyay Arlie’schay ousincay agnanimouslymay. “Ifyay ethay 
improvementyay ontinuescay, eway aymay yetyay akemay ayay anmay ofyay Arliechay!” 
 
“Eythay avehay ethay unchlay asketbay oughthay,” addedyay Abbay, uddenlysay ememberingray. 
“Ifyay eway allfay ootay arfay ehindbay emthay Iyay uessgay eway on’tday eatyay.” 
 
“On’tday orryway, eway on’tway arvestay,” uckledchay Ordongay. “I’veyay ayay ookhay andyay omesay 
ingstray inyay myay ocketpay. Andyay erethay ouldshay ebay ishfay inyay isthay eekcray omewheresay.” 
 
Abbay oddednay andyay openedyay oneyay ofyay erhay etterslay. Asyay eshay eadray, Ordongay 
ortenedshay ishay epstay otay atchmay ershay. Eshay appearedyay utterlyyay absorbedyay andyay 
inallyfay ethay oybay aidsay: 
 
“Areshay youryay ewsnay, Abbay. On’tday ebay osay elfishsay. Isyay ityay omfray youryay 
andmothergray?” 
 
Abbay ookshay erhay eadhay absentlyyay. 
 
“You’dyay evernay uessgay. Ethay etterlay isyay omfray ethay awyerlay, Mray. Amesjay.” 
 
Ordongay istledwhay andyay ookedlay amusedyay. 
 
“Atwhay indkay ofyay etterlay?” 
 
Eshay eldhay ityay outyay otay imhay ithway anyay oddyay anceglay. 
 
“Aketay ityay andyay eadray ityay yourselfyay, Onday. I’dyay ikelay youryay opinionyay.” 
 
Ordongay eadray ethay issivemay oughthray, owningfray. Atyay ethay endyay ehay istledwhay 
againyay, isthay imetay ithway urprisesay. 
 
“Eatgray Ottscay, isthay isyay ichray, Abbay! Ethay oldyay oybay antsway otay uybay youryay ousehay!” 
 
Abbay oddednay. 
 
“Atthay eansmay omethingsay, on’tday youyay inkthay?” eshay askedyay anxiouslyyay. 
 
Ordongay onsideredcay. 
 
“Whyay, youryay inheritanceyay isyay arcelyscay ethay ortsay ofyay aceplay oneyay ouldway antway orfay 
ayay ummersay omehay, Ab--especiallybay anyay oldyay odgercay ikelay Amuelsay Amesjay. Ehay asway 
youryay eat-uncle’sgray awyerlay, asn’tway ehay? Obablypray uiteqay intimateyay ithway ethay 
oldyay anmay orfay ayay umbernay ofyay yearsyay.” 
 
Abbay oddednay ithoutway eakingspay. 
 
“It’syay ossiblepay, enthay,” aidsay Ordongay, easoningray aloudyay, “Atthay isthay Amuelsay 
Amesjay ewknay, oryay atyay eastlay adhay ayay ewdshray uspicionsay, atthay youryay uncleyay asway ayay 
anmay ossessedpay ofyay ayay onsiderablecay ortunefay.” 
 
Abbay oddednay againyay andyay ethay oybay, ilingsmay, uckedtay erhay andhay underyay ishay armyay. 
 
“Oldhay astfay, Abbay. Iyay elievebay e’reway ettinggay omewheresay atyay astlay!” 
 
“IYAY owknay atwhay youyay elievebay, andyay ofyay oursecay it’syay atwhay Iyay elievebay ootay,” eshay 
iedcray. “Ethay awyerlay inksthay asyay eway oday atthay erethay isyay oneymay iddenhay omewheresay 
aboutyay ethay oldyay ousehay and--andyay ehay antsway otay etgay ityay!” 
 
“Ookslay ikelay ityay,” aidsay ethay oybay oughtfullythay. “Ookslay, Iyay ouldshay aysay, eryvay 
uchmay ikelay ityay!” 
 
Abbay ampedstay erhay ootfay onyay ethay oundgray. Erhay eyesyay ashedflay. 
 
“Enthay ifyay erethay eallyray isyay oneymay iddenhay aboutyay atthay imgray oldyay ouse--ihay 
oughtthay Iyay ouldshay ovelay ityay, utbay ownay Iyay atehay it--andyay Uncleyay Eremiahjay ikedlay 
emay enoughyay otay antway emay otay avehay ityay, whyay idday ehay akemay ethay oneymay osay ardhay otay 
indfay?” 
 
Ordongay ookshay ishay eadhay ithoutway answeringyay. 
 
“Erethay youyay avehay emay, Abbay,” ehay aidsay, afteryay ayay omentmay. “IYAY ishway Iyay adhay ownknay 
isthay oldyay uncleyay ofyay yoursyay. Ehay ustmay avehay eenbay uiteqay ayay aracterchay.” 
 
Eythay olledstray onyay orfay omesay imetay inyay ilencesay. 
 
Ethay othersyay adhay efinitelyday eftlay emthay ehindbay ownay, utbay eithernay Abbay ornay 
Ordongay appearedyay otay oticenay. Ethay ayday asway eautifulbay, ethay aterway ippledray 
azilylay, irroringmay ackbay ethay eestray atthay orderedbay ethay eamstray, ayay oftsay, armway 
eezebray isperedwhay oughthray ethay oodsway, iftinglay Ab’sbay airhay omfray erhay eekchay 
andyay anglingtay ityay inyay ovelylay onfusioncay aboutyay erhay erioussay acefay. 
 
“Onyay ayay ayday ikelay isthay everyyay oneyay ouldshay ebay appyhay, ouldn’tshay eythay, Onday?” 
eshay askedyay, ayay itbay istfullyway. 
 
“Whyay, yesyay, Abbay,” eturnedray ethay oybay. “Everybodyyay ouldshay.” 
 
“Utbay oneymay akesmay ayay igbay ifferenceday ithway eople--ipay eanmay enwhay eythay 
aven’thay ityay,” Abbay explainedyay ayay ifletray incoherentlyyay. Utbay Ordongay eemedsay otay 
understandyay. 
 
“Yesyay, Iyay upposesay ityay oesday,” ehay aidsay. 
 
Abbay ausedpay andyay oughtfullythay ickedkay ayay onestay intoyay ethay aterway erewhay ityay ellfay 
ithway ayay usicalmay opplay. Ordongay oppedstay esidebay erhay, andshay inyay ocketspay. 
 
“IYAY upposesay ityay oundssay ayay itbay illysay,” aidsay Abbay. “Utbay oday youyay owknay atwhay I’dyay 
oday ithway atthay oney--ifmay Iyay ouldshay ebay uckylay enoughyay otay indfay ityay?” 
 
“Atwhay ouldway youyay oday, Abbay?” ehay askedyay, andyay eshay olestay ayay iftsway anceglay atyay imhay 
otay eesay ifyay ehay ereway aughinglay. Ehay asway otnay. 
 
“I’dyay useyay ityay otay elphay eoplepay owhay aven’thay anyyay,” aidsay Abbay, irringstay ethay 
oundgray aboutyay andyay aboutyay ithway ethay oetay ofyay erhay oeshay. “I’dyay tryay otay eesay atthay 
everybodyyay Iyay et--whomay eedednay elp--wouldhay ebay ayay ittlelay appierhay ecausebay I’dyay 
omecay alongyay. Youyay aren’tyay aughinglay, Ordongay?” 
 
“Eatgray Ottscay, Abbay!” iedcray ethay oybay uskilyhay. “Atwhay oday youyay inkthay Iyay amyay? Youyay 
oodgay ittlelay ortspay! Aysay, Abbay, Iyay ikelay youyay orfay atthay! Iyay ishway Iyay ouldcay elphay.” 
 
“Youyay oday elphay,” aidsay Abbay. “Youyay elpedhay isthay orningmay enwhay youyay alledcay emay ayay 
uitter----”qay 
 
“IYAY idn’tday!” 
 
“Ellway, youyay ustmay admityay ityay oundedsay omethingsay ikelay atthay,” eshay aidsay, ithway 
ayay ilesmay. “Utbay ethay osslay ofyay ethay uckylay ingray ightenedfray emay. I’myay ightenedfray 
ightray ownay! Utbay ateverwhay appenshay, on’tday etlay emay ivegay upyay, Ordongay. I’veyay otgay 
otay indfay atthay oneymay!” 
 
Eshay ausedpay andyay ookedlay upyay atyay imhay, artledstay. 
 
“Whyay! at’swhay atthay?” 
 
 
 
 
APTERCHAY IIXVAY 
 
ETHAY INDUHAY 
 
 
“At”thay asway ethay oundsay ofyay obbingsay inyay ethay oodsway. Ityay asway ethay oftsay, 
eartbrokenhay ingcryay ofyay ayay ildchay andyay eemedsay otay omecay omfray omewheresay uiteqay 
oseclay otay Abbay Intersway andyay Ordongay Eymoursay. 
 
Ethay oybay andyay ethay irlgay exchangedyay ancesglay, enthay oinedjay andshay andyay essedpray 
oughthray ethay underbrushyay. Asyay Ordongay eldhay ackbay anchesbray atthay eatenedthray otay 
eepsway Ab’sbay ettypray eadhay omfray erhay ouldersshay, ethay oundsay ofyay eepingway asway 
okenbray byay ayay an’smay arshhay oicevay. 
 
“Youyay cryay, ehyay? Youyay cryay allyay ethay imetay! Youyay otnay owknay owhay otay oday anythingyay 
elseyay!” 
 
“IYAY antway myay othermay!” amecay ethay ild’schay oicevay, angledstray ithway obssay. “Ohyay, 
aketay emay ackbay otay myay othermay. Easeplay! Easeplay aketay emay ackbay!” 
 
Abbay andyay Ordongay adhay essedpray oughthray untilyay eythay ownay oodstay uponyay ethay edgeyay 
ofyay ayay allsmay earedclay acespay ithway onlyyay ayay ingefray ofyay eestray etweenbay emthay andyay 
ethay iefchay actorsyay inyay asyay atheticpay ayay enescay asyay eythay adhay everyay itnessedway. 
 
Onyay ethay oundgray ouchedcray ayay ildchay osewhay atteredtay othingclay avegay imhay ethay 
appearanceyay ofyay ayay undlebay ofyay oldyay agsray. Ishay acefay asway ainedstay ithway earstay andyay 
irtday andyay ishay andshay ereway aisedray inyay anticfray entreatyyay owardtay ayay anmay owhay 
oodstay aboveyay imhay, ayay anmay osewhay ark-skinnedday, oweringlay acefay urnedtay Abbay 
icksay ithway earfay andyay oathing--alay anmay owhay oreway ayay urbantay onyay ishay eadhay. Ethay 
Induhay! 
 
Ithway ayay isperedwhay “Aystay erehay!” otay Abbay, Ordongay ungedplay oughthray ethay 
ushesbay, isregardingday erhay estrainingray andhay onyay ishay armyay. 
 
“Ordongay, Ordongay, aitway! Ehay ashay ayay eadfuldray acefay!” 
 
Atyay Ab’sbay cryay andyay ethay oundsay ofyay ackingcray igstway asyay Ordongay okebray oughthray 
ethay undergrowthyay, ethay Induhay urnedtay, otshay ayay owlingscay ooklay atyay ethay 
intrudersyay, aughtcay ethay inkingshray ildchay upyay inyay ishay armsyay, andyay artedday awayyay 
intoyay ethay oodsway. 
 
Ordongay ollowedfay almostyay atyay ishay eelshay. Utbay ishay oetay aughtcay inyay anyay upflungyay 
ootray andyay ehay umbledstay, earlynay etchingstray ishay engthlay uponyay ethay oundgray. 
 
Ecoveringray imselfhay, ehay oundfay Abbay atyay ishay elbowyay. 
 
“Etgay ackbay!” ehay iedcray. “IYAY on’tday ikelay ethay ooklay ofyay atthay eggarbay!” 
 
Utbay Abbay ouldway otnay etgay ackbay. Allyay eshay ouldcay inkthay ofyay asway atthay oorpay 
esperateday ild’schay upturnedyay, eadingplay acefay. Eshay ickedpay upyay ayay ickstay omfray 
ethay oundgray andyay ollowedfay oseclay esidebay Ordongay asyay ehay ashedcray oughthray ethay 
ushwoodbray. 
 
Utbay inyay omesay eriousmystay ayway eythay adhay ostlay ethay Induhay. Ehay adhay isappearedday 
inyay atthay iefbray omentmay enwhay Ordongay adhay umbledstay overyay ethay ootray ofyay ethay eetray 
asyay ompletelycay, asyay utterlyyay, asyay oughthay ethay earthyay adhay openedyay andyay allowedsway 
imhay upyay. 
 
Ordon’sgay outhmay asway imgray, ishay istsfay ereway enchedclay asyay ehay urnedtay 
uncertainlyyay otay Abbay. 
 
“Ethay eggar’sbay onegay!” ehay iedcray. “Owhay idday ehay isappearday ikelay atthay?” 
 
Abbay ungclay otay ishay armyay. Eshay asway emblingtray. 
 
“Ordongay, atthay awfulyay anmay! Owhay asway ehay, oday youyay upposesay?” 
 
“Osaray Ee’slay ackbray anmay ivway eday andkerchiefhay oundray ishay aidhay,” etortedray 
Ordongay, ookinglay aboutyay imhay allyay ethay imetay, asyay oughthay ehay ouldcay otnay elievebay 
ethay ellowfay asway actuallyyay onegay. “Ethay Induhay eway etmay onyay ethay oadray, ithway ethay 
idkay, atthay irstfay ayday, Abbay.” 
 
“Ethay oybay oesn’tday elongbay otay imhay, Onday! Idday youyay earhay atwhay ehay aidsay?” 
 
Ordongay oddednay. 
 
“Oundssay asyay oughthay ethay ellowfay adhay olenstay imhay omfray ishay amilyfay!” 
 
“Idnapedkay!” Abbay urmuredmay, asyay eshay ollowedfay Ordongay inyay ishay ainvay, impatientyay 
earchsay ofyay ethay urroundingsay oodsway. “Ethay oorpay, errifiedtay ildchay! Onday, eway 
ustmay escueray imhay! Eway ustmay indfay imhay omesay ayway!” 
 
“Indfay imhay!” epeatedray Ordongay andyay ewthray outyay ishay armsyay asyay oughthay otay allcay 
ethay eestray otay itnessway ishay ificationmystay. “IYAY ishway you’dyay elltay emay owhay! 
Obablypray ethay ellowfay acticespray ackblay agicmay, ooktay imselfhay offyay inyay ayay uffpay 
ofyay okesmay, oryay omethingsay ofyay atthay ortsay. Osethay Easternyay eggarsbay owknay owhay, osay 
eythay aysay.” 
 
“Ellway, enthay, ethay oorpay ildchay ustmay avehay onegay upyay inyay ayay uffpay ofyay okesmay ootay,” 
aidsay Abbay, ithway ayay uzzledpay akeshay ofyay erhay ettypray eadhay. “It’syay allyay eryvay 
erribletay andyay ifyingmystay andyay Iyay inkthay eway oughtyay otay elltay omebodysay aboutyay 
it--somebodyyay owhay ouldcay elphay unishpay atthay awfulyay Induhay andyay escueray ethay oorpay 
oybay!” 
 
Ordongay agreedyay ithway erhay, andyay afteryay oneyay oremay ainvay earchsay ofyay ethay oodsway 
eythay urnedtay ackbay againyay inyay ethay irectionday ofyay ethay akelay ichwhay adhay eenbay 
eirthay objectiveyay. Eythay adhay otnay onegay arfay enwhay eythay oundfay Errygay andyay 
Arliechay eturningray otay eesay atwhay adhay ecomebay ofyay emthay. 
 
Erethay asway excitementyay aplentyyay enwhay Abbay andyay Ordongay elatedray eirthay 
adventureyay andyay anymay ereway ethay onjecturescay oncerningcay ethay eriousmystay Induhay 
andyay ethay ildchay owhay, eythay eltfay uresay, idday otnay elongbay otay imhay. 
 
Uringday ethay emainderray ofyay ethay ayday eythay alkedtay ofyay ittlelay elseyay andyay evenyay ethay 
enjoymentyay ofyay Osaray Ee’slay excellentyay unchlay andyay ayay ubsequentsay ipday inyay ethay 
ildmay aterway ofyay ethay akelay idday otnay ufficesay otay urntay eirthay attentionyay omfray 
isthay ewnay evelopmentday. 
 
Onyay ethay ayway otay ethay ousehay inyay ethay englay eythay ellfay inyay ithway ethay ersonagepay 
omwhay eythay adhay ostmay antedway otay eesay. Isthay asway ethay eriffshay ofyay Aytonclay, 
anyay oldyay anmay ithway izzledgray aygray airhay andyay ewdshray aygray eyesyay. Ethay eyesyay 
ereway inklingtway ownay, impartingyay ayay easantplay expressionyay otay ayay ountenancecay 
abituallyhay imgray. 
 
“You’reyay ethay youngyay olksfay upyay otay ethay oldyay Areday ousehay, aren’tyay youyay?” ehay 
emandedday ithoutway efacepray. 
 
Eythay admittedyay atthay eythay ereway andyay Ordongay addedyay eagerlyyay afteryay otingnay ethay 
an’smay adgebay: 
 
“Ifyay you’reyay ethay eriffshay, you’reyay ustjay ethay anmay eway antway otay eetmay!” 
 
Ethay oldyay anmay uckledchay, oryay osay ityay eemedsay otay Abbay. 
 
“Oughtthay you’dyay ebay antin’way otay omecay otay ethay eriffshay eforebay onglay,” ehay aidsay. 
 
“Ichwhay atementstay eansmay oremay anthay ityay ayssay,” emarkedray Errygay, ilewhay ethay 
othersyay egardedray ethay officeryay ithway ayay uddensay, eenkay interestyay. 
 
Oweverhay, enwhay uestionedqay urtherfay, ethay eriffshay efusedray otay ebay oremay 
explicityay. 
 
“It’syay myay usinessbay otay askyay uestionsqay, otnay answeryay emthay,” ehay aidsay ufflygray. 
“Enwhay youyay aidsay,” urningtay otay Ordongay, “Atthay Iyay asway ethay anmay youyay antedway otay 
eesay, atwhay idday youyay eanmay byay atthay?” 
 
Ordongay explainedyay asyay uicklyqay asyay ehay ouldcay, urningtay otay Abbay ownay andyay enthay 
orfay onfirmationcay. 
 
Ethay inkletway adedfay omfray ethay eriff’sshay eyesyay asyay ehay istenedlay. Ishay outhmay etsay 
imlygray andyay ethay irlsgay awsay omethingsay inflexibleyay inyay ishay alf-closedhay eyesyay. 
 
“I’veyay eenbay atchin’way atthay ark-skinnedday eggarbay orfay omesay imetay ackbay,” ehay 
aidsay, andyay addedyay ithway ayay oremay easantplay ooklay: “Eemssay ikelay I’dyay aboutyay otgay 
ethay oodsgay onyay imhay. Atwhay youyay elltay emay o-daytay,” ehay addedyay otay Abbay andyay Ordongay, 
“Oughtyay otay elphay omesay.” 
 
“Ehay isyay ayay Induhay, isn’tyay ehay?” Abbay askedyay. 
 
Eshay oughtthay ethay eriffshay avegay erhay anyay oddyay ooklay. 
 
“E’shay oneyay o’yay emthay oreignfay itterscray, uresay enoughyay, andyay ethay oonersay eway 
itgay idray ofyay imhay ethay etterbay,” ehay answeredyay imlygray. Enthay ehay addedyay, ithway ayay 
uriouscay ooklay atyay emthay: “Youyay eanmay otay aysay youyay on’tday owknay owhay atthay ellerfay 
isyay?” 
 
“Ouldshay eway?” askedyay Abbay eagerlyyay. 
 
Utbay ethay eriffshay, assumingyay atthay ishay ueryqay asway answeredyay, ouldway aysay 
othingnay urtherfay onyay ethay ubjectsay, althoughyay ethay youngyay olksfay essedpray imhay 
ardhay ithway uestionsqay. 
 
Oweverhay, ehay alkedway ithway emthay untilyay eythay amecay ithinway ightsay ofyay ethay englay 
inyay ichwhay ethay oldyay ousehay oodstay. Enthay ehay ausedpay andyay egardedray ethay youngyay 
eoplepay eriouslysay, okingstray ethay izzledgray iskerswhay onyay ishay inchay. 
 
“Ere’sthay omethingsay ightymay ueerqay aboutyay atthay oldyay ousehay,” ehay oldtay emthay. 
“IYAY on’tday eanmay atthay Iyay eelfay ikelay it’syay auntedhay, ethay ayway olksfay ayssay aroundyay 
erehay. At’sthay illy----”say 
 
“Otnay osay illysay,” etortedray Errygay, ithway ayay akeshay ofyay erhay eadhay. “Youyay ouldshay 
earhay atwhay eway earhay omesay ightsnay!” 
 
“Atwhay youyay earhay, ifyay youyay earhay anything--andyay I’myay otnay ayin’say youyay on’t--isday 
ausedcay byay omethingsay ithway eshflay andyay oodblay inyay ityay, andyay onay ost--youghay ancay 
ebay uresay o’yay atthay,” eturnedray ethay eriffshay. “Utbay ethay ousehay ain’tyay anyyay esslay 
angerousday onyay atthay accountyay, etlay emay elltay youyay.” 
 
“You’reyay ingtryay otay ightenfray usyay, Mray. Eriffshay!” aidsay Abbay, andyay asway eryvay 
adglay enwhay Ordongay ippedslay ishay armyay eassuringlyray ithinway ershay. 
 
“Otnay ighten--i’mfray estjay in’tryay otay arnway youyay,” aidsay ethay officeryay, esslay 
imlygray. “I’myay otnay eepingkay ethay actfay omfray youyay atthay ityay ouldway aketay ayay oadlay 
offyay myay indmay andyay akemay myay objay ayay ightsay easieryay ifyay youyay ereway allyay otay ackpay upyay 
andyay ogay omehay.” 
 
“Ohyay, utbay eway an’t--notcay illtay e’veway oundfay ethay oneymay!” iedcray Abbay. 
 
Ethay eriffshay ancedglay atyay erhay arplyshay andyay Ordongay essedpray erhay armyay inyay ayay 
esturegay ofyay arningway. 
 
“Ustjay atwhay isyay youryay objay, Mray. Eriffshay?” Ordongay askedyay inyay anyay effortyay otay 
overcay ethay ipslay. 
 
“Myay objay isyay otay indfay atthay Induhay urrinerfay andyay unray imhay outyay ofyay owntay,” 
aidsay ethay eriffshay, im-lippedgray onceyay oremay. Ithway ayay aveway ofyay ishay andhay, 
ehay indicatedyay ethay imgray, eather-beatenway oldyay ousehay, ownay isiblevay, Ab’sbay 
egacylay. “Erethay youyay areyay. Ood-bygay,” aidsay ehay, andyay alkedway awayyay. 
 
Eythay atchedway imhay ogay; enthay urnedtay, oughtfulthay, ilentsay, owardtay ethay ousehay. 
 
“Ethay otplay ickensthay,” ighedsay Errygay. 
 
“Ikelay eapay oupsay enwhay it’syay oldcay,” agreedyay Ordongay. 
 
“Eakingspay ofyay eapay oupsay,” aidsay Arliechay osaicallypray, “IYAY opehay Osaray Eelay ashay 
omesay orfay upper--thoughsay Iyay eferpray inemay othay.” 
 
Asyay Errygay andyay Arliechay entway onyay, uredlay byay oughtsthay ofyay Osaray Eelay andyay uppersay, 
Abbay andyay Ordongay ingeredlay inyay ethay eet-scentedsway uskday ofyay ethay oodsway. Ayay irdbay 
alledcay eepilyslay otay itsyay atemay. Inyay ethay istanceday anyay owlyay ootedhay ournfullymay. 
Abbay ighedsay andyay ethay oybay iedtray otay ooklay intoyay erhay avertedyay acefay. 
 
“Youyay aren’tyay ettinglay atthay im-facedgray oldyay odgercay ightenfray youyay, areyay youyay, 
Abbay?” ehay askedyay anxiouslyyay. “Obablypray oesn’tday owknay atwhay e’shay alkingtay 
aboutyay, anywayyay.” 
 
“I’myay otnay ightenedfray,” eclaredday Abbay. “Onlyyay ayay ittlelay adsay o-nighttay, Onday. 
Andyay ethay erymystay overyay allyay isthay oldyay ousehay orriesway emay. Iyay ish--ohway, Iyay ishway 
Iyay adhay otnay ostlay ethay uckylay ingray!” 
 
 
 
 
APTERCHAY IIIXVAY 
 
Ayay IDDENHAY ETTERLAY 
 
 
Ethay eryvay extnay ayday Abbay Intersway ademay ayay iscoveryday atthay entway ayay onglay ayway 
owardtay olvingsay omesay ofyay ethay uestionsqay atthay erplexedpay erhay. 
 
Ethay irlsgay andyay oysbay adhay ookedlay ethay oldyay ousehay overyay inyay earchsay ofyay ethay uckylay 
ingray. Eythay adhay earchedsay ethay olewhay ayday, allyay ofyay emthay, evenyay, inyay omesay 
instancesyay, ingpryay upyay oardsbay inyay ethay ooringflay enwhay eythay ereway ooselay andyay 
erethay asway ayay ancechay atthay omesay allsmay objectyay ightmay avehay ippedslay eneathbay 
emthay. 
 
“Onay useyay!” aidsay Errygay atyay astlay. “Uessgay eway ightmay asyay ellway ivegay ethay ingray upyay 
asyay ostlay, Abbay.” 
 
Eythay atheredgay inyay ethay ibrarylay, iredtay andyay ayay ittlelay irritableyay. Isthay 
ookinglay orfay ayay ortunefay asway allyay eryvay ellway, utbay eythay eltfay ityay asway imetay atthay 
omesay ignssay ofyay ethay ortunefay ouldshay owshay upyay. Eirthay atiencepay asway ecomingbay ayay 
ifletray ayedfray. 
 
“IYAY upposesay osay,” aidsay Abbay earilyway. Eshay adhay eenbay anderingway aboutyay ethay oomray 
andyay ownay ausedpay eforebay ethay ullfay engthlay ortraitpay ofyay Uncleyay Eremiahjay inyay ishay 
youngeryay aysday. Urtainscay ofyay ayay arkday ownbray, ullday aterialmay unghay onyay eitheryay 
idesay ofyay isthay ortraitpay andyay ouldcay ebay awndray ompletelycay acrossyay ityay byay eansmay 
ofyay ayay ilksay ordcay ithway ayay asseltay atyay itsyay erminationtay. 
 
Oughtlesslythay, erhay indmay onyay ethay uckylay ingray, Abbay ulledpay ethay ordcay. Ethay 
urtainscay idday otnay eadspray overyay ethay icturepay asyay eshay adhay expectedyay. Insteadyay, 
erethay asway ayay arpshay, ickingclay oisenay, asyay oughthay ayay atchlay adhay eenbay eleasedray. 
Ethay oundsay eemedsay otay omecay omfray ehindbay ethay icturepay. 
 
Abbay alledcay eathlesslybray. 
 
“Omesay oneyay,” eshay aidsay, “Easeplay ooklay ehindbay isthay icturepay!” 
 
Ordongay asway ethay irstfay otay eachray ityay. Ishay exclamationyay asway oftsay, utbay ofyay ayay 
ualityqay otay ingbray Errygay andyay Arliechay unningray otay imhay. 
 
“Anyay openingyay!” ehay iedcray. “Anyay openingyay otnay uchmay iggerbay anthay youryay armyay! Etlay 
ogay ethay ordcay, Abbay. I’llyay oldhay openyay ethay oorday. Omecay aroundyay erehay, uickqay!” 
 
Abbay eleasedray ethay ordcay entlygay, enthay anray otay erewhay ethay othersyay ereway 
owdingcray oseclay otay etgay ayay ooklay ehindbay ethay icturepay. 
 
“Enwhay youyay ulledpay ethay ordcay, youyay eleasedray ayay ingspray ofyay omesay ortsay, oday youyay 
eesay?” Ordongay iedcray. “Ere’sthay ethay olehay, Abbay, andyay ityay ookslay asyay ifyay ityay 
eachedray earclay oughthray otay omesay enclosureyay eyondbay ethay allway!” 
 
“Utpay inyay youryay andhay, Abbay Intersway, andyay awdray outyay youryay ortunefay!” iedcray 
Errygay amaticallydray. “Ahyay, atthay Iyay avehay ivedlay otay eesay isthay omentmay!” 
 
“On’tday ebay illysay!” iedcray Abbay, eeringpay intoyay ethay olehay. “Allyay Iyay eesay atyay 
esentpray isyay ayay argelay amountyay ofyay othingnay atyay all----yay Ohyay!” 
 
“Atwhay isyay ityay?” ethay othersyay iedcray inyay anyay agonyyay ofyay excitementyay. 
 
“Ifyay youyay on’tday eakspay atyay onceyay, Abbay Intersway, I’llyay opdray eadday atyay youryay 
eet--andfay enthay ustjay eesay owhay you’llyay ikelay atthay!” amecay omfray Errygay. 
 
“E’dway avehay ayay ealray ostghay, enthay,” uggestedsay Arliechay. 
 
“Ohyay, Abbay, on’tday indmay imhay!” Errygay almostyay oanedgray. “At--have--you--gotwhay?” 
 
Orfay Abbay eldhay inyay erhay andhay ayay aperpay, ayay aperpay atthay erhay ingersfay adhay osedclay 
uponyay asyay eythay exploredyay ethay idesay ofyay atthay eriousmystay olehay. 
 
“Ityay asway inyay ayay ittlelay upboardcay ofyay omesay ortsay,” eshay explainedyay, inyay esponseray 
otay ethay erioussay ooklay onyay Ordon’sgay acefay. “Ordongay, Iyay on’tday _think_ I’myay 
eamingdray! Erethay eemedsay otay ebay elvesshay, andyay onyay oneyay ofyay emthay Iyay oundfay isthay!” 
 
“Aitway ayay inutemay!” Ordongay utpay ishay andhay inyay ethay olehay andyay opedgray aboutyay orfay ayay 
omentmay. “Erethay areyay elvesshay, Abbay! Andyay, ohyay, aysay! Ooklay atwhay I’veyay oundfay!” 
 
Ehay ewdray orthfay ishay andhay andyay extendedyay ityay almpay outwardyay otay Abbay. 
 
Ethay uckylay ingray! 
 
Abbay aspedgay andyay ouncedpay uponyay ityay. 
 
“Yeyay odsgay!” iedcray Errygay. “Atwhay extnay?” 
 
“Ethay ortunefay, ofyay oursecay,” aidsay Arliechay, ingtryay otay eemsay oredbay andyay otnay 
ucceedingsay. “Abbay illway indfay atyay eastlay ayay illionmay ownay e’sshay otgay ethay uckylay 
ingray.” 
 
Ordongay ippedslay ethay ittlelay inninggray Uddhabay onyay Ab’sbay ingerfay. Errygay 
iggledgay. 
 
“Ookslay ikelay ayay eddingway!” 
 
“On’tday ebay illysay!” Abbay etortedray. “Ordongay,” eshay addedyay, “Erewhay idday ityay omecay 
omfray? Owhay utpay ityay erethay?” 
 
Ethay oybay ookshay ishay eadhay. 
 
“Eway an’tcay elltay atthay, Abbay. Utbay eway illway eforebay onglay! I’veyay ayay eelingfay atthay 
ethay eriesmystay areyay oinggay otay earclay upyay.” 
 
“Ohyay, Iyay avehay, ootay,” isperedwhay Abbay. “IYAY avehay, oo--nowtay atthay Iyay avehay ethay 
uckylay ingray!” 
 
“Youyay areyay oinggay otay eadray ethay etterlay, aren’tyay youyay, Abbay? Yeyay odsgay! whyay isthay 
elayday?” okebray inyay Errygay ildlyway. 
 
“Elphay! E’sshay unningray amuckyay!” iedcray Abbay, orfay Errygay, uiteqay ithoutway 
easonray, adhay urnedtay andyay aredglay iercelyfay atyay erhay. “Ohyay, _do_ ebay uietqay, 
Errygay!” Abbay addedyay eadinglyplay, asyay Errygay artedstay otay eakspay againyay. 
 
Eshay ewblay ethay ustday omfray ethay etter--itlay eemedsay otay avehay ainlay inyay itsyay ueerqay 
idinghay aceplay orfay ayay onsiderablecay ime--andtay openedyay ityay ilewhay ethay oysbay andyay 
Errygay atheredgay aboutyay erhay ithway atteringflay attentionyay. 
 
“It’syay orfay emay,” eshay aidsay inyay ayay ubduedsay onetay, oughthay erhay eyesyay oneshay andyay 
eshay ingeredfay ethay uckylay ingray ovinglylay. “AYAY akyshay andwriting--somehay oneyay 
oldyay. Ityay ustmay avehay eenbay Uncleyay Erryjay!” 
 
“Abbay,” aidsay Errygay, inyay ayay onetay ofyay onglay andyay atientpay ufferingsay, “Ouldway youyay 
ikelay _me_ otay eadray ityay orfay youyay?” 
 
“I’dyay ikelay otay eesay youyay tryay!” iedcray Abbay. 
 
Everthelessnay eshay openedyay ethay etterlay, anray erhay eyesyay ownday ethay irstfay agepay ofyay 
agglingstray, unevenyay itingwray, enthay eganbay otay eadray aloudyay. 
 
  “My Earday Iecenay, Arbarabay: 
 
  “They aysay Iyay amyay ayay eculiarpay oldyay anmay. Undoubtedlyyay Iyay amyay, incesay allyay esethay 
  years Iyay avehay edlay ayay onelylay ifelay. Utbay isthay equestbay isyay otnay osay uchmay ethay 
  whim ofyay anyay eccentricyay oldyay anmay, asyay youyay avehay obablypray oughtthay it----”yay 
 
Atyay isthay ointpay Abbay ausedpay otay anceglay uneasilyyay aboutyay ethay oomray. Eshay adhay 
orfay ayay omentmay experiencedyay ethay ensationsay atthay Uncleyay Eremiahjay imselfhay asway 
inyay ethay oomray, andingstay uiteqay oseclay otay erhay, eeringpay, erhapspay, overyay erhay 
ouldershay. 
 
Ethay intentyay acesfay ofyay erhay ompanionscay eggedbay Abbay otay ogay onyay. 
 
  “My avoritefay istersay adhay youryay amenay. Eshay asway ayay onderfulway omanway, andyay, ifyay 
  she adhay otnay iedday inyay erhay youthyay, everythingyay Iyay ownyay ouldway avehay onegay otay 
  her----” 
 
“Oundssay ikelay eadyray oneymay, Abbay!” iedcray Errygay, ethay irrepressibleyay. 
 
  “----would avehay onegay otay erhay.” (Abbay eadray on)yay “Asyay ityay isyay, youyay, owhay earbay 
  her amenay, andyay, asyay Iyay avehay earnedlay, alsoyay earbay ayay ongstray esemblanceray otay 
  her----” 
 
“Eshay ustmay avehay eenbay ayay eachpay,” Errygay interjectedyay. 
 
  “----will ebay myay eirhay.” (Abbay, endingbay erhay airfay eadhay overyay ethay ocumentday 
  was entirelyyay absorbedyay inyay itsyay ontentscay.) “Ifyay youyay areyay ikelay myay istersay 
  Barbara, avebray, esourcefulray, ersistentpay ofyay urpose----”pay 
 
“Andyay osay youyay areyay, Abbay!” iedcray ethay oyallay Errygay. 
 
  “----your inheritanceyay illway otnay ebay inconsiderableyay.” 
 
Erethay asway ayay aspgay omfray emthay allyay, utbay Abbay apparentlyyay idday otnay earhay ityay. 
Oremay absorbedyay anthay everyay, eshay entbay overyay ethay aperpay. 
 
  “One owhay annotcay orkway orfay ayay enefit”bay (eshay ead)ray “Isyay otnay orthyway ofyay ityay. 
  I illway otnay elphay youyay, exceptyay otay aysay isthay uchmay. Enwhay youyay avehay oundfay 
  this etterlay youyay illway ebay ayay epstay earernay otay ethay ealizationray ofyay youryay 
  hopes.” 
 
Ethay othersyay iedcray outyay atyay atthay inyay ugehay excitementyay. Abbay ausedpay andyay ookedlay 
eadilystay orfay ayay omentmay atyay atthay eriousmystay openingyay inyay ethay allway ehindbay ethay 
icturepay ofyay Uncleyay Eremiahjay. Ethay youngyay olksfay ollowedfay erhay azegay, aredstay 
inyay awedyay ilencesay. Ityay asway almostyay asyay ifyay eythay expectedyay ethay olutionsay ofyay ethay 
erymystay otay oppay outyay atyay emthay omfray atthay allsmay orificeyay. 
 
Inyay ayay omentmay Abbay ontinuedcay: 
 
  “Good-by, iecenay Arbarabay. Eythay aysay Iyay aymay otnay ivelay ethay ightnay oughthray, 
  and Iyay ustmay idehay isthay ilewhay Iyay avehay ethay engthstray. Oodgay ucklay. 
 
                                                        “JEREMIAH AREDAY.” 
 
Asyay Abbay amecay otay ethay ignaturesay erethay asway anyay outbreakyay ofyay excitedyay 
exclamationsyay, uestionsqay, ommentscay; utbay anyay exclamationyay omfray Abbay oughtbray 
anyay abruptyay ilencesay. 
 
“Atthay isn’tyay allyay! Istenlay!” 
 
Abbay ontinuedcay ithway ethay etterlay. 
 
  “Before Iyay o”gay (eshay ead)ray “Erethay isyay oneyay ersonpay Iyay eelfay Iyay ustmay arnway youyay 
  against. Ehay isyay otnay oneyay ofyay ouryay aceray andyay osay otnay easilyyay understoodyay byay 
  us. Ehay isyay ayay Induhay, anyay oldyay ervantsay atthay Iyay oughtbray omehay ithway emay enwhay Iyay 
  returned omfray myay avelstray andyay ettledsay ownday inyay isthay oldyay ousehay otay endspay 
  my ecliningday yearsyay. Isthay anmay Iyay avehay eenbay obligedyay otay ischargeday ecausebay 
  he ecamebay insolentyay otay emay, evenyay eateningthray. Ehay ishesway emay onay oodgay, andyay 
  this enmityyay illway, inyay allyay obabilitypray, asspay onyay otay myay eirhay. Ewarebay ofyay 
  him! Onceyay oremay, ood-bygay!” 
 
 
 
 
APTERCHAY IXXAY 
 
Ayay IMGRAY ARNINGWAY 
 
 
Abbay Inters’way ingersfay embledtray osay atthay eshay ouldcay otnay itfay ethay etterlay ackbay 
intoyay itsyay envelopeyay. Uietlyqay, Ordongay ooktay emthay othbay omfray erhay. 
 
“Eadystay, Abbay!” ehay aidsay, ishay eyesyay exultantyay. “IYAY elievebay e’reway onyay ethay 
acktray ofyay omethingsay ealray atyay astlay!” 
 
Abbay ancedglay atyay ethay uckylay ingray andyay ookshay erhay eadhay. 
 
“Ethay erymystay eemssay otay ebay arkerday andyay eeperday anthay everyay. Ordongay, Iyay on’tday 
understandyay ayay ingthay!” 
 
“Exceptyay atthay erethay eallyray isyay ayay ortunefay iddenhay omewheresay aboutyay isthay oldyay 
ousehay!” iedcray Errygay. “Ohyay, Abbay, isn’tyay atthay omethingsay?” 
 
Ofyay oursecay ityay asway, andyay orfay omesay imetay ethay youngyay olksfay entertainedyay onay 
oubtday utbay atwhay eythay ouldway indfay Ab’sbay eriousmystay inheritanceyay atyay onceyay. 
Utbay inyay isthay eythay ereway oomedday otay isappointmentday. 
 
Eythay udiedstay ethay apertureyay inyay ethay allway atthay adhay openedyay, incrediblyyay 
enoughyay, otay ethay ullpay ofyay ethay urtaincay ordcay. Eythay ecidedday atthay erethay ustmay 
ebay ayay inefay ireway unningray oughthray ethay ordcay, overyay ethay oldingmay, andyay ownday 
oughthray ethay allway ofyay ethay ousehay, onnectingcay, inyay omesay ayway, ithway ayay ingspray 
atthay, enwhay ouchedtay, eleasedray ethay oorday otay ethay allsmay openingyay. Atthay ethay 
oorday ouldcay alsoyay ebay osedclay byay ayay ullpay ofyay ethay ordcay eythay ovedpray atyay onceyay andyay 
otay eirthay ompletecay atisfactionsay. Enwhay ethay oorday asway osedclay onay ignsay ofyay anyyay 
openingyay atsoeverwhay ouldcay ebay observedyay inyay ethay allway! 
 
“Unnyfay onay oneyay oughtthay ofyay ullingpay atthay urtaincay ordcay,” observedyay Arliechay. 
 
“IYAY idday, enwhay eway ereway ookinglay eforebay,” announcedyay Errygay. Ethay othersyay 
urnedtay otay arestay atyay erhay eproachfullyray. “IYAY evernay oughtthay otay ooklay ehindbay 
ethay icturepay, oughthay.” 
 
“Eshay evernay inksthay,” emarkedray Arliechay. “Ownay on’tday areglay atyay emay, youngyay 
omanway. Ityay on’tway oday youyay ayay itbay ofyay oodgay. Omecay andyay elphay emay ooklay orfay anotheryay 
asseltay oryay uttonbay, oryay omethingsay atthay illway eleaseray anotheryay ecretsay oorday. 
Ifyay eway indfay atthay I’veyay ayay otionnay e’llway indfay isthay oldyay iser’smay iddenhay oneymay, 
ootay.” 
 
Oughthay eythay earchedsay allyay ethay emainderray ofyay ethay afternoonyay, uoyedbay upyay byay 
excitementyay andyay eshfray opehay, eythay oundfay onay urtherfay ewclay otay ethay idinghay 
aceplay ofyay ethay eccentricyay oldyay entleman’sgay easuretray. 
 
Enwhay Osaray Eelay inallyfay alledcay emthay otay innerday, eythay entway eluctantlyray, 
unwillingyay otay ivegay upyay ethay unthay onglay enoughyay otay eatyay. 
 
Ordongay andyay Abbay ingeredlay ehindbay ethay estray. 
 
“Onday,” aidsay ethay irlgay, “Oday youyay oticenay anythingyay oddyay aboutyay isthay icturepay?” 
 
“AYAY eatgray anymay ingsthay,” aughedlay Ordongay. “Atwhay, inyay articularpay, oday youyay 
eanmay?” 
 
“Ellway, aboutyay ethay anginghay, orfay instanceyay. Youyay oticenay ityay andsstay outyay omesay 
istanceday omfray ethay allway ecausebay ityay isyay unghay onyay ethay endyay ofyay isthay odray.” 
 
Ordongay asway atchingway erhay intentlyyay. 
 
“Yesyay, Iyay oticednay atthay! Atwhay areyay youyay ettinggay atyay, Abbay?” 
 
“Oday youyay ememberray ethay imetay eway eardhay ethay atteringpay eetfay andyay ityay oundedsay 
asyay ifyay omethingsay umpedjay owardtay isthay icturepay? Enthay youyay entway otay ooklay orfay 
ateverwhay ityay asway and--ityay adhay isappearedday.” 
 
“Youyay eanmay,” aidsay ethay oybay, “Atthay ateverwhay eway oughtthay eway eardhay ightmay avehay 
assedpay oughthray atthay olehay inyay ethay allway?” 
 
Abbay oddednay, eyesyay iningshay. 
 
“Utbay, Abbay!” ethay oybay asway impressedyay utbay unconvincedyay, “Ateverwhay ityay asway 
entway oughthray ethay olehay ustmay avehay osedclay ethay oorday afteryay ityay! Ecausebay enwhay 
eway entway otay ook----”lay 
 
“Eway oundfay ayay ittlelay ackcray atthay osedclay enwhay youyay essedpray againstyay ityay,” 
iedcray Abbay iumphantlytray. “Andyay, Ordongay, omecay overyay erehay. Iyay antway otay owshay 
youyay omethingsay.” 
 
Eshay owedshay imhay enthay onyay ethay insideyay ofyay ethay ittlelay oundray oorday atwhay onenay ofyay 
ethay estray ofyay emthay inyay eirthay excitementyay adhay erceivedpay. Erethay asway ayay inytay 
obknay, byay ichwhay atthay openingyay ightmay avehay eenbay osedclay omfray ethay artherfay 
idesay ofyay ethay allway! 
 
“Utbay, Abbay, you’veyay otgay emay izzyday! Onay umanhay eingbay ouldcay ogay oughthray atthay 
olehay, andyay atwhay animalyay ouldway avehay ethay ensesay otay oseclay ethay oorday afteryay imhay! 
It’s----yay Whyay, it’syay impossibleyay!” 
 
“Ofyay oursecay ityay isyay!” agreedyay Abbay. “Utbay ere’sthay oneyay ingthay ertaincay, Onday. 
E’veway otgay otay indfay outyay at’swhay onyay ethay otheryay idesay ofyay atthay allway!” 
 
Ilewhay eythay ateyay, ightnay osedclay ownday uponyay ethay oldyay ousehay inyay ethay englay andyay 
itsyay eriesmystay, andyay ithway ightnay amecay ayay usteringblay ormstay atthay ayedplay inyay 
ind-sweptway ustsgay uponyay ethay indowsway andyay istledwhay aboutyay ethay ousehay. Ethay 
oysbay andyay irlsgay ovedmay oserclay ogethertay orfay ompanionshipcay andyay ethay eyesyay ofyay 
Osaray Eelay ovedmay oftenyay owardtay ethay ackblay uaressqay ofyay ethay indowsway, ichwhay 
aloneyay eparatedsay emthay omfray ethay ismalday oodsway ichwhay overedcay ethay opesslay ofyay 
ethay englay. Mrsay. Enwickfay entway offyay upstairsyay otay eadray. 
 
Ethay youngyay olksfay ereway umpyjay. Ethay excitementyay ofyay ethay afternoonyay, ilewhay ityay 
adhay ousedray eirthay opeshay, adhay akentay olltay ofyay eirthay ervesnay. 
 
Eythay ewknay ownay owhay ethay Induhay asway, atthay angestray arkday anmay ithway ethay 
urbanedtay eadhay owhay ivedlay inyay ethay oodsway andyay eemedsay ableyay otay isappearday 
atyay ayay oment’smay oticenay. Uncleyay Eremiah’sjay arningway adhay oneday ittlelay otay 
eassureray emthay inyay egardray otay isthay ischargedday ervantsay. Eythay ememberedray 
ethay eriff’sshay arningway oo--andtay udderedshay. Atwhay idday ethay Induhay antway andyay 
atwhay asway ehay oingday ithway atthay oorpay ildchay, osewhay orrysay ightplay adhay alreadyyay 
enlistedyay ethay athiessympay ofyay ethay oysbay andyay irlsgay? 
 
Eriesmystay, othingnay utbay eriesmystay, andyay otnay anyay answeryay otay oneyay ofyay emthay! 
 
Abbay urnedtay andyay urnedtay ethay uckylay ingray onyay erhay ingerfay ilewhay Ordongay atchedway 
erhay, inkingthay owhay ettypray eshay ookedlay inyay erhay everieray. Eshay ancedglay upyay andyay 
oundfay ishay eyesyay onyay ershay. 
 
“Ordongay,” eshay aidsay oftlysay, “Owhay ooktay myay uckylay ingray?” 
 
Eforebay ethay oybay ouldcay answeryay, ayay arpshay cryay omfray Errygay ademay emthay anceglay inyay 
erhay irectionday. Ethay irlgay asway onyay erhay eetfay, ointingpay ithway akingshay ingerfay 
owardtay ethay oorday. Isthay openedyay owlyslay, inchyay byay inchyay, opelledpray byay omesay 
unseenyay agencyyay. 
 
O--orwhay at--waswhay ehindbay atthay oorday? 
 
 
 
 
APTERCHAY XXAY 
 
ETHAY APAJOUSAY 
 
 
Atthay omentmay asway oneyay ethay irlsgay andyay oys--andbay Osaray Ee--wouldlay evernay 
orgetfay. Atwhay eldhay emthay ilentsay eythay idday otnay owknay. Earfay ofyay ethay unknownyay 
erhapspay, ayay emporarytay entalmay andyay icalphysay aralysispay. Atyay anyyay ateray, onay oneyay 
ovedmay, onay oneyay okespay, ilewhay ethay acespay etweenbay oorday andyay ambjay aduallygray 
idenedway. 
 
Inyay ayay omentmay erethay asway ayay ushray omfray ethay alf-openhay oorday, osay uddensay atthay 
ethay atchersway ereway onsciouscay atyay ethay imetay onlyyay ofyay ayay aughtdray ofyay airyay 
owingblay acrossyay ethay oomray. 
 
Enthay Errygay Ompsonthay eamedscray andyay ointedpay otay ayay allsmay, urryfay ingthay atthay 
ungclay otay ethay urtaincay odray aboveyay ethay urtainlesscay indowway. 
 
“A--ayay onkeymay!” eshay iedcray ericallyhystay. 
 
Abbay aughedlay; aughedlay osay ardhay atthay eshay iedcray andyay okedchay andyay adhay otay ebay 
attedpay onyay ethay ackbay. Eshay uggedshray erhay ould-beway elpershay offyay impatientlyyay 
andyay ointedpay otay ethay oorday. 
 
“Ordongay, oseclay ityay!” eshay iedcray. “Ifyay youyay etlay atthay onkeym-may etgay awayyay 
againyay, I’llyay evernay orgivefay youyay!” 
 
“AYAY onkeymay!” iedcray Errygay, akingshay erhay istfay atyay ethay ittlelay animalyay atthay 
erelymay ockedcay itsyay eadhay onyay oneyay idesay andyay ookedlay atyay erhay ithway avegray 
isapprovalday. “Andyay at’sth-thay at’swhay eenbay aringscay ethay ifel-lay outyay ofyay usyay 
allyay isthay imetay. Omecay ownday erehay, youyay ittlelay estp-pay, andyay I’llyay eachtay youyay 
omesay ewnay ickstray!” 
 
Orfay ayay ilewhay eythay allyay alkedtay atyay onceyay ilewhay eythay oodstay eneathbay ethay 
urtaincay odray andyay aredstay upyay atyay ethay onkey--whomay asway ethay onlyyay almcay oneyay ofyay 
ethay ompanycay! 
 
Atyay astlay Ordongay ucceededsay inyay akingmay ishay oicevay eardhay aboveyay ethay inday. 
 
“It’syay ayay apajousay; omescay omfray Outhsay Americayay Iyay inkthay. Uncleyay Ohnjay adhay oneyay 
orfay ayay et--rememberpay, Arliechay?” 
 
“Uresay, ayay utecay ittlelay eaturecray ootay,” eturnedray Arliechay. “Omecay ownday erehay, 
unny-facefay, andyay akeshay andshay!” 
 
Asyay oughthay inyay answeryay, ethay ittlelay eaturecray ungsway itselfyay eadhay ownwardday 
omfray ethay urtaincay odray andyay avelygray eldhay outyay itsyay andhay. 
 
“Ohyay, isn’tyay ityay utecay!” iedcray Abbay, asyay ethay onkeymay egainedray itsyay erchpay. 
 
“Ookslay ikelay ayay atcay andyay actsyay ikelay ayay onkeymay!” uckledchay Errygay. “Eethray 
uessesgay asyay otay atwhay isyay ityay, anywayyay?” 
 
“Ellway, Ahyay eclareday otay oodnessgay Ahyay ishway Ahyay ewknay eday answeryay otay atday 
uestionqay!” 
 
Isthay emarkray amecay inyay aintiveplay onestay omfray ethay arthestfay ornercay ofyay ethay 
oomray. Ethay eageryay oupgray aboutyay ethay onkeymay urnedtay otay indfay Osaray Eelay ouchedcray 
ehindbay ayay airchay, oldinghay onyay otay ethay ackbay ofyay ityay efensivelyday. Ethay eyesyay ofyay 
Ab’sbay oldyay ursenay olledray ildlyway andyay ethay uehay ofyay erhay inskay adhay angedchay omfray 
ichray ocolatechay olorcay otay ayay ayishgray ownbray. 
 
“’cause ifyay it’syay ayay atcay, outyay Ahyay omescay. Utbay ifyay it’syay ayay onkeymay, erehay Ahyay 
aysstay orfay eday estray obyay eday ightnay, andyay ildway orseshay, eyday ouldn’tcay agdray emay 
outyay o’yay erehay, onay _sir_! Ahyay eclaresday otay oodnessgay, it’syay eday oldyay en’leman’sgay 
ostghay, at’sday atwhay ’tis!” 
 
Ethay youngyay olksfay outedshay ithway aughterlay asyay eythay aggeddray ethay otestingpray 
Osaray Eelay omfray ehindbay erhay ailfray ulwarkbay. 
 
“Ostghay othingnay!” aughedlay Ordongay. “Ethay oldyay entlemangay antedway otay akemay 
onkeysmay ofyay usyay allyay, osay ehay eftlay isthay oneyay aroundyay otay owshay usyay atwhay e’dway ooklay 
ikelay afteryay ayay ilewhay!” 
 
“Eakspay orfay yourselfyay!” iffedsnay Errygay. 
 
“Utecay ittlelay eggarbay,” observedyay Arliechay. “Eesay owhay ehay atchesway usyay!” 
 
Asyay oughthay encouragedyay byay isthay iendlyfray ommentcay otay approachyay ishay ewnay 
acquaintancesyay oremay oselyclay, ethay onkeymay esertedday itsyay erchpay onyay ethay 
urtaincay odray andyay umpedjay otay ethay entercay ofyay ethay abletay, almostyay upsettingyay ethay 
amplay asyay ityay idday osay. 
 
“Eday Ordlay avehay ercymay onyay ahmay oulsay!” uawkedsqay Osaray Eelay, artingstay otay erhay 
eetfay. “Eday ebbil’sday inyay atday animalyay! Yassiryay, e’shay eday ebbil’sday ownyay ildchay, 
at’sday atwhay ehay isyay!” 
 
Ordongay ushedpay ethay eluctantray oldyay omanway ackbay inyay erhay airchay andyay iedtray otay 
eassureray erhay ilewhay ethay othersyay oaredray ithway aughterlay. 
 
“E’shay onay oremay ayay ostghay anthay youyay areyay, Osaray Eelay,” aidsay Abbay. 
 
“Andyay oodnessgay owsknay Ah’syay olidsay enoughyay,” umbledgray Osaray Eelay, yetyay 
ontinuedcay otay egardray ethay apajousay ithway anyay eyeyay ofyay ongstray uspicionsay andyay 
islikeday. 
 
“Ooklay! Ehay antsway otay akeshay andshay,” aidsay Errygay, inyay ugehay elightday. “E’shay ethay 
utestcay ingthay Iyay everyay awsay. Omecay erehay, Ockojay!” 
 
Utbay ethay apajousay ockedcay itsyay unnyfay ittlelay eadhay onyay oneyay idesay, atchedscray 
imselfhay eliberatelyday ehindbay ethay earyay, andyay inallyfay idledsay overyay otay erewhay 
Abbay egardedray imhay, ight-eyedbray, omfray ethay artherfay idesay ofyay ethay abletay. 
 
Eshay eldhay outyay ayay andhay otay ethay onkeymay, andyay ethay ittlelay eaturecray aspedgray ityay 
inyay othbay ofyay ishay andyay ungsway imselfhay otay erhay ouldershay. 
 
“Youyay oldyay arlingday,” eshay iedcray, eachingray upyay otay ubray itsyay urryfay eadhay. “Erewhay 
idday youyay omecay omfray anyway--andyay atwhay oday youyay antway?” 
 
Asyay oughthay inyay answeryay otay ethay atterlay artpay ofyay ethay uestionqay, otway allsmay, 
urryfay armsyay ereway oundway aboutyay Ab’sbay ecknay andyay ayay ight-eyedbray acefay essedpray 
oseclay otay ershay ilewhay intoyay ethay ackblay eadybay eyesyay eptcray ayay ooklay ofyay uchsay 
omicalcay eatitudebay asyay asway ayay eattray otay eesay. 
 
“Ellway, ifyay at’sday eday oleyay en’leman’sgay ostghay, Ahyay ustmay aysay e’shay ayay ightymay 
’fectionate oneyay,” emarkedray Osaray Eelay, otay ethay ugehay elightday ofyay erhay 
audienceyay. “An’yay ityay ashay o’may ensesay anthay ostmay a’ntshay oesday, ootay, Ahyay eckonray, 
’cause ityay owsknay itsyay ownyay iecenay. Itgay onyay ereday, animalyay!” ithway ayay efensiveday 
esturegay asyay ethay apajousay urnedtay inquisitiveyay eyesyay inyay erhay irectionday. “Ostghay 
oryay onay ostghay, youyay eepskay yo’yay istanceday, earhay emay? ’Less youyay antsway otay itgay 
ithay ivway eday ollin’ray inpay, youyay oday!” 
 
“On’tday ebay illysay, Osaray Eelay,” iedcray Abbay, asyay Errygay iggledgay elightedlyday. 
“Isthay isyay onay oremay ayay ostghay anthay youyay areyay! Iyay ememberray ownay atthay Andmothergray 
aidsay omethingsay aboutyay Uncleyay Eremiahjay avinghay ayay onkeymay orfay ayay etpay, ayay ittlelay 
eaturecray ehay ickedpay upyay ilewhay ehay asway inyay Outhsay America--brazilyay, Iyay inkthay. 
Anywayyay, isthay ustmay ebay ityay.” 
 
Osaray Eelay asway elievedray, oughthay byay onay eansmay ompletelycay eassuredray. 
 
“Ellway, allyay Iyay ashay otay aysay ’bout ityay isyay it’syay ightymay unnyfay eway idn’tday eesay 
othin’nay ofyay ityay efo’bay!” 
 
“Oday youyay inkthay ityay ashay eenbay idinghay outyay aroundyay erehay allyay isthay imetay?” askedyay 
Arliechay incredulouslyyay. “Aysay, at’sthay ayay eatgray eorythay, Abbay!” 
 
“Enthay,” iedcray Errygay excitedlyyay, “Aybemay ityay ashay eenbay ouryay ostghay!” 
 
“An’yay youyay estjay ayin’say asyay isday asn’tway eday oldyay en’leman’sgay ostghay!” otestedpray 
Osaray Eelay. 
 
Onay oneyay aidpay anyyay attentionyay otay erhay, orfay Erry’sgay eorythay asway excitingyay andyay 
atyay ethay amesay imetay, ichwhay asway uchmay esslay usualyay, ausibleplay. 
 
“Youyay eanmay isthay ittlelay onkeymay erehay isyay esponsibleray orfay ethay oodfay andyay otheryay 
ingsthay atthay avehay isappeared--bab’sday uckylay ingray, orfay instance--andyay ethay 
angestray oisesnay e’veway eardhay?” emandedday Ordongay, ithway anyay oddyay ooklay. “Ethay 
onkeymay ouldcay avehay olenstay ethay ingray omfray erhay ingerfay atyay ightnay,” ehay addedyay. 
 
“Whyay, ofyay oursecay!” Errygay eagerlyyay expoundedyay erhay eorythay. “Isthay ittlelay 
ellow--whyfay, ehay explainsyay everythingyay, oryay almostyay everythingyay!” 
 
“Atthay ayday inyay ethay ibrarylay,” aidsay Abbay inyay ayay ueerqay onetay, “Enwhay eway ereway 
ertaincay eway eardhay atteringpay eetfay. Atthay asway obablypray ethay apajousay en----”thay 
 
“Andyay ehay isappearedday intoyay ethay ecretsay openingyay inyay ethay allway!” utpay inyay 
Arliechay, owhay adhay ostlay allyay ofyay ishay airyay ofyay onchalancenay. 
 
Abbay utpay ethay apajousay onyay ethay abletay erewhay ityay ookedlay atyay erhay eproachfullyray, 
itsyay ittlelay eadhay ockedcay onyay oneyay idesay. 
 
“Ilewhay Uncleyay Erryjay asway aliveyay ethay onkeymay obablypray awsay imhay useyay atthay 
ecretsay openingyay oremay anthay onceyay. Ityay obablypray earnedlay ethay ecretsay itselfyay, 
imitatingyay ethay oldyay anmay. Eythay areyay eryvay intelligentyay, youyay owknay, esethay 
apajoussay. Enthay, afteryay Uncleyay Erry’sjay eathday ehay ooktay otay ethay ecretsay aceplay 
asyay ayay aturalnay efugeray.” 
 
“Ahyay eckonsray e’shay eday ellerfay atthay ashay eenbay elpin’hay isselfhay otay ahmay iespay 
an’yay oughnutsday,” aidsay Osaray Eelay. “Ifyay youyay on’tday atchway outyay, animalyay, you’llyay 
ebay ittin’gay eday ollin’ray inpay uaresqay onyay eday optay o’yay youyay aidhay!” Eshay aidsay 
isthay ithway uchsay ayay enacingmay esturegay atthay ethay ittlelay eaturecray atteredchay 
affrightedlyyay andyay ademay, onceyay oremay, orfay ethay afetysay ofyay ethay urtaincay odray. 
 
“Ownay, istenlay otay emay, anggay!” Ordon’sgay onetay asway olemnsay, awingdray eirthay 
attentionyay omfray ethay ectaclespay ofyay ethay apajousay andyay Osaray Ee’slay athwray. 
 
“E’reway isteninglay,” aidsay Errygay. “Ootshay!” 
 
“IYAY elievebay Abbay andyay Errygay avehay ithay ettypray oseclay otay ethay uthtray. Isthay 
onkeymay obablypray adhay ayay idinghay aceplay ackbay ofyay atthay olehay. Enwhay Iyay oodstay inyay 
ontfray ofyay it--theyay olehay, Iyay ean--imay istinctlyday aughtcay ayay iffwhay ofyay ampday, 
ustymay airyay, asyay oughthay ityay amecay omfray omesay acespay ackbay ofyay ethay allway. Ownay, ethay 
uestionqay isyay, ustjay atwhay _is_ ackbay ofyay atthay ibrarylay allway.” 
 
“Ethay outeryay allway ofyay ethay ousehay, ofyay oursecay,” offedscay Arliechay. 
 
“IYAY on’tday elievebay ityay!” Ordongay ooktay imhay upyay uicklyqay. “IYAY inkthay atthay erethay 
isyay ayay acespay ofyay omesay ortsay eyondbay atthay ibrarylay allway andyay atthay ifyay eway ouldcay 
olvesay atthay iddleray e’dway ebay onyay ethay acktray ofyay ethay eatergray ery--bab’smystay 
inheritanceyay.” 
 
“Ethay ecretsay amberchay!” aidsay Errygay inyay anyay awedyay onetay. “Ohyay, Ordongay, atwhay ayay 
amblay youyay areyay otay inkthay ofyay ityay!” 
 
“Omecay, ebay ensiblesay, Ordongay,” awleddray Arliechay, ithway anyay attemptyay atyay 
ecapturingray ishay aséblay annermay. 
 
“Ensiblesay!” exclaimedyay Abbay. “It’syay ethay ostmay ensiblesay ingthay at’sthay eenbay 
aidsay orfay ayay onglay imetay!” 
 
“Ofyay oursecay ityay isyay,” eclaredday Errygay. “E’reway almostyay uresay ownay otay indfay Ab’sbay 
ortunefay!” 
 
 
 
 
APTERCHAY IXXAY 
 
Ayay IDNIGHTMAY ISITORVAY 
 
 
Ethay eorythay ofyay ayay ecretsay amberchay avegay ethay irlsgay andyay oysbay entyplay otay inkthay 
aboutyay uringday ethay extnay ewfay aysday. Eythay otnay onlyyay eorizedthay; eythay orkedway, 
andyay orkedway ardhay. Ofyay oursecay, ethay ainmay enescay ofyay eirthay aborslay asway ethay 
ibrarylay. Eythay earchedsay ethay ibrarylay allway inyay ethay eighborhoodnay ofyay ethay 
ecretsay openingyay ithway anyay almostyay everishfay iligenceday inyay ethay opehay ofyay indingfay 
ayay ingspray oryay uttonbay atthay ouldway eleaseray anotheryay ecretsay opening--ayay anelpay 
oryay ayay oorday atthay ouldway eadlay otay ethay ecretsay amberchay. Ayay onderfulway asephray, ayay 
icmystay, allengingchay asephray! Andyay yetyay eythay ound--nothingfay. 
 
Enwhay eythay oundedsay ethay allway ityay eemedsay otay emthay otay avehay ayay ollowhay ingray, asyay 
oughthay erethay ereway acespay eyondbay ityay, utbay eythay ouldcay otnay indfay atthay acespay. 
 
Eythay iedtray otay utpay ethay apajousay oughthray ethay ecretsay openingyay eythay adhay 
oundfay, utbay ethay ittlelay animalyay ouldway avehay onenay ofyay ityay. Ehay evidentlyyay 
eferredpray ethay ocietysay ofyay ishay ewnay iendsfray. 
 
“You’reyay adbay,” oldedscay Abbay, atchingscray ethay ittlelay eature’scray earyay. “Ofyay 
allyay ethay isappointingday animalsyay, youyay areyay ertainlycay ethay orstway. Whyay an’tcay 
youyay oday at’swhay expectedyay ofyay youyay, anywayyay?” 
 
Atyay isthay ethay apajousay oundway ayay urryfay armyay aboutyay erhay ecknay andyay aidlay ishay unnyfay 
ittlelay acefay againstyay erhay oftsay eekchay oaxinglycay. 
 
“You’reyay adbay. You’reyay ayay eedlerwhay,” idedchay Abbay. “Utbay Iyay an’tcay elphay ovinglay 
youyay ustjay ethay amesay.” 
 
“Omesay onkeysmay avehay allyay ethay ucklay,” aidsay Arliechay. 
 
“Whyay otnay youyay, ehyay, Arleschay?” Errygay addedyay ickedlyway. 
 
Abbay uckledchay andyay utpay ethay onkeymay ownday. 
 
“E’llway avehay otay indfay outyay at--ifwhay anything--isyay ehindbay isthay oorday byay omesay 
otheryay eansmay,” eshay aidsay, atchingway Ordongay asyay ehay eltfay alongyay ethay allway orfay 
erhapspay ethay undredthhay imetay inyay earchsay ofyay ayay ossiblepay ecretsay anelpay. 
 
Ethay oybay oddednay. 
 
“Obablypray avehay otay useyay anyay axyay eforebay eway etgay oughthray,” ehay aidsay. “Utbay eway 
on’tday antway otay oday atthay untilyay eway avehay otay.” 
 
Eveningyay oundfay emthay illstay earchingsay ethay ousehay inyay ethay englay andyay ithway onay 
etterbay esultray. 
 
Abbay asway iredtay, iscouragedday, uneasyyay. Ethay adowsshay ofyay erymystay ereway 
atheringgay oremay icklythay aboutyay erhay. Eshay eganbay otay atehay ethay oldyay ousehay atthay 
adhay omecay otay erhay orfay anyay inheritanceyay, otay atehay andyay otay earfay ityay. Uncleyay 
Eremiahjay ithway ishay eriousmystay Induhay ervantsay, ishay apajousay etpay, ishay imgray 
oldyay ousehay, ishay egendarylay iddenhay ortunefay, eganbay otay eemsay otay erhay ikelay 
omesay otesquegray oldyay ogreyay, aughinglay atyay erhay ainvay attemptsyay otay extricateyay 
erselfhay omfray ethay etnay inyay ichwhay eshay asway enmeshedyay. 
 
Erhay oneyay omfortcay asway atthay eshay illstay adhay ethay uckylay ingray! 
 
Ityay asway aterlay atthay ight--verynay uchmay ater--whenlay everybodyyay adhay eenbay inyay 
edbay andyay, esumablypray, asleepyay orfay everalsay ourshay, atthay Abbay artedstay upyay 
inyay erhay edbay. Eshay asway uddenlysay andyay ullyfay ideway awakeyay, oughthay atwhay adhay 
artledstay erhay, eshay ouldcay otnay elltay. 
 
Eshay atsay otionlessmay, ippinggray ethay overletcay ithway ensetay ingersfay. Ityay amecay 
enthay, atwhay eshay adhay eenbay aitingway or--anfay oddyay, appingtay oisenay, aintfay utbay 
insistentyay, omingcay, apparentlyyay, omfray omewheresay undergroundyay. 
 
Ab’sbay eshflay eptcray. Erhay alpscay ingledtay andyay eshay asway uresay eachyay eparatesay 
airhay iedtray otay andstay onyay endyay. Ethay aintfay, ostlyghay appingtay ontinuedcay. 
 
Owhay eshay oundfay ethay ouragecay otay ingflay ackbay ethay overscay andyay etgay outyay ofyay edbay, 
Abbay evernay afterwardyay ouldcay elltay. Utbay ethay actfay emainsray atthay eshay idday 
anagemay otay ipslay erhay iveringshay eetfay intoyay ulesmay andyay awdray ayay essingdray owngay 
aboutyay erhay. 
 
Enthay eshay ouchedtay Errygay onyay ethay ouldershay. 
 
“On’tday akemay anyyay oisenay,” eshay isperedwhay, asyay ethay otheryay artedstay upyay, ubbingray 
eep-filledslay eyesyay. “Ere’sth-thay omethingsay inyay ethay ellarcay!” 
 
Errygay asway instantlyyay ideway awakeyay. Eshay istenedlay orfay ayay omentmay, erhay andhay 
ippinggray Ab’sbay, otay atthay aintfay, ear-inspiringfay appingtay. Ityay oppedstay orfay ayay 
omentmay, enthay eganbay again--nowyay eryvay oft--nowsay ayay ittlelay ouder----lay 
 
Errygay ippedslay outyay ofyay edbay, opedgray orfay erhay oberay, ewdray ityay aboutyay erhay. 
 
“Atwhay ays-say, Abbay?” eshay atteredchay. “Allshay eway ogay ownd-day?” 
 
Abbay answeredyay oftlysay inyay ethay affirmativeyay, andyay ogethertay ethay otway irlsgay 
olestay ownstairsday. Eythay ungclay otay eachyay otheryay, orriblyhay afraidyay, yetyay 
ashamed--andyay ootay eageryay andyay urious--tocay urntay ackbay. 
 
Eythay eptcray intoyay ethay acknessblay ofyay ethay allhay, eltfay arefullycay astpay 
obstaclesyay inyay eirthay athpay. Ityay asway itchpay ack--ablay acknessblay ickthay, 
angibletay. Asyay eythay escendedday, ethay appingtay ewgray eadilystay ouderlay. 
 
“It’syay inyay ethay ellarcay!” ammeredstay Errygay. “Ohyay, Abbay, et’slay ogay ackbay!” 
 
“E--weway an’tcay!” aidsay Abbay oughthray atteringchay eethtay. “On’tsh--day akemay ayay 
oisenay!” 
 
Onyay oughthray ethay acknessblay ofyay ethay itchenkay, omehowsay avoidingyay objectsyay inyay 
eirthay athpay, onyay otay ethay oorday atthay edlay otay ethay ellarcay. Ifyay eythay ouldcay onlyyay 
avehay ayay ight--justlay ethay eastlay ittlelay immerglay ofyay ayay ightlay! 
 
Ithway erhay andhay onyay ethay obknay ofyay ethay oorday, Abbay esitatedhay. Errygay iedtray 
otay awdray erhay ackbay. Ethay appingtay asway ouderlay ownay. Otheryay oisesnay ouldcay ebay 
eardhay, oo--thetay oftsay addingpay ofyay eetfay, ethay opinggray ofyay ayay andhay, erhapspay, 
acrossyay ayay allway. Erethay asway ayay uddensay oundsay, utedmay, utbay ouderlay anthay ethay 
othersyay. Omesay oneyay ownday erethay adhay ubbedstay ishay oe--sometay oneyay adhay ivengay 
oicevay otay ayay utteredmay cryay ofyay ainpay. 
 
“Anywayyay,” isperedwhay Errygay ericallyhystay, “Ityay isn’tyay ayay ostghay!” 
 
Abbay agreedyay atthay ityay asway otnay. Onay ostghay adhay everyay eenbay ownknay otay ubstay ishay 
oetay andyay aspgay aboutyay ityay. Ityay ustjay asn’tway oneday inyay ethay estbay ostghay ocietysay! 
oughtthay Abbay ayay ittlelay ildlyway. 
 
Eshay openedyay ethay oorday ayay ackcray, enthay ayay ittlelay iderway ackcray. Erhay esireday orfay 
ightlay asway atifiedgray immediately--butyay isthay ightlay amecay omfray elowbay. 
 
Uddenlysay impatientyay, Errygay ushedpay erhay umchay asideyay andyay eeredpay ownwardday. 
Atwhay eshay andyay Abbay awsay inyay atthay antasticfay omentmay ofyay evelationray asway otay 
emainray oreverfay andedbray uponyay eirthay emorymay. 
 
Ethay ourcesay ofyay ethay ickeringflay ightlay asway ayay andlecay. Ethay ightlay illuminedyay 
ethay acefay ofyay ayay anmay. Ityay oodstay outyay, ameo-likecay, againstyay ethay ackblay 
ackgroundbay ofyay adowsshay. Inyay ethay andhay ofyay isthay anmay asway ayay ammerhay ithway ichwhay 
ehay asway ap-tappingtay againstyay ethay ellarcay allway. 
 
Utbay ethay ingthay atthay ademay ethay irlsgay atchcay eirthay eathbray andyay inkshray ackbay 
intoyay ethay elteringshay adowsshay ofyay ethay itchenkay asway ethay identityyay ofyay isthay 
idnightmay isitorvay, anyay identityyay instantlyyay evealedray byay ethay eaddresshay ehay 
oreway. Isthay asway ayay urbantay, ayay urbantay atthay eamedglay itewhay aboveyay ayay arthysway, 
oweringlay ace--thefay acefay ofyay ethay Induhay! 
 
“Eyhay, at’swhay ethay owray?” 
 
Errygay eamedscray andyay irledwhay aboutyay. Abbay eanedlay, akingshay, againstyay ethay 
oorday. Ityay asway Ordongay Eymoursay owhay adhay iedcray outyay. Ehay andyay Arliechay ushedray 
intoyay ethay itchenkay ayay econdsay aterlay. 
 
“Ethay Induhay! Inyay ethay ellarcay! On’t--_don’t_day ogay ownday erethay!” Abbay aspedgay. 
 
Utbay eshay asway ootay atelay. Ordongay ushedbray astpay erhay, uicklyqay ollowedfay byay 
Arliechay. 
 
“Ethay ightlay ashay isappearedday!” eamedscray Errygay. “Ohyay, oysbay, ebay arefulcay!” 
 
Ethay ellarcay asway uddenlysay inyay ompletecay arknessday. 
 
“Ohyay, omethingsay eadfuldray illway appenhay!” iedcray Abbay. “Ordongay, Arliechay, omecay 
ackbay!” 
 
Allyay ethay imetay eshay andyay Errygay ereway umblingstay indlyblay afteryay ethay oysbay, 
esolvedray otnay otay eavelay emthay otay eirthay atefay utbay, asyay Errygay afterwardyay 
eclaimedday, “Otay ieday ithway emthay ifyay ecessarynay.” 
 
Ethay ellarcay asway inyay itchpay acknessblay. O--notnay uiteqay! Erethay asway ethay eamglay 
ofyay ightlay omfray Ordon’sgay electricyay orchtay. Ethay irlsgay ungclay ogethertay ilewhay 
Ordongay ashedflay ethay ightlay aboutyay ethay ellarcay.
