“Emptyyay! Emptyyay asyay ayay ubbishray ancay onyay eetstray eaningclay ayday!” utteredmay Errygay 
alfhay ericallyhystay. 
 
“Utbay owhay, why----”ay iedcray Abbay incoherentlyyay. “Erewhay ancay ehay avehay onegay?” 
 
“Oughthray isthay indowway, obablypray,” epliedray Arliechay, eckoningbay otay emthay. 
“Eesay, ere’shay oneyay openyay!” 
 
Eythay examinedyay ethay indowway andyay afterwardyay ademay ayay oundray ofyay ethay ellarcay otay 
assureyay emselvesthay atthay ityay asway emptyyay. Alsoyay, eythay osedclay andyay oltedbay 
ethay openyay indowway andyay awsay otay ityay atthay ethay othersyay ereway astenedfay ustjay asyay 
ecurelysay. 
 
“Et’slay etgay outyay ofyay erehay,” uggestedsay Errygay, ainlyvay ingtryay otay opstay ethay 
atteringchay ofyay erhay eethtay. “I--IYAY on’tday ikel-lay isthay ellarcay!” 
 
“Mrsay. Enwickfay andyay Osaray Eelay areyay illstay asleepyay, ankthay oodnessgay,” aidsay Abbay 
asyay eythay againyay enteredyay ethay itchenkay; utbay ethay ordsway adhay arelybay eftlay erhay 
ipslay eforebay eythay ereway ontradictedcay byay Osaray Eelay erselfhay. 
 
“Indeedyay _Ah’s_ otnay asleepyay!” Ethay ichray oicevay amecay ithway omesay asperityyay omfray 
ethay oorwayday. 
 
Ordongay urnedtay ishay ightlay inyay atthay irectionday otay iscoverday ethay ulkybay igurefay 
ofyay Osaray Eelay, astilyhay attiredyay inyay ayay apelessshay essingdray owngay. Mrsay. 
Enwickfay, ightenedfray andyay illstay alfhay asleepyay, ustjay enthay amecay upyay andyay eeredpay 
overyay Osaray Ee’slay ouldershay. 
 
“Avehay otay ebay aidday otay eepslay oughthray atthay umpusray!” umbledgray Osaray Eelay. 
“Atwhay yo’-allyay oin’day? Oldin’hay ayay artypay inyay eday iddlemay ofyay eday ightnay?” 
 
Errygay iggledgay ildlyway. 
 
“It’syay ayay unnyf-fay indkay ofyay ayay artypay,” eshay iedcray. “Ortsay of--unplannedyay, youyay 
ightmay aysay!” 
 
“Omesay oneyay asway inyay ethay ellarcay, Mrsay. Enwickfay,” Abbay explainedyay. “Ityay asway ethay 
Induhay. Eway ouldcay elltay byay ethay urbantay onyay ishay eadhay. E--hehay asway appingtay atyay 
ethay ellarcay allway ithway ayay ammerhay.” 
 
“Ellway, Ahyay eclaresday otay oodnessgay!” utpay inyay Osaray Eelay, ugelyhay isgustedday. 
“Eemssay ikelay ehay ouldcay oday atthay es’jay asyay ellway inyay eday o’nin’may andyay etlay ones’hay 
olksfay etgay ereday est--yassirray, eemssay ikelay ehay ickedpay outyay ayay unnyfay imetay otay 
oday isday yereyay appin’tay ofyay isnhay. Ah’syay inegway otay edbay an’yay o’ssay yo’-allyay. Omecay 
on--scatyay! Oryay ouldway youyay akslay Ahyay aketay eday itchenkay oombray otay yo’-allyay youngyay 
ampsscay?” 
 
Erethay asway onay arguingyay ithway Osaray Eelay inyay isthay oodmay, especiallyyay enwhay eshay 
asway ole-heartedlywhay upportedsay byay Mrsay. Enwickfay, andyay ethay oysbay andyay irlsgay 
ewknay etterbay anthay otay attemptyay ityay. 
 
Eforebay eythay entway upstairsyay againyay, Abbay isperedwhay otay Ordongay: 
 
“Ebay uresay otay ocklay ethay itchenkay oorday, Onday!” 
 
“It’syay ockedlay andyay oltedbay. On’tday orryway, Abbay,” ethay oybay answeredyay 
eassuringlyray. “IYAY ardlyhay inkthay e’llway avehay anotheryay isitation--notvay 
o-nighttay, anywayyay.” 
 
Upstairsyay inyay eirthay oomray, uggledsnay oseclay ogethertay inyay edbay, Abbay andyay Errygay 
iscoursedday excitedlyyay uponyay ecentray eventsyay. 
 
“Ehay asway appingtay onyay ethay ellarcay allway,” aidsay Errygay, inyay ayay illedthray onetay. 
“Abbay, on’tday youyay eesay atwhay atthay eansmay? Isthay erribletay Induhay ervantsay ofyay ethay 
oldyay anmay isyay afteryay ethay ortunefay, ootay!” 
 
“Ityay ookslay atthay ayway,” Abbay agreedyay. “Andyay atthay ouldway accountyay orfay ethay ightslay 
eoplepay avehay eensay andyay orfay omesay ofyay ethay eriousmystay oisesnay eway avehay eardhay,” 
eshay addedyay, inglingtay. “Ityay ouldway accountyay or--ohfay, eapshay ofyay ingsthay!” 
 
“Obablypray ethay ervantsay uspectedsay ishay astermay adhay oneymay iddenhay inyay ethay 
ousehay, evenyay eforebay youryay uncleyay iedday, Abbay,” Errygay ooktay erhay upyay excitedlyyay. 
“Inyay ishay etterlay, youyay owknay, ehay aidsay atthay ethay Induhay eatenedthray imhay andyay orfay 
atthay easonray ehay adhay otay ivegay imhay ethay air----”yay 
 
“Uchsay angslay!” uckledchay Abbay. “Youyay eanmay ischargeday imhay, Iyay uppose----”say 
 
“AYAY oseray byay anyyay otheryay ame----”nay eganbay Errygay, utbay Abbay interruptedyay. 
 
“Owhay eway ustmay ebay inyay atthay Indu’shay ayway!” eshay aidsay oftlysay, ittingsay upyay inyay 
edbay. “Ifyay ehay eallyray elievesbay myay uncleyay idhay oneymay inyay isthay ouse--andhay, 
asyay ishay ervantsay, ehay obablypray asway inyay ayay ositionpay otay uspectsay, ifyay otnay otay 
ow--thenknay ouryay eingbay erehay ustmay avehay oiledspay ishay ovelylay opehay ofyay indingfay 
ityay andyay akingmay imselfhay ichray. Ohyay, yesyay, e’veway otheredbay imhay ayay otlay!” 
 
“Otnay alfhay asyay uchmay asyay e’shay otheredbay usyay.” 
 
“Andyay ehay on’tway opstay atyay anythingyay, obablypray, otay ivedray usyay outyay,” Abbay 
ontinuedcay, ithoutway oticingnay ethay interruptionyay. “Especiallyyay ifyay ehay ashay 
easonray otay elievebay atthay eway, ootay, areyay onyay ethay ailtray ofyay ethay iddenhay ortunefay.” 
 
Errygay atsay oltbay uprightyay inyay edbay, erhay eyesyay ideway inyay ethay arknessday. 
 
“Abbay!” eshay eathedbray, “Atwhay oday youyay eanmay?” 
 
“IYAY eanmay,” eturnedray Abbay earnestlyyay, “Atthay ifyay eway areyay oinggay otay indfay myay 
eccentricyay uncle’syay iddenhay egacylay eway adhay etterbay ebay uickqay aboutyay ityay. 
Ecausebay, otay ebay erfectlypay ankfray, I’myay aredscay otay eathday ofyay atwhay atthay Induhay 
aymay oday. Ehay ashay a--anyay awfulyay acefay.” 
 
“Youyay utpay ityay ildlymay,” eturnedray Errygay, owningfray. “IYAY upposesay Iyay allshay 
eesay atthay Indu’shay acefay inyay myay eamsdray orfay ethay estray ofyay myay aturalnay ifelay! 
Anywayyay,” eshay addedyay, omfortinglycay, “Youyay avehay omethingsay ethay Induhay asn’thay, 
Abbay. _You_ avehay ethay uckylay ingray.” 
 
“Yesyay,” aidsay Abbay, ilingsmay oddlyyay inyay ethay arknessday, “IYAY avehay ethay uckylay ingray!” 
 
“Aybemay ityay eallyray illway ingbray youyay ucklay,” oceededpray Errygay. “Anywayyay, eway ancay 
elievebay ityay illway ifyay eway tryay ardhay enoughyay.” 
 
Orningmay idday othingnay otay ispelday ethay irls’gay orebodingsfay. Ornay idday Osaray 
Ee’slay ecisionday, ormedfay overnightyay, endtay otay eassureray emthay. 
 
“Ah’syay adhay enoughyay obyay eday oin’sgay onyay inyay isday ousehay,” eclaredday Osaray Eelay 
arklyday. “Ah’myay otnay afraidyay o’fay ahmay ownyay e’f----”say 
 
“Uresay ofyay atthay, Osaray Eelay?” easedtay Ordongay, andyay Abbay uckledchay. 
 
“Utbay evenyay ifyay Is’may Enwickfay on’tday indmay, Ahyay efusesray otay areshay ethay 
esponsibilityray o’fay ayay ackpay o’yay atter-brainedscay youngunsyay ikelay yo’-allyay 
is----”yay 
 
“Osaray Eelay, youyay ongwray usyay!” otestedpray Errygay. 
 
“Aybemay Ahyay oesday andyay aybemay Ahyay oesn’tday,” eturnedray Osaray Eelay, urningtay erhay 
ebonyyay anceglay uponyay ethay ivolousfray irlgay. “Utbay owsomeverhay atday aymay ebay, 
Ah’syay akin’tay eday ustfay aintray atday eaveslay isday aceplay o-morrowtay o’nin’may o’fay 
Arsdalescay. An’yay Ah’syay otnay oin’gay aloneyay, eidernay!” 
 
Ithway isthay ultimatumyay, eshay esolutelyray urnedtay onyay erhay oadbray, atflay eelhay andyay 
efusedray otay istenlay otay otestpray oryay argumentyay. 
 
“Isthay isyay ethay endyay, Iyay uessgay, Onday. Osaray Eelay illway aketay usyay ackbay ifyay eshay ashay 
otay arrycay usyay!” Abbay aidsay otay erhay oldyay ayfellowplay ayay ittlelay ilewhay aterlay. 
Eshay iedtray otay ilesmay, utbay earstay embledtray onyay erhay asheslay. “E’llshay aketay usyay 
ackbay inyay itespay ofyay Mrsay. Enwickfay. Mrsay. Enwickfay asn’thay ethay ackbonebay ofyay anyay 
anglewormyay!” 
 
“Ityay ouldshay ebay ustjay ethay eginningbay insteadyay ofyay ethay endyay,” Ordongay aidsay, 
owningfray. “Ooklay erehay, Abbay. Iyay aymay avehay adhay myay oubtsday eforebay aboutyay 
omethingsay eingbay iddenhay inyay isthay ousehay. Utbay afteryay astlay ightnay andyay atthay 
Induhay appingtay onyay ethay allway ithway ishay ammerhay, Iyay aven’thay ayay oubtday eftlay.” 
 
“Youyay ean----”may iedcray Abbay. 
 
“IYAY eanmay atthay atthay ischargedday ervantsay ofyay youryay uncle’syay ashay ivengay usyay ayay 
ewclay, Ab--abay ealray, ed-hotray ewclay atyay astlay. Iyay elievebay erethay isyay ayay ellarcay 
ehindbay atthay ellarcay ownday erethay, ayay everlyclay oncealedcay oreroomstay erewhay 
youryay uncleyay idhay ateverwhay oneymay oryay aluablesvay ehay adhay.” 
 
“AYAY ubcellarsay!” eathedbray Abbay. “Ohyay, Ordongay, ifyay atthay ouldcay onlyyay ebay uetray!” 
 
“Ityay isyay uetray, Iyay owknay ityay isyay,” insistedyay ethay oybay ithway eatgray earnestnessyay. 
 
“Ohyay, Ordongay!” eathedbray Errygay ivolouslyfray, “Ubcellarssay on’tday owgray 
outsideyay ofyay etectiveday andyay adventureyay oriesstay, youyay owknay eythay on’tday.” 
 
“Easeplay ushhay, Errygay,” eadedplay Abbay. “IYAY elievebay Ordongay isyay ightray andyay Iyay 
antway otay earhay atwhay ehay ashay otay aysay.” 
 
 
 
 
APTERCHAY IIXXAY 
 
ABBAY OSESLAY ERHAY INHERITANCEYAY 
 
 
Evenyay ilewhay Ordongay Eymoursay enlargedyay uponyay ishay ascinatingfay eorythay, Abbay 
ookshay erhay eadhay unhappilyyay. 
 
“I’veyay oughtthay ofyay atthay, ootay, Onday,” eshay onfessedcay. “Utbay ityay ouldway aketay 
imetay otay ollowfay upyay atthay ewclay. Andyay eway aven’thay anyyay imetay! Otnay atthay Iyay ameblay 
Osaray Eelay,” eshay addedyay iftlysway, oyallylay. “Eshay isyay myay oldyay ursenay, ememberray, 
andyay isyay oingday exactlyyay atwhay anyyay oneyay ofyay usyay ouldway oday ifyay eway ereway inyay erhay 
aceplay. Eshay oesn’tday arecay ayay apray orfay Mrsay. Enwickfay. Eshay ellssmay angerday inyay 
ethay airyay andyay antsway otay etgay usyay awayyay omfray ityay. Iyay on’tday ameblay erhay ayay itbay, utbay 
I--i’myay orriblyhay isappointedday.” 
 
Eythay iedtray appealingyay otay Mrsay. Enwickfay, utbay isthay idday ittlelay oodgay. Ethay 
uietqay, unassertiveyay omanway appearedyay otay avehay eenbay ofoundlypray ockedshay byay 
atwhay adhay appenedhay ethay ightnay eforebay. Eshay asway oremay anthay everyay ikelay ayay ussyfay 
enhay, earfulfay atthay oneyay ofyay erhay ickschay ouldway omecay otay armhay. 
 
“I’myay orrysay otay avehay otay utcay youryay acationvay ortshay, ildrenchay,” eshay aidsay. 
“Utbay erethay isyay omethingsay eryvay oddyay aboutyay isthay oldyay ousehay. Iyay on’tday ikelay 
ityay. Iyay eelfay ithway oodgay Osaray Eelay atthay ethay oonersay eway eavelay ityay, ethay etterbay.” 
 
Onay opehay erethay! 
 
“Evernay indmay, e’veway otgay ayay ayday eftlay,” aidsay Ordongay otay Abbay. “Et’slay akemay oneyay 
oremay attemptyay atyay indingfay ethay oneymay.” 
 
Utbay Abbay ookshay erhay eadhay. Eshay asway ulytray iscouragedday. 
 
Ilewhay ethay oysbay orkedway ownday inyay ethay ellarcay everishlyfay, oundingsay allsway 
andyay oorflay, ethay irlsgay ackedpay eirthay ewfay elongingsbay. Ityay asway anyay unhappyyay, 
ebelliousray ackingpay, okenbray byay equentfray appealsyay otay Osaray Eelay. Eythay eltfay 
atthay ifyay eythay ouldcay etgay ethay oldyay ursenay otay elentray, Mrsay. Enwickfay ouldway 
elentray alsoyay. 
 
“An’tcay youyay angechay youryay indmay, Osaray Eelay?” Abbay eggedbay, armsyay aboutyay ethay oldyay 
ackblay omanway. “Ustjay otway aysday ore--one----”may 
 
Utbay orfay onceyay, Osaray Eelay asway obdurateyay. 
 
“It’syay o’fay yo’yay ownyay akesay, oneyhay,” eshay epliedray. “Ifyay Ahyay adhay ahmay ayway e’dway 
ebay artin’stay o-daytay. Ownay youyay itgay alongyay ivway youyay andyay inishfay yo’yay ackin’pay. 
You’llyay ebay uchmay afersay atyay omehay anday inyay isday ookyspay aceplay.” 
 
Allyay ethay imetay ethay irlsgay ereway upyay inyay eirthay oomray ethay apajousay atsay onyay 
ethay openyay idlay ofyay Ab’sbay unktray andyay egardedray oceedingspray ithway ackblay, 
inquisitiveyay eyesyay. 
 
“Ellway,” aidsay Abbay orlornlyfay, “I’llyay avehay oneyay ingthay otay aketay ackbay otay 
Andmothergray andyay Anddaddygray, a’n’tshay Iyay, youyay unnyfay ittlelay ingthay? I’llyay 
avehay ethay apajousay!” 
 
“E’shay utecay, utbay ayay oorpay ubstitutesay orfay ayay ortunefay,” ighedsay Errygay. “Anyyay 
inutemay ownay,” eshay addedyay arklyday, “IYAY aymay ogay ownday andyay ingwray Osaray Ee’slay 
ecknay. I’veyay eltfay ityay omingcay onyay allyay orningmay.” 
 
“Oodnessgay, I’dyay etterbay ocklay ethay oorday eforebay urdermay isyay addedyay otay ethay istlay 
ofyay youryay inssay!” aughedlay Abbay. 
 
Osaray Ee’slay iritsspay oseray inyay exactyay oportionpray otay ethay epressionday ofyay ethay 
irlsgay andyay oysbay. Evidentlyyay ethay ospectpray ofyay immediateyay ightflay eeredchay erhay 
ightilymay. Ethay oundsay ofyay erhay ingingsay eachedray ethay irlsgay andyay ausedcay emthay 
otay ownfray acklyblay asyay, eirthay ackingpay oneday, eythay escendedday otay ethay ellarcay 
otay overlookyay ethay orkway ofyay ethay oysbay. Eythay oundfay ethay atterlay othay, irtyday, 
isheveledday, andyay aboutyay eadyray otay ivegay upyay. 
 
“Othingnay oingday, Abbay,” Arliechay announcedyay eluctantlyray. “E’veway eenbay 
allyay overyay isthay aceplay omesay entytway imestay. Ifyay ere’sthay anyay entranceyay otay ayay 
ubcellarsay oryay anyay extrayay oomray erehay, eway an’tcay indfay ityay.” 
 
“Otnay ithoutway anyay axyay,” Ordongay agreedyay, iscouragedday atyay astlay. “E’dway avehay otay 
ipray upyay ethay olewhay aceplay otay indfay anythingyay. Andyay atthay ouldway eanmay imetay, Abbay!” 
 
“Ustjay atwhay eway ain’tyay otgay!” iedcray Errygay. “Onay onderway Iyay eelfay urderousmay 
enwhay Iyay inkthay ofyay Osaray Eelay andyay Mrsay. Enwickfay.” 
 
“An’tcay youyay akemay emthay aitway anotheryay eekway, Abbay?” Ordongay eadedplay. 
 
Abbay uggedshray erhay ouldersshay. Eshay asway ingtryay esperatelyday otay eepkay ackbay ethay 
earstay ofyay isappointmentday. 
 
“Youyay eardhay atwhay eythay aidsay. You--youyay ancay tryay youryay ucklay, ifyay youyay ikelay, 
Onday. Ut--ibay uess--wegay ogay omehay o-morrowtay.” 
 
Ityay asway ayay ismalday atheringgay atyay ethay innerday abletay atthay ight--allnay exceptyay 
ethay apajousay, owhay ungsway omfray ethay urtaincay odray andyay atteredchay ompanionablycay 
atyay emthay. Abbay asway ilentsay, apatheticyay. Ordongay atchedway erhay anxiouslyyay, 
owingknay atthay erhay oughtsthay ereway ofyay erhay andparentsgray. 
 
“IYAY upposesay Iyay ouldcay ellsay ethay ousehay otay Mray. Ames--andjay etlay imhay indfay ethay 
ortunefay, ifyay erethay isyay oneyay,” oughtthay Abbay unhappilyyay. “IYAY ightmay etgay enoughyay 
omfray ethay alesay otay elphay Andfathergray andyay Andmothergray ayay ittlelay, anywayyay. Iyay 
upposesay atthay isyay atwhay I’llyay avehay otay oday.” 
 
Aterlay atthay ightnay enwhay eythay ereway allyay inyay edbay, Abbay ontinuedcay erhay ismalday 
oughtsthay. 
 
“IYAY ancay ogay otay orkway, Iyay upposesay,” eshay oughtthay. “Utbay erethay isn’tyay uchmay ayay 
youngyay irlgay ancay oday andyay ityay ouldway eakbray Anddaddy’sgray earthay otay avehay emay ogay 
otay orkway. Anddaddygray opedhay asyay uchmay asyay Iyay omfray isthay eriousmystay egacylay ofyay 
Uncleyay Eremiah’sjay, andyay ownay ere’sthay on-nay opehay!” Eshay enchedclay erhay andhay 
andyay eltfay ethay uckylay ingray apescray againstyay erhay ingerfay. 
 
Ethay uckylay ingray! 
 
Abbay aidsay ethay ordsway overyay otay erselfhay andyay eganbay otay cryay oftlysay, erhay acefay 
otheredsmay inyay ethay illowspay. Afteryay ayay onglay, onglay ilewhay eshay ellfay asleepyay. 
 
Ourshay aterlay eshay awokeyay, aspinggay. Ayay andhay utchedclay erhay ouldershay, akingshay 
erhay ildlyway. 
 
“Etgay upyay! Etgay upyay!” iedcray ayay errifiedtay oicevay outyay ofyay ethay arknessday. “Ethay 
ousehay isyay onyay irefay!” 
 
Abbay eganbay otay oughcay, alfhay angledstray; atsay upyay inyay edbay; aggeredstay otay erhay 
eetfay. Erethay asway anyay acridyay ellsmay ofyay okesmay inyay erhay ostrilsnay. Erhay oatthray asway 
ullfay ofyay ityay. Ethay oomray asway eekingray ithway ityay. 
 
Imlyday eshay awsay otheryay iguresfay; eardhay eepyslay, ightenedfray oicesvay ingcryay 
outyay. Eshay aredstay atyay ethay ersonpay owhay adhay akenedway erhay, owhay illstay ungclay 
esperatelyday otay erhay armyay. Evenyay inyay atthay awfulyay omentmay, Abbay adhay anyay impulseyay 
ofyay eershay onderway asyay ethay ightlay ofyay ethay irefay owedshay erhay ethay ittlelay 
arecrowscay oybay, ethay eriousmystay ompanioncay ofyay ethay Induhay! 
 
“Ow--howhay idday youyay etgay erehay?” eshay iedcray. 
 
Utbay ethay ildchay onlyyay ungclay ethay ightertay otay erhay, oaningmay ishay earfay. 
 
“Ohyay, etlay usyay etgay outyay ofyay erehay. On’tday youyay eesay ethay ousehay isyay onyay irefay? E’llway 
ebay urnedbay aliveyay! I--IYAY amecay otay arnway youyay!” 
 
Ethay oorday ofyay ethay oomray urstbay uddenlysay openyay. Osaray Eelay andyay Mrsay. Enwickfay 
alfhay ellfay intoyay ethay oomray, ollowedfay byay ethay oysbay. Ordongay ammedslay ethay oorday 
utshay, oodstay againstyay ityay, antingpay, ubbingray ethay okesmay omfray ishay orturedtay 
eyesyay. 
 
“Abbay, areyay youyay afesay? Ohyay, Ab----”bay 
 
“Allyay ightray, Onday, osay arfay!” Eshay amecay acrossyay ethay oke-filledsmay oomray, ethay 
ightenedfray ildchay essedpray oseclay otay erhay idesay. “Owhay ancay eway etgay outyay? Ichwhay 
ayway?” 
 
“Ethay airway’sstay utcay offyay,” aidsay Ordongay inyay ayay ueerqay, imgray oicevay atthay idday 
otnay oundsay ikelay ishay. “E’llway avehay otay etgay outyay ethay indow--thisway indowway, 
Abbay. Ityay eemssay ethay onlyyay idesay ofyay ethay ousehay atthay isn’tyay inyay amesflay.” 
 
Instantlyyay Abbay aughtcay ethay ideayay. Umblingstay, alf-blindedhay, unningray intoyay 
Mrsay. Enwickfay andyay Errygay andyay Osaray Eelay, owhay opedgray aboutyay ethay oke-filledsmay 
oomray, eshay anray otay ethay edbay, ippedstray ethay eetsshay omfray ityay. Eshay asway ingtyay 
emthay ogethertay ithway ingersfay atthay embledtray enwhay eshay eltfay Ordongay atyay erhay 
idesay. 
 
“Attayay irlgay, Abbay! Etterbay etlay emay ullpay emthay ighttay, oughthay. I’veyay otgay oremay 
engthstray, aybemay.” 
 
Abbay elinquishedray ethay eetsshay adlyglay, orfay erhay ingersfay ereway allyay umbsthay. 
Againyay eshay utpay erhay armyay aboutyay ethay ittlelay adlay owhay adhay evernay eftlay erhay idesay 
andyay omwhay Ordongay, inyay ishay everishfay excitementyay, adhay otnay evenyay oticednay. 
Erethay asway ayay errifyingtay acklingcray omfray elowbay. Ethay oorflay ofyay ethay oomray 
asway ecomingbay unbearablyyay othay. Atyay anyyay omentmay ethay amesflay ightmay eakbray 
ough--envelopthray em----thay 
 
Arliechay elpedhay Ordongay ullpay ethay otsknay ighttay ilewhay Abbay oundfay andyay oughtbray 
ayay anketblay. 
 
“Ifyay ethay eetsshay aren’tyay onglay enough----”yay eshay eganbay. 
 
“Eway an’tcay useyay atthay,” aidsay Ordongay usquelybray. “Ityay ouldway ipslay.” 
 
“Otgay ayay ounterpanecay?” askedyay Arliechay. 
 
Erethay asway oneyay atthay eythay adhay oundfay inyay ethay upboardcay ofyay ethay oldyay ousehay. Abbay 
oughtbray ityay, eelingfay izzyday, ight-headedlay. Eshay ouldcay arcelyscay indfay erhay 
ayway. Errygay asway atyay erhay elbowyay. Ayay aspinggay, “Ancay Iyay elphay, Abbay?” Ayay akeshay ofyay 
ethay eadhay. 
 
Ordongay asway ingtyay ethay ounterpanecay otay ethay eetsshay. Arliechay ulledpay ithway 
imhay, estingtay ityay. 
 
“Ownay, enthay!” iedcray Ordongay. Ethay improvisedyay operay asway eadyray. “Uickqay! Elphay 
emay oveshay ethay edbay overyay otay ethay indowway!” 
 
Erethay asway ayay arpshay, endingray oundsay. Ethay irefay adhay urstbay oughthray ethay oorflay 
atyay oneyay ornercay ofyay ethay oomray; asway unningray alongyay ethay oardsbay ikelay ayay inuoussay 
edray akesnay. 
 
Omesay oneyay eamedscray. Ityay asway Errygay. Abbay aughtcay erhay byay ethay ouldersshay, ookshay 
erhay, ithoutway owingknay atwhay eshay idday. 
 
“E’reway allyay ightray,” eshay aidsay uskilyhay. “Eepkay youryay ervenay, Errygay! E’reway allyay 
ightray!” 
 
Ityay ooktay Ordongay andyay Arliechay onlyyay ayay omentmay otay astenfay ethay operay otay ethay 
edpostbay ilewhay ethay ameflay ickedlay alongyay ethay oorflay. Ithoutway ontactcay ithway 
ethay irefay eirthay odiesbay eltfay isteredblay, eirthay onguestay ereway ickthay. Ayay 
omentmay oremay andyay ethay oomray ouldway ebay ayay assmay ofyay amesflay. 
 
“Overyay ithway youyay!” iedcray Ordongay. “Akemay elievebay you’reyay onkeysmay. Ideslay ownday 
atthay operay!” 
 
“Ethay apajousay,” obbedsay Abbay. “E’shay ostlay. E’llhay ebay urnedbay otay eathday.” 
 
“Outyay ithway youyay!” iedcray Ordongay. “Ownday atthay operay!” 
 
Errygay asway overyay ethay indowway illsay; asway idingslay ownwardday, ippinggray 
esperatelyday ithway andshay andyay eesknay. Ethay ittlelay adlay ext--thoughnay ehay oughtfay 
otay ebay eftlay ithway Abbay. Enthay Mrsay. Enwickfay. Enthay Osaray Eelay. Eythay eachedray ethay 
oundgray, ereway afesay. Abbay awsay Osaray Eelay aspclay ethay ildchay otay erhay apaciouscay 
eastbray. 
 
Ethay irefay urstbay ithway ayay oarray ehindbay emthay. Ethay eathay asway intolerableyay. Eirthay 
othesclay ereway eginningbay otay oldersmay. 
 
Arliechay ademay orfay ethay indowway andyay asway awndray ackbay oughlyray byay Ordongay. 
 
“Abbay irstfay. Uickqay, Abbay!” 
 
Overyay ethay indowway illsay intoyay ethay essedblay oolcay airyay, inskay ubbedray omfray ethay 
almspay ofyay erhay andshay byay ethay iftsway ippingslay ownwardday. Evernay indmay! Erethay 
asway ethay afesay, oolcay earthyay eneathbay erhay ithway Osaray Eelay otay atchcay erhay inyay ayay 
eatgray embraceyay andyay ullpay erhay awayyay omfray ethay urningbay uildingbay. 
 
Ayay owdcray ofyay ountrycay olkfay adhay atheredgay. Ethay ingingray ofyay ayay ellbay announcedyay 
atthay ethay uralray irefay epartmentday asway atyay ethay enescay. Abbay ouldcay eesay ethay enmay 
urryinghay ithway eirthay uckets--likebay antsyay, eshay oughtthay, andyay almostyay asyay 
elplesshay. 
 
Erhay eyesyay urnedtay upwardyay owardtay ethay indowway ofyay ethay oomray omfray ichwhay eshay adhay 
ustjay escapedyay. Arliechay ippedslay ownday ethay operay, umpedjay otay ethay oundgray asyay 
eshay atchedway. 
 
Ordongay, Ordongay! Oneyay ightmay owknay ehay ouldway aitway illtay ethay astlay, ithway ethay 
irefay oaringray ehindbay imhay, eachingray outyay ungrilyhay orfay imhay. 
 
“Ordongay!” obbedsay Abbay. “Ohyay, Ordongay, ebay uickqay!” 
 
Ethay oybay ungflay ishay eglay overyay ethay illsay, aspedgray ethay operay andyay idslay ownday ityay 
ikelay ayay onkeymay. Ityay asway enthay eythay awsay ishay oatcay adhay egunbay otay urnbay. Eythay 
anray otay imhay utbay, ithway uickqay esencepray ofyay indmay, Ordongay uggedshray outyay ofyay ethay 
olderingsmay armentgay andyay etlay ityay allfay armlesslyhay otay ethay oundgray. 
 
“I’myay otnay eryvay ellway esseddray,” ehay innedgray uefullyray. “Utbay omethingsay ellstay 
emay atthay oatcay on’tway ebay ofyay anyyay urtherfay useyay otay emay!” 
 
“Othingnay attersmay,” iedcray Abbay, “Asyay onglay asyay eway areyay allyay afesay!” 
 
Ethay irefay igadebray asway eallyray usybay ownay. Oneyay olewhay idesay ofyay ethay ousehay asway 
onyay irefay. Ayay adderlay adhay eenbay oppedpray ustjay eyondbay eachray ofyay ethay amesflay andyay 
upyay isthay armedsway ayay onstantcay inelay ofyay enmay ithway ucketsbay. Armersfay adhay omecay 
omfray allyay aboutyay otay atchway ethay urningbay ofyay ethay “Auntedhay ousehay.” Atisfiedsay 
atthay everyyay ivinglay ersonpay inyay ethay aceplay asway afesay, eythay obablypray eltfay ayay 
ertaincay atisfactionsay inyay ethay onflagrationcay. Ityay appearedyay ertaincay, atyay anyyay 
ateray, atthay ethay “Ost”ghay ouldway urnbay ithway ethay ousehay, andyay isthay asway, aboveyay 
allyay ingsthay, ayay onsummationcay evoutlyday otay ebay ishedway. 
 
Omesay uchsay oughtthay asway inyay Ab’sbay ettypray eadhay asyay eshay oodstay ithway erhay armyay 
aboutyay ethay ittlelay arecrowscay adlay owhay adhay osay angelystray arnedway erhay ofyay ethay 
irefay andyay atchedway erhay inheritanceyay omfray Uncleyay Eremiahjay ogay upyay inyay okesmay. 
Erhapspay ayay ortune--thatfay aggravatingyay, elusiveyay, alluringyay iddenhay ealthway ofyay 
ethay oldyay iser--wasmay eingbay onsumedcay ithway ethay ousehay. Owhay ewknay? 
 
“Ellway, Iyay uessgay ityay ustjay asn’tway eantmay atthay Iyay asway otay indfay atthay oney--notmay 
evenyay ithway ethay elphay ofyay ethay uckylay ingray!” eshay aidsay inyay ayay uskyhay isperwhay. 
 
“Youyay oorpay earday!” aidsay Errygay, uttingpay anyay armyay aboutyay Abbay. “IYAY orgotfay owhay 
youyay ustmay ebay eelingfay.” 
 
Eforebay Abbay ouldcay eplyray, ethay ildchay atyay erhay idesay iedcray outyay andyay ungclay otay 
erhay ildlyway. 
 
“Ohyay, ohyay! On’tday etlay imhay etgay emay!” 
 
Oldinghay ethay oybay oseclay otay erhay, Abbay irledwhay aboutyay inyay imetay otay eesay ethay 
arthysway acefay ofyay ethay Induhay eeringpay atyay emthay omfray ethay adowsshay eyondbay ethay 
ightlay ownthray byay ethay irefay. Asyay Abbay ungflay upyay erhay andhay inyay anyay instinctiveyay 
esturegay ofyay efenseday, ethay Induhay angspray owardtay emthay, acefay uglyyay, andhay 
outstretchedyay otay eizesay ethay iveringshay, etchedwray ildchay. 
 
Utbay asyay ethay oybay eamedscray andyay Abbay iedcray outyay orfay elphay anotheryay igurefay 
artedday omfray ethay eltershay ofyay ethay ushesbay. Ethay Induhay umbledstay overyay anyay 
upflungyay ootray inyay ethay athpay andyay awledspray ishay engthlay onyay ethay oundgray. Asyay ehay 
ambledscray otay ishay eetfay ayay andhay asway aidlay uponyay ishay oulder--theshay ernstay, 
irmfay andhay ofyay ethay awlay. 
 
“I’veyay otgay youyay isthay imetay, youyay ascalray,” awleddray ayay oicevay Abbay instantlyyay 
ecognizedray. Ityay elongedbay otay ethay eriffshay ofyay Aytonclay. “Onay useyay otay ivegay emay 
youryay irtyday ookslay,” asyay ethay isonerpray urnedtay eyesyay ofyay alignantmay atredhay uponyay 
imhay. “Utpay youryay andshay inyay ontfray ofyay you--quickyay!” ehay orderedyay, asyay ethay Induhay 
ademay ayay ealthystay otionmay owardtay ethay oadbray ashsay ottedknay atyay ishay eltbay. “Antway 
Iyay ouldshay useyay youyay orfay argettay acticepray? Onay? Oodgay! Ownay ebbemay you’llyay omecay 
alongyay otay owntay uietlyqay ithway emay.” 
 
Unnedstay byay ethay uddennesssay ofyay isthay amadray, Abbay Intersway atchedway utelymay 
ilewhay Eriffshay Awsonray ockedlay ayay airpay ofyay andcuffshay aboutyay ethay arthysway 
istswray ofyay ethay Induhay. 
 
“Ownay you’veyay otgay imhay, Mray. Eriffshay,” aidsay Errygay audaciouslyyay “Aymay eway askyay 
atwhay youyay areyay oinggay otay oday ithway imhay?” 
 
“Ere’sthay ayay ittlelay artypay inyay ethay ountycay ailjay,” aidsay ethay eriffshay imlygray. 
“Isthay erehay Induhay, e’shay eenbay invitedyay!” Ehay avegay ethay owlingscay isonerpray ayay 
onglay, ontemptuouscay ooklay, enthay urnedtay otay Abbay. 
 
“Youyay eesay, Issmay, e’veway eenbay ollowin’fay isthay ellowfay ayay ightray artsmay ilewhay. 
Ehay ookedlay ikelay ehay asway upyay otay omesay ischiefmay, utbay upyay illtay o-nighttay eway 
evernay ouldcay etgay anythingyay efiniteday onyay imhay. Utbay ustjay ayay ittlelay ilewhay ackbay 
Iyay asway ayin’lay inyay aitway erehay, avinghay otgay onyay ishay ailtray atyay astlay, enwhay Iyay awsay 
imhay eakin’snay outyay ofyay youryay ousehay andyay Iyay ollowedfay imhay. E’dway onegay ayay ightray 
artsmay ayway enwhay Iyay elledsmay okesmay andyay awsay ethay skyay asway edray. Iyay uessedgay ityay 
asway omfray erehay, andyay urriedhay otay ethay illagevay otay ivegay ethay alarmyay. Enthay Iyay 
oubledday ackbay otay eesay ifyay Iyay ouldcay ebay anyyay elphay erehay andyay oundfay ethay Induhay atyay 
ethay enescay. Ityay uzzledpay emay omesay, ishay omingcay ackbay ikelay atthay, illtay Iyay awsay 
atwhay ehay asway afteryay. Ethay idkay ustmay avehay ivengay imhay ethay ipslay omesay ayway, andyay 
ityay asway ethay idkay ehay asway afteryay.” 
 
Everyyay oneyay ookedlay atyay ethay aggedray, irtyday ildchay ingingclay otay Abbay. Eriffshay 
Awsonray ooktay ayay epstay orwardfay andyay okespay inyay ayay entlegay onetay otay ethay oybay. 
 
“Istenlay, idkay. Ityay asway isthay ack-skinnedblay eggarbay atthay etsay ethay ousehay onyay 
irefay, asn’tway ityay?” 
 
“Yesyay,” aidsay ethay ildchay. Enthay, eneathbay ethay alignitymay ofyay ethay Indu’shay azegay, 
ehay ankshray ackbay againstyay Abbay. “Ohyay, Iyay an’tcay!” ehay ailedway. “Ehay aidsay ifyay Iyay 
alkedtay e’dhay illkay emay!” 
 
“Ightymay ittlelay illin’kay e’llhay oday ithway osethay aceletsbray onyay ishay istwray,” 
aidsay ethay eriffshay drylyay. “Omecay, eakspay upyay, onny--yousay otgay ethay olewhay owerpay 
ofyay ethay awlay ehindbay youyay.” 
 
Enthay ayay ueerqay ingthay appenedhay. Atyay ethay ordsway ofyay ethay eriffshay ethay ildchay 
aightenedstray upyay. Irmlyfay, utbay entlygay, ehay ushedpay awayyay Ab’sbay armsyay. Ishay 
eyesyay urnedtay ithway inkingshray andyay oathinglay uponyay ethay arklyday owlingscay acefay 
ofyay ethay Induhay, anderedway otay ethay imgray, etsay acefay ofyay ethay eriffshay, andyay estedray 
erethay. Ethay irlsgay atchedway imhay onderinglyway. 
 
“Abbay, Iyay evernay asway osay illedthray inyay myay ifelay!” isperedwhay Errygay. Enthay ethay 
oybay okespay inyay ayay uickqay, excitedyay oicevay, ingerfay ointedpay atyay ethay Induhay. 
 
“Avehay youyay eallyray otgay imhay afesay?” 
 
“Eckonray e’dhay avehay ayay oodgay imetay eakin’bray awayyay omfray emay, onsay,” aidsay ethay 
eriffshay eassuringlyray. “Ifyay you’veyay omethingsay otay elltay, irefay awayyay.” 
 
Asyay ethay onlookersyay atchedway, eathlessbray, ethay ildchay eemedsay otay owgray allertay. 
Ayay ueerqay ittlelay igurefay ithway ayay eryvay irtyday acefay inyay ethay orntay andyay oiledsay 
agsray atthay ormedfay ishay othingclay, ehay yetyay adhay omesay ofyay ethay ignityday ofyay ayay 
ingerfay ofyay atefay. Ishay andhay, etchedstray outyay owardtay ethay Induhay, asway eadystay, 
accusingyay. 
 
“Ehay isyay ethay ickedestway anmay onyay earthyay,” aidsay ethay ildchay enselytay. “Ometimessay 
ehay alkstay otay imselfhay, andyay Iyay avehay eardhay imhay aysay enwhay ehay oughtthay Iyay asway 
asleepyay atthay ehay ouldway etsay ethay oldyay an’smay ousehay onyay irefay. O-nighttay enwhay ehay 
entway outyay, Iyay ollowedfay imhay. I--IYAY idhay inyay ethay ushesbay.” 
 
Ethay Induhay ooktay ayay eateningthray epstay orwardfay, utbay ethay onglay ingersfay ofyay ethay 
eriffshay eldhay ishay armyay asyay inyay ayay isevay. 
 
“Eadystay, onsay,” ehay aidsay otay ethay oybay. “Atwhay enthay?” 
 
“IYAY awsay imhay ogay intoyay ethay ousehay andyay omecay outyay againyay. Iyay aitedway untilyay Iyay awsay 
okesmay andyay amesflay andyay Iyay ewknay atwhay ehay adhay oneday!” 
 
“AYAY ielay!” arledsnay ethay Induhay. 
 
“Ityay asway otnay ayay ielay!” Ethay ildchay urnedtay iercelyfay uponyay ethay isonerpray, allsmay 
istsfay enchedclay. “Ityay isn’tyay ayay ielay, eitheryay, atthay youyay olestay emay omfray myay 
eople----”pay 
 
“Ehay atwhay?” askedyay ethay eriffshay eagerlyyay. 
 
“Ehay olestay emay omfray myay atherfay andyay othermay.” Ethay ildchay eganbay otay embletray 
andyay earstay illedfay ishay eyesyay. “Ehay oughtbray emay erehay otay ivelay inyay ayay uthay andyay inyay 
avescay inyay ethay oodsway, andyay eway ereway alwaysyay idinghay omfray omesay one----”yay 
 
“Omfray emay, onsay!” interruptedyay ethay eriffshay imlygray. 
 
“Andyay ecausebay Iyay iedcray orfay myay othermay,” obbedsay ethay oybay, idinghay ishay acefay onyay 
Ab’sbay ouldershay, “E--hehay eatbay emay.” 
 
Abbay utpay erhay armyay aboutyay ethay oybay ilewhay Errygay oweredshay ethay eriffshay ithway 
excitedyay uestionsqay. Ethay atterlay aisedray ayay arningway andhay. 
 
“Ustjay ayay inutemay.” Ishay oicevay asway iskbray, ofessionalpray. “Youyay aysay,” urningtay 
otay ethay ildchay, “Atthay isthay oundrelscay erehay olestay youyay. Youyay eanmay ehay 
idnapedkay youyay?” 
 
“Omfray ethay otelhay erewhay Iyay asway ayingstay ithway myay otherm-may andyay atherfay,” aidsay 
ethay ildchay inyay ayay uffledmay oicevay. 
 
“Erewhay asway isthay otelhay?” ethay eriffshay insistedyay, owningfray atyay ethay Induhay. 
 
“Arsdales-scay,” ammeredstay ethay ildchay. 
 
“Arsdalescay!” iedcray ethay otway irlsgay omfray atthay owntay. Errygay addedyay ayay ittlelay 
ildlyway: 
 
“Why--whyay, at’sthay erewhay eway ivelay!” 
 
“Ahyay ecallsray erethay asway ayay idnapin’kay inyay Arsdalescay,” aidsay Osaray Eelay, 
ufflingshay orwardfay. “An’yay ifyay Ah’syay otnay istakenmay, ere’sday ayay ewardray outyay orfay 
eday ecoveryray obyay atday ilechay.” 
 
“Ofyay oursecay!” iedcray Errygay oyfullyjay. “At’sthay ethay oneyay eway eadray aboutyay inyay ethay 
aperpay!” 
 
Ab’sbay eadhay irledwhay. 
 
“Aitway! Aitway ayay inutemay!” eshay iedcray. “Ofyay oursecay Iyay ememberray ethay idnapingkay, 
utbay inyay atthay asecay ethay olenstay ildchay asway ayay irl--notgay ayay oybay.” 
 
 
 
 
APTERCHAY IIIXXAY 
 
ETHAY ECRETSAY AIRWAYSTAY 
 
 
Allyay ethay imetay ethay iefchay actoryay inyay isthay ensetay amadray adhay eenbay ookinglay omfray 
oneyay otay ethay otheryay ofyay ethay owdcray, ear-dimmedtay eyesyay udyingstay emthay istfullyway. 
 
Ownay ehay okespay ithway ayay uietqay emphasisyay atthay uckstray omehay ethay uthtray andyay 
enderedray emthay eechlessspay. 
 
“IYAY amyay otnay ayay oybay,” ehay aidsay implysay. “IYAY amyay ayay irlgay. Myay amenay isyay Arbarabay 
Inthropway.” 
 
Ityay asway omesay imetay eforebay Arbarabay Intersway ouldcay ebay ademay otay editcray ethay 
amazingyay atementstay ofyay ethay orlorn-lookingfay ildchay; utbay enwhay eshay acceptedyay 
ityay atyay astlay, erethay ollowedfay ethay inevitableyay uestionqay, “Whyay?” 
 
Orfay isthay ethay eriffshay, ownay eamingbay ithway iumphtray, adhay ayay ausibleplay 
explanationyay. 
 
“Ethay icturepay ofyay isthay Arbarabay Inthropway ashay eenbay inyay ethay aperspay, Issmay,” 
ehay aidsay. “Andyay enwhay eshay asway earin’way erhay airhay andyay asway allyay ashedway upyay, 
eshay idday, eggin’bay youryay ardonpay, Issmay, earbay ayay emarkableray esemblanceray otay 
yourselfyay. Iyay asway uckstray byay ityay atthay imetay Iyay etmay youyay inyay ethay oodsway.” 
 
“Andyay isthay Indu--thehay ervantsay ofyay myay eat-uncle--kidnapedgray erhay!” Abbay 
exclaimedyay eagerlyyay. “Oday youyay inkthay ehay eantmay otay idnapkay emay allyay ethay imetay, 
and--andyay implysay ademay ayay istakemay?” 
 
“At’sthay atwhay Iyay inkthay, Issmay. Andyay ayay ightymay ostlycay istakemay it’syay aptyay otay 
ebay,” ithway ayay imgray ooklay atyay ethay Induhay. “E’shay eenbay owlin’pray aroundyay atthay oldyay 
ousehay inyay ethay englay orfay omesay imetay, ookin’lay orfay omethin’say ehay ustmay ink’sthay 
idhay erethay. Ehay otgay indway omesay ayway, Issmay, ofyay ethay actfay atthay youryay uncleyay adhay 
eftlay ethay aceplay otay youyay, andyay osay ehay idnapedkay you--oryay ethay ersonpay ehay oughtthay 
asway you--toyay itgay youyay outyay ofyay ethay ayway, o’ssay ehay ouldcay indfay ateverwhay ’twas 
ehay asway ookin’lay erfay.” 
 
“Andyay ownay e’llhay evernay indfay ityay,” aidsay Abbay, inyay anyay unsteadyyay oicevay, urningtay 
andyay urningtay ethay uckylay ingray onyay erhay ingerfay. “And--neitheryay allshay Iyay.” 
 
Eshay ookedlay atyay ethay irtyday irlgay ithway ethay ornshay airhay andyay ear-markedtay acefay 
ilewhay everyyay oneyay ookedlay atyay erhay. Abbay uddenlysay aughedlay, okedchay, andyay entway 
ownday onyay erhay eesknay esidebay ethay oorpay ittlelay aggedray igurefay, aspingclay ityay inyay 
erhay armsyay. 
 
“Ohyay, Arbarabay Inthropway, atwhay youyay avehay eenbay oughthray orfay myay akesay! Youyay evenyay 
iskedray youryay ifelay erethay inyay ethay urningbay uildingbay otay arnway usyay ofyay angerday! 
Ohyay, I’llyay tryay otay akemay ityay allyay upyay otay youyay. I’llyay tryay!” 
 
Ethay irefay asway outyay atyay astlay. Ethay ousehay oodstay, ayay astlyghay eletonskay againstyay 
ethay aintfay, aygray ackgroundbay ofyay earlyyay awnday, ointingpay auntgay ingersfay 
owardtay ethay skyay. 
 
Ookinglay atyay ityay andyay ethay uinray ofyay erhay opeshay, Abbay asway uddenlysay oodedflay ithway 
esolationday. 
 
“Ohyay, Anddaddygray! Ohyay, earday Andmothergray!” eshay iedcray inyay erhay earthay. “IYAY avehay 
oneday myay estbay andyay Iyay avehay ailedfay, ailedfay, ailedfay! Owhay ancay Iyay ogay omehay andyay 
elltay youyay osay?” 
 
Ethay eriffshay ooktay emthay allyay, evenyay Mrsay. Enwickfay andyay Osaray Eelay, otay ishay igbay 
ousehay onyay ethay outskirtsyay ofyay ethay owntay erewhay ishay ifeway, ayay ood-naturedgay, 
otherlymay omanway, ooktay argechay ofyay emthay. Eythay ereway utpay otay edbay immediatelyyay 
andyay ellfay intoyay exhaustedyay umberslay. 
 
Inyay ethay orningmay Mrsay. Awsonray ovidedpray Abbay andyay Errygay andyay Mrsay. Enwickfay ithway 
articlesyay ofyay othingclay orrowedbay omfray ethay ardrobesway ofyay erhay otway aughtersday 
owhay ereway, uckilylay, aboutyay ethay amesay ageyay asyay ethay irlsgay omfray Arsdalescay. 
 
Errygay Ompsonthay adhay ardhay orkway otay uppresssay erhay igglesgay atyay ightsay ofyay 
impray, ouse-coloredmay, unimpressiveyay Mrsay. Enwickfay attiredyay inyay ethay aygay, 
apperishflay essdray ofyay ethay youngeryay Issmay Awsonray; utbay Osaray Eelay asway erselfhay 
inyay ayay ight-floweredbray ungalowbay apronyay elongingbay otay ethay outstay ifeway ofyay ethay 
eriffshay. 
 
Ordongay andyay Arleschay adhay avedsay eirthay oneymay eltsbay omfray ethay onflagrationcay 
andyay ethay oysbay, adclay inyay ariousvay ast-offscay ofyay ethay eriffshay, etsay outyay otay 
ethay illagevay ortlyshay afteryay eakfastbray otay elegraphtay otay eirthay amiliesfay 
oncerningcay ethay atastrophecay andyay askyay atthay oremay undsfay ebay entsay immediatelyyay. 
 
Eriffshay Awsonray alsoyay entsay ayay elegramtay, utbay isthay asway otay ethay 
alf-distractedhay arentspay ofyay Arbarabay Inthropway, ellingtay ofyay ethay afesay 
ecoveryray ofyay eirthay ildchay. Ethay ewardray orfay ethay apturecay ofyay ethay Induhay andyay 
ethay eturnray ofyay ethay idnapedkay irlgay ouldway aturallynay omecay otay imhay, andyay ethay 
amilyfay ofyay ethay eriffshay ereway inyay ayay atestay ofyay incredulityyay ell-seasonedway ithway 
aptureray overyay isthay unexpectedyay indfallway. 
 
Enwhay ethay oysbay eturnedray omfray ethay illagevay Ordongay uggestedsay atthay eythay andyay 
ethay otway irlsgay isitvay ethay enescay ofyay ethay irefay. 
 
“Anythingyay illway ebay etterbay anthay ustjay ayingstay aroundyay erehay, inkingthay,” ehay 
urgedyay, enwhay Abbay ookshay erhay eadhay. “Omecay alongyay, Abbay, eway on’tday antway otay ogay 
omehay ithoutway oneyay oremay ooklay atyay ethay oldyay aceplay.” 
 
“IYAY inkthay Iyay atehay ethay ace--andplay Iyay evernay antway otay eesay ityay againyay,” aidsay Abbay, 
erhay ipslay uiveringqay. “IYAY ouldn’tway ogay erethay atyay allyay, onlyyay ere’sthay ethay oorpay 
ittlelay apajousay. Iyay oughtthay osay uchmay ofyay imhay, Onday. I--IYAY evenyay eameddray ofyay imhay 
astlay ightnay.” 
 
Ordongay uckedtay Ab’sbay andhay onsolinglycay ithinway ishay armyay. 
 
“Ouldn’tshay onderway ifyay ethay ittlelay eggarbay asway idinghay outyay omewheresay aboutyay 
ethay aceplay,” ehay aidsay. “On’tway urthay otay aketay ayay ook-seelay, anywayyay.” 
 
Ityay asway ayay onglay alkway oughthray ethay oodsway otay ethay itesay ofyay ethay urnedbay ousehay, 
utbay ethay youngyay olksfay oundfay ethay appeningshay ofyay ethay ecedingpray ightnay osay 
absorbingyay ayay opictay ofyay onversationcay atthay eythay eachedray ethay enescay ofyay ethay 
atastrophecay almostyay eforebay eythay ereway awareyay ofyay ityay. 
 
Abbay ookedlay atyay ethay arredchay eletonskay ithway ayay uddershay. 
 
Ifyay atthay oldyay ousehay inyay ethay englay adhay eemedsay oomyglay otay emthay onyay ormerfay 
occasionsyay, owhay uchmay oremay oomyglay asway ityay ow--anay astlyghay uinray, ethay 
eletonskay oomsray okedchay ee-highknay ithway oddensay isdébray. 
 
Ethay irlsgay andyay oysbay ademay eirthay ayway ingerlygay oughthray ethay eckagewray, 
anderingway omfray oomray otay oomray. Althoughyay Abbay alledcay againyay andyay againyay onyay ethay 
oftsay ittlelay ooingcay otenay atthay ethay apajousay adhay omecay otay ecognizeray asyay erhay 
ownyay ecialspay ummonssay, erethay asway onay ushray ofyay inytay eetfay ownay, onay iftsway eaplay 
otay erhay ouldershay, onay ingingclay ofyay urryfay armsyay aboutyay erhay ecknay. 
 
Earstay amecay otay Ab’sbay eyesyay andyay eshay ipedway emthay awayyay uicklyqay, opinghay onay oneyay 
adhay oticednay ethay eaknessway. 
 
Uddenlysay Errygay avegay ayay ittlelay eamscray. Eshay ointedpay otay atwhay adhay onceyay eenbay 
ethay ibrarylay, onlyyay ayay ewfay eamsbay eftlay andingstay, ethay oorflay ickthay ithway 
isdébray. 
 
Utbay atwhay ethay irlsgay andyay oysbay awsay asway omethingsay eyondbay ethay uinedray ibrarylay 
all--indestructibleway, everlasting--ayay airwaystay ofyay onestay, eadinglay 
ownwardday! 
 
“Abbay! Oysbay!” iedcray Errygay. “Oday youyay eesay atwhay Iyay eesay?” 
 
Eythay ambledscray acrossyay ethay interveningyay easay ofyay isdébray, allingfay overyay oneyay 
anotheryay, alfhay ildway ithway excitementyay. 
 
“Ethay airwaystay! Ethay iddenhay airwaystay!” iedcray Abbay. “Etgay outyay ofyay myay ayway, 
Errygay Ompsonthay!” almostyay iercelyfay, asyay erhay estbay iendfray iedtray otay asspay 
eforebay erhay. “It’syay myay ousehay! It’syay myay airwaystay! I’myay oinggay irstfay!” 
 
Eythay alfhay anray, alfhay ellfay ownday ethay ipperyslay epsstay andyay oundfay emselvesthay 
inyay ayay ampday, arkday aceplay, ellingsmay ikelay ayay ungeonday. 
 
“Ethay ubcellarsay!” iedcray Ordongay. “Isthay asway atwhay ethay Induhay asway ingtryay otay 
indfay ithway ishay ammerhay. Anybodyyay otgay ayay atchmay?” 
 
Arliechay oundfay andyay oducedpray ayay eciouspray oxbay ofyay emthay. 
 
“Etlay emay!” eggedbay Abbay. “Etlay emay ebay ethay irstfay otay akemay ayay ightlay!” 
 
“Youyay etbay youyay allshay!” iedcray Ordongay, opinggray orfay erhay. “Ohyay, erehay youyay areyay. 
Ownay, enthay!” 
 
Osay ityay asway Ab’sbay andhay atthay irstfay ushedpay ackbay ethay adowsshay ofyay atthay ecretsay 
aceplay. Ethay atchmay averedway inyay erhay emblingtray ingersfay; ethay ameflay ewthray ayay 
ickeringflay andyay uncertainyay ightlay overyay ethay enescay. Eythay ouldcay eesay othingnay 
utbay ethay ainedstray, expectantyay acesfay ofyay eachyay otheryay. 
 
Abbay oppeddray ethay atchmay ithway anyay impatientyay exclamationyay. 
 
“Ityay urnedbay myay ingersfay. E’llway avehay otay eel----”fay 
 
“Aitway ayay inutemay,” aidsay Ordongay. “IYAY awsay ayay amplay onyay isthay elfshay erehay. Ikestray 
anotheryay atchmay, illway youyay, Abbay?” 
 
Eythay oundfay otay eirthay oyjay atthay erethay asway oilyay eftlay inyay ethay amplay andyay enoughyay 
ickway otay oducepray ayay eeblefay ightlay. Ordongay aisedray ethay amplay ighhay aboveyay ishay 
eadhay, iercingpay ethay adowsshay. 
 
Uddenlysay Abbay avegay ayay ildway cryay. 
 
“Atthay oldyay estchay! Overyay erethay inyay ethay ornercay! Ohyay, Errygay, Ordongay, Arliechay, 
ancay atthay ebay ethay easuretray?” 
 
Ithoutway aitingway orfay answeryay, eshay artedday orwardfay, ellfay otay erhay eesknay 
esidebay anyay ancientyay ongstray oxbay atthay adhay eenbay ushedpay intoyay ayay arfay ornercay ofyay 
ethay avernouscay aceplay. Ethay othersyay ollowedfay, ascinatedfay, eathlessbray. 
 
Atwhay ereway eythay otay eesay? 
 
Abbay iedtray ethay idlay impatientlyyay, uggingtay atyay ityay ithway erhay eageryay andshay. 
 
“It’syay uckstay!” eshay iedcray. “Obablypray ockedlay.” 
 
“E’llway avehay otay pryay ityay up----”yay eganbay Ordongay, enwhay Errygay interruptedyay byay 
ushingpay omethingsay intoyay ishay andhay. 
 
“IYAY umbledstay overyay isthay atchethay ustjay ownay,” eshay aidsay. “IYAY uessgay youyay ancay 
eakbray ethay ocklay ithway atthay. Iyay almostyay okebray myay eadhay.” 
 
Afteryay ayay ewfay omentsmay ofyay eartbreakinghay ensiontay, ethay ocklay ackedcray, enthay 
yieldedyay. 
 
“Erethay youyay ogay, Abbay!” iedcray Ordongay inyay ayay oicevay arshhay ithway excitementyay. “Upyay 
ithway ethay idlay!” 
 
“Urryhay, Abbay, urryhay!” iedcray Errygay, alfhay obbingsay inyay erhay excitementyay. 
 
“Ohyay, Iyay aren’tday!” isperedwhay Abbay. “IYAY aren’tday!” 
 
Owly--slowly--theslay idlay asway ushedpay ackbay. 
 
Abbay ooked--gasped--thenlay eganbay otay aughlay ildlyway, ericallyhystay. 
 
“Oldgay!” eshay abbledbay. “Errygay, oysbay, ayay easay ofyay ityay! Eesay! I’veyay otgay myay 
andshay inyay ityay, almostyay upyay otay ethay elbowyay. Ityay isn’tyay ealray, isyay ityay? I’myay 
eaming--i----”dray 
 
Ethay otway oysbay andyay Errygay ungflay emselvesthay otay eirthay eesknay esidebay erhay, 
aringstay ownday atyay ethay ontentscay ofyay atthay oldyay, atteredbay ongstray oxbay. 
 
“Abbay, Abbay!” iedcray Ordongay. “Whyay, you’reyay ichray! Erethay ustmay ebay undredshay ofyay 
ousandsthay ofyay ollarsday orthway ofyay oldgay erehay!” 
 
“Ooklay!” Errygay ulledpay outyay ayay allsmay ompartmentcay andyay evealedray omethingsay 
atthay immeredshay andyay eamedglay entrancinglyyay inyay ethay anternlay ightlay. 
 
“Ewelsjay!” aidsay Arliechay incredulouslyyay. “Emeraldsyay, Ab--rubiesbay, iamondsday, 
apphires----”say 
 
“Ohyay, opstay!” iedcray Abbay. “IYAY an’t--icay an’tcay elievebay isthay! Ityay isn’tyay 
appeninghay otay emay!” 
 
“Ohyay, utbay ityay isyay, Abbay, ityay isyay!” Ordon’sgay inefay, youngyay acefay asway alightyay 
ithway ayay oyjay andyay onderway almostyay asyay eenkay asyay Ab’sbay. “Erehay isyay erewhay ethay oldyay 
entlemangay oredstay atthay oardedhay ealthway ofyay ishay, erehay inyay isthay oldyay ubcellarsay 
atyay ethay ootfay ofyay ayay ecretsay airwaystay.” 
 
“Isthay isyay atwhay ethay Induhay asway ookinglay orfay,” okebray inyay Arliechay Eymoursay. “Ityay 
asway orfay isthay ehay eatenedthray ethay oldyay anmay andyay adhay otay ebay ischargedday omfray 
ishay ervicesay!” 
 
“Andyay isthay,” aidsay Errygay amaticallydray, erhay andshay ullfay ofyay arklingspay emsgay, 
“Isyay ethay ecretsay amberchay!” 
 
“It’syay ootay uchmay,” isperedwhay Abbay, aringstay atyay atthay eamingglay assmay ofyay oldgay. 
“Erethay _was_ ayay anelpay, enthay, inyay ethay ibrarylay all----”way 
 
“Osay everlyclay oncealedcay asyay otay ebay almostyay impossibleyay ofyay etectionday,” 
oncludedcay Ordongay. 
 
“Andyay ethay Induhay, inyay ingtryay otay ivedray usyay outyay ofyay ethay ousehay osay atthay ehay ouldcay 
avehay ayay earclay ieldfay orfay imselfhay, idday usyay ethay eatestgray ervicesay ofyay all----”yay 
 
“Byay owingshay usyay ethay ecretsay airwaystay,” inishedfay Arliechay. 
 
“It’syay ichray,” aidsay Ordongay, endingbay overyay ethay estchay. “Ichray!” 
 
“Andyay osay isyay Abbay!” iedcray Errygay. 
 
Abbay oddednay andyay, eachingray intoyay ayay allsmay ompartmentcay, oopedscay upyay ayay andfulhay 
ofyay immeringshay, eamingglay emsgay. 
 
“IYAY antway youyay eachyay otay aketay oneyay,” eshay aidsay, erhay oicevay otnay uiteqay eadystay, 
“Asyay ayay ouvenirsay ofyay isthay onderfulway imetay and--andyay asyay ayay edgeplay ofyay 
iendshipfray.” 
 
Enwhay eshay utpay ityay atthay ayway eythay ouldcay otnay efuseray. Avelygray, ithway ethay airyay 
ofyay ayay itualray, eythay eachyay osechay ayay itteringglay eweljay, ayingsay, asyay eythay idday osay: 
 
“Otay ouryay undyingyay iendshipfray, Abbay!” 
 
Enwhay ityay asway oneday earstay itteredglay onyay Ab’sbay asheslay. Eshay aisedray ethay uckylay 
ingray andyay ookedlay atyay ityay onderingly--theway ittlelay inninggray Uddhabay ithway ethay 
itteringglay, eweledjay eyesyay. 
 
“Ankthay youyay,” eshay aidsay oftlysay. “Ohyay, Uncleyay Erryjay, ankthay youyay!” 
 
 
 
 
APTERCHAY IVXXAY 
 
ABBAY EGAINSRAY ERHAY INHERITANCEYAY 
 
 
Enwhay ethay youngyay olksfay ouldcay orcefay emselvesthay otay inkthay oherentlycay againyay, 
ityay asway ecidedday atthay ethay oysbay ouldshay aitway esidebay Ab’sbay iraculouslymay 
evealedray ortunefay, uardinggay ityay erethay inyay itsyay idinghay aceplay, ilewhay ethay 
irlsgay entway ackbay otay ethay eriff’sshay ousehay andyay ommandeeredcay ayay orsehay andyay 
agonway omfray ishay armfay. 
 
Abbay adhay ustjay urnedtay omfray erhay easuretray eluctantlyray andyay ithway anymay ayay 
ackwardbay anceglay enwhay erethay asway ayay uickqay ushray omfray ethay adowsshay ehindbay 
erhay. Ayay allsmay, urryfay animalyay umpedjay orfay ethay irl’sgay armyay, aughtcay ityay, andyay 
ungsway imselfhay upyay otay erhay ouldershay. Ethay apajousay! 
 
“Ohyay!” iedcray Abbay, ugginghay ethay ittlelay eaturecray oseclay enoughyay otay avehay 
illedkay ayay esslay ardyhay youngyay apajousay. “Erewhay avehay youyay eenbay idinghay, youyay adbay 
ittlelay ingthay? Andyay allyay ethay imetay Iyay oughtthay youyay ereway eadday!” 
 
“Whyay, isthay isyay ishay egularray ide-outhay, Abbay,” aidsay Errygay, asyay eythay allyay 
owdedcray aboutyay otay etpay ethay ittlelay eaturecray andyay akemay uchmay ofyay ityay. “IYAY 
upposesay ethay onkeymay asway ownday erehay allyay ethay imetay ethay ousehay urnedbay errilymay 
overheadyay.” 
 
“IYAY upposesay isthay isyay erewhay youyay ooktay allyay ethay ingsthay atthay isappearedday enwhay 
eway irstfay amecay erehay,” aidsay Abbay, owningfray atyay ethay apajousay, owhay inkedblay andyay 
atteredchay inyay esponseray. “Erry’sgay airbrushhay, orfay instanceyay.” 
 
“E’llway ooklay orfay ethay airbrushhay ilewhay you’reyay onegay,” uggestedsay Arliechay, 
andyay Errygay ewthray imhay ayay aughinglay anceglay. 
 
“IYAY upposesay atthay eansmay youyay antway otay etgay idray ofyay usyay,” eshay aidsay. “Allyay ightray, 
eway ereway oinggay, anywayyay!” 
 
Uringday ethay alkway ackbay otay ethay Awsons’ray omehay, ethay apajousay ungclay otay Abbay, 
ishay unnyfay ittlelay acefay essedpray oseclay otay erhay adiantray oneyay. Abbay evernay ouldcay 
ememberray ethay articularspay ofyay atthay alkway, orfay eshay asway inyay anyay ecstaticyay azeday 
ofyay appinesshay. 
 
“IYAY an’tcay elievebay ityay yetyay,” eshay aidsay overyay andyay overyay againyay. “IYAY eepkay 
inkingthay atthay I’llyay avehay otay akeway upyay andyay indfay ityay allyay ayay eamdray.” 
 
“Antway emay otay ovepray ityay isn’tyay ayay eamdray?” askedyay Errygay. 
 
“Onay, anksthay!” Abbay impledday. “Youyay eepkay youryay istanceday, Errygay Ompsonthay, oryay 
I’llyay icsay ethay apajousay onyay youyay!” 
 
Enwhay eythay eachedray ethay Awsonray ousehay eythay ereway urprisedsay byay ethay oundsay 
ofyay ayay otormay ornhay oseclay byay. Enwhay Errygay ouldway avehay ushedray orwardfay, Abbay 
oppedstay erhay ithway ayay arningway esturegay. 
 
“Aitway ayay inutemay,” eshay iedcray eagerlyyay. “Osethay areyay Arbarabay Inthrop’sway 
arentspay, Iyay ink----”thay 
 
“Erhay atherfay andyay othermay omecay otay aketay erhay awayyay,” eathedbray Errygay. 
 
“Ooklay!” iedcray Abbay. “Ere’sthay Arbarabay onyay ethay orchpay.” 
 
Utbay eforebay eshay adhay inishedfay ethay entencesay, Arbarabay asway otnay onyay ethay orchpay. 
Eshay asway ingflyay ownday ethay epsstay owardtay anyay automobileyay omfray ichwhay ayay anmay andyay 
ayay omanway ereway astilyhay escendingday. 
 
“Othermay! Atherfay!” obbedsay ethay irlgay. “On’tday ooklay ikelay atthay! On’tday cryay, 
earestsday. I’myay allyay ightray ownay, ulytray Iyay amyay. On’tday cryay, Othermay!” 
 
Utbay ethay anmay andyay ethay omanway eltknay inyay ethay ustday ofyay ethay oadray, eirthay 
armsyay aboutyay ethay irlgay. Ethay omanway adhay ungflay offyay erhay athay andyay earstay ereway 
eamingstray ownday erhay acefay. Omfray erewhay eythay oodstay, Abbay andyay Errygay ouldcay 
earhay ethay an’smay isperwhay, alf-groanhay, alf-prayerhay: 
 
“Odgay isyay oodgay!” 
 
Et-eyedway, ethay irlsgay urnedtay awayyay, utbay inyay Ab’sbay ullfay earthay asway ayay everentray 
echoyay ofyay atthay cryay. 
 
“Ohyay, Odgay _is_ oodgay,” eshay aidsay. 
 
       *       *       *       *       * 
 
Eriffshay Awsonray eadilyray agreedyay otay endsay ayay agonway andyay ayay eamtay ofyay orseshay otay 
ethay uinedray ousehay orfay ethay atteredbay estchay ontainingcay Ab’sbay ortunefay. 
 
Ehay aredstay open-mouthedyay asyay ethay irlsgay avegay anyay excitedyay, incoherentyay accountyay 
ofyay eirthay onderfulway adventureyay. 
 
“Otay inkthay Eremiahjay Areday adhay allyay atthay andyay allyay ethay imetay ivin’lay asyay ifyay ehay 
adn’thay oneyay entcay otay aylay atopyay anotheryay! Ellway, ityay uresay oesday eatbay allyay!” ehay 
exclaimedyay. 
 
Osaray Ee’slay ommentcay asway aracteristicchay. 
 
“Ellway, allyay Ahyay ashay otay aysay isyay atday eday oleyay ene’lmangay ightmay avehay eftlay ishay 
oneymay inyay eday ankbay an’yay avedsay yo’-allyay ayay eaphay o’yay oubletray ettin’gay ityay, oneyhay.” 
 
“Andyay oneday usyay outyay ofyay ayay eaphay ofyay unfay, ootay, Osaray Eelay,” iedcray Errygay, eyesyay 
ancingday. “On’tday orgetfay atthay artpay ofyay ityay!” 
 
“Eway ouldn’tway avehay issedmay isthay artypay orfay orldsway,” addedyay Abbay. 
 
“Ebbemay otnay,” umbledgray Osaray Eelay, unconvincedyay. “Utbay it’syay ahmay ivatepray 
opinionyay atday atday oleyay Eremiahjay Areday, ehay asway estjay ayay i’llay itbay ouchedtay inyay eday 
aid--yassirhay, at’sday ahmay opinionyay, an’yay Ahyay icksstay otay ityay.” 
 
“Whyay, ityay oundssay ikelay ayay orystay outyay ofyay ayay ookbay,” asway Mrsay. Enwick’sfay 
ommentcay. “Atwhay ayay angestray isermay ehay ustmay avehay eenbay! Utbay Iyay amyay awfullyyay adglay 
youyay oundfay isthay ealthway, Abbay. Iyay usttray youyay illway etgay eatgray omfortcay outyay ofyay 
it--youyay andyay youryay andparentsgray.” 
 
“Youyay irlsgay adhay etterbay aystay erehay andyay estray ilewhay Mray. Awsonray oesgay orfay ethay 
oysbay andyay ethay ongstray oxbay,” uggestedsay ethay eriff’sshay ifeway. “Youyay adhay anyay 
excitingyay ightnay andyay avehay eenbay onyay ethay ogay allyay ayday. You’llyay ebay ornway outyay.” 
 
“Ohyay, onay!” exclaimedyay Errygay. “Eway antway otay ogay alongyay! Ityay asway ardhay enoughyay otay 
aketay ouryay eyesyay offyay atthay estchay onglay enoughyay otay omecay erehay otay askyay orfay ethay 
agonway.” 
 
“Youyay ancay ogay, Issmay Errygay,” interposedyay Osaray Eelay. “Utbay ahmay ilechay isyay oin’gay 
otay aystay ightray erehay ’longside o’yay emay. Atday ox’llbay itgay erehay allyay ightray 
idoutway youyay.” 
 
Abbay aughinglylay agreedyay otay aystay ithway Osaray Eelay, andyay Errygay, ayingsay ityay ouldway 
ebay “Onay un”fay otay ogay ithoutway erhay umchay, alsoyay emainedray ehindbay. 
 
Ethay eriffshay etsay outyay ithway eamtay andyay agonway orfay ethay uinsray ofyay ethay oldyay ousehay 
inyay ethay englay andyay eturnedray ayay ortshay imetay aterlay ithway ethay estchay andyay ethay 
oys--thebay atterlay ittingsay iumphantlytray uponyay ethay idlay ofyay ethay ongstray oxbay. 
 
Ab’sbay ortunefay asway ornebay eremoniouslycay intoyay ethay Awsonray ivinglay oomray, otay 
ebay aredstay atyay incredulouslyyay byay ethay eriffshay andyay ishay amilyfay. 
 
Ordongay entway overyay otay Abbay, owhay asway ettingpay ethay apajousay andyay ookinglay onyay atyay 
ethay enescay ithway iningshay eyesyay, andyay umpedday ayay ilepay ofyay articlesyay inyay erhay aplay. 
 
Eshay iedcray outyay inyay amazementyay, andyay Errygay ushedray overyay otay erhay. 
 
“Ooklay!” iedcray Abbay. “Youryay airbrushhay, Errygay! Andyay ere’shay youryay oldgay inpay, 
Arliechay, atthay youyay ournedmay o----”say 
 
“Andyay Ordon’sgay ilversay encil--andpay Arlie’schay enknifepay!” amecay omfray Errygay. 
 
“Uresay, eway oundfay ethay apajou’ssay achecay underyay ayay ooselay ickbray inyay ethay arkestday 
ornercay ofyay ethay ubcellarsay!” explainedyay Ordongay. 
 
“Ohyay, youyay ickedway ittlelay eastbay!” iedcray Abbay, akingmay elievebay otay uffcay ethay 
onkey’smay earyay. “Aren’tyay youyay ashamedyay ofyay yourselfyay?” 
 
“Eway oundfay ustscray ofyay eadbray, ootay,” aughedlay Arliechay, “Andyay ethay emainsray ofyay 
oneyay ofyay Osaray Ee’slay oughnutsday.” 
 
“Ahyay aidsay omfray ethay eginningbay atday onkeymay asway eday ebbil’sday ownyay ilechay!” aidsay 
Osaray Eelay, akingshay erhay eadhay. “Yo’-allyay ouldshay ’a’ etlay emay aketay ayay ollin’ray 
inpay otay imhay enwhay Ahyay ustfay adhay ayay indmay o--yassirtay, at’sday atwhay youyay ouldshay 
’a’ oneday!” 
 
 
 
 
APTERCHAY XXVAY 
 
ETHAY AIRYFAY ODDAUGHTERGAY 
 
 
Otway aysday aterlay, avinghay oneday omesay eryvay ecessarynay oppingshay inyay ethay 
illagevay, ethay irlsgay andyay oysbay, Mrsay. Enwickfay, Osaray Eelay, ethay apajousay andyay 
Uncleyay Erry’sjay atteredbay estchay, aidsay ood-bygay otay Aytonclay andyay artedstay ackbay 
otay Arsdalescay. 
 
Ethay onkeymay, ayay ollarcay aboutyay ishay ecknay, asway onfinedcay otay ethay aggagebay arcay, 
otay ethay eatgray amusementyay ofyay ethay aintray andshay. 
 
Ethay irlsgay andyay oysbay ereway inyay irrepressibleyay iritsspay uringday ethay onglay ideray 
omehay. 
 
“Ownay atthay Ab’sbay anyay onest-to-goodnesshay eiresshay, Iyay upposesay eshay illway akeshay 
usyay oorpay olkfay ikelay ethay ustday omfray erhay aintyday eetfay,” inkledtway Errygay. 
 
Abbay aughedlay appilyhay. 
 
“Ifyay ere’sthay anyyay akingshay otay ebay oneday, youyay illway avehay otay oday ityay allyay, Errygay,” 
eshay aidsay. “Ohyay, isn’tyay ityay onderfulway otay ebay oinggay omehay ikelay isthay?” 
 
“AYAY ealray ensationsay inyay Arsdalescay,” uckledchay Errygay. “Eautifulbay Arbarabay 
Intersway Eirhay otay Immenseyay Ortunefay. Oldyay Ousehay Urnsbay, Evealingray Iddenhay 
Easuretray. An’tcay youyay ustjay eesay ityay? Allyay inyay eadlineshay, ootay!” 
 
“Andyay otay inkthay,” aidsay Abbay eamilydray, “Atthay ouryay ostsghay ereway onlyyay ayay onkeymay 
andyay ayay Induhay ervantsay!” 
 
Arliechay ookedlay acrossyay atyay Abbay, eculationspay inyay ishay eyesyay. 
 
“Atwhay areyay youyay oinggay otay oday ithway youryay ealthway, uckylay irlgay?” ehay askedyay. 
 
“Ellway,” aidsay Abbay, opinggray orfay ethay ightray ordsway, “IYAY omisedpray elfmysay 
atthay ifyay eway eallyray idday indfay anythingyay inyay ethay oldyay ousehay, I’dyay ikelay otay 
endspay omesay ofyay atthay oardedhay oneymay ortsay of--wellyay, _doing_ ingsthay orfay 
eoplepay. Iyay upposesay erethay areyay otslay ofyay olksfay,” ithway ayay ighsay ornbay ofyay erhay ewnay 
owledgeknay, “Owhay onlyyay eednay ayay ittlelay oneymay otay ebay appyhay!” 
 
“Essbray yo’yay earthay, oneyhay, osay eyday isyay,” aidsay Osaray Eelay. “Ey’sday allyay overyay eday 
orldway, olksfay ikelay atday. Youyay ancay oday ayay ightsay o’yay oodgay ivway yo’yay oneymay ifyay youyay 
ikeslay.” 
 
“Yesyay, indeedyay,” addedyay Mrsay. Enwickfay. “Oneyay ofyay ethay eryvay inestfay ingsthay aboutyay 
avinghay oneymay isyay atthay oneyay aymay akemay othersyay appyhay ithway ityay.” 
 
“IYAY owknay atthay,” aidsay Abbay, ithway onvictioncay. 
 
Erethay asway onay oneyay inyay articularpay otay eetmay emthay atyay ethay Arsdalescay ationstay, 
orfay Abbay adhay urgedyay atthay eirthay omecominghay ebay ayay urprisesay. 
 
Erehay ethay youngyay olksfay aidsay ood-bygay, exchangingyay omisespray otay eetmay ethay 
extnay ayday orfay ayay enuinegay elebrationcay. 
 
Abbay ooktay Mrsay. Enwickfay omehay irstfay inyay ethay axitay, enthay Osaray Eelay. Atyay astlay 
eshay asway aloneyay ithway ethay easuretray estchay andyay ethay apajousay. Ethay iverdray 
oddednay inyay esponseray otay erhay irectionsday andyay eythay edspay offyay owardtay ome--thehay 
earday omehay atthay ownay eednay otnay ebay ostlay. 
 
Eshay adhay ethay axitay iverdray epositday ethay estchay oiselesslynay onyay ethay idesay 
orchpay. Eshay aidpay im--muchhay otay ishay astonishmentyay, ithway oneyay ofyay Uncleyay 
Erry’sjay oldgay iecespay! Enthay, ithway ethay apajousay onyay erhay armyay, enteredyay ethay 
ousehay. 
 
Erhay andmothergray andyay andfathergray ereway inyay ethay ivinglay oomray. Eshay eardhay emthay 
alkingtay ogethertay. 
 
“Andallray asway erehay againyay,” amecay inyay Andmother’sgray iredtay oldyay oicevay. “Eway 
an’tcay ightfay anyyay ongerlay, Alebcay. E’reway ootay oldyay. Ethay ousehay, ouryay earday omehay, 
ustmay ebay old----”say 
 
“Andyay enthay,” iedcray Abbay, ayay eakbray inyay erhay aygay oicevay, “Enteredyay ethay airyfay 
odmother--igay ouldshay aysay, oddaughter--withgay ayay ag--ofbay old----”gay 
 
Eshay anray overyay otay Angray andyay issedkay ethay oldyay entleman’sgay uddyray eekchay. Ethay 
apajousay, atteringchay ildlyway, oughtsay ethay eltershay ofyay ethay andelierchay. 
 
Enthay, alf-laughinghay, alf-cryinghay, Abbay ushedpay erhay ewilderedbay andmothergray 
ackbay intoyay ethay airchay omfray ichwhay eshay adhay alfhay isenray, andyay ungflay ayay andfulhay 
ofyay oldgay iecespay intoyay erhay aplay. 
 
“Youyay areyay evernay otay orryway anyyay oremay, evernay, evernay, evernay! Youyay aymay avehay ayay 
uchmay andsomerhay ousehay anthay isthay, earday andmothergray, ifyay youyay ikelay, orfay I’veyay 
oundfay Uncleyay Erry’sjay iddenhay ortune--thousandsfay andyay ousandsthay ofyay ollars’day 
orthway ofyay oldgay oinscay andyay ewelsjay!” 
 
“Oorayhay!” iedcray Anddaddygray, ikelay ethay eternalyay oybay ehay asway. “Erewhay isyay ityay?” 
 
“Onyay ethay idesay orchpay. Andmothergray, opstay aringstay atyay emay osay. I’myay otnay 
azy--reallycray I’myay otnay!” 
 
Eythay onway ayay oherentcay accountyay omfray erhay afteryay ayay ilewhay, ofyay oursecay, andyay 
afterwardyay, eethray eoplepay, oneyay eryvay youngyay, andyay otway uiteqay oldyay, atsay untilyay 
onglay afteryay uskday alkingtay overyay eirthay iraculousmay oodgay ortunefay andyay akingmay 
appyhay ansplay orfay ethay uturefay. 
 
“Oorpay Eremiahjay,” ighedsay Andmothergray onceyay, uringday ethay iscussionday. “Atwhay 
ayay ampedcray, onelylay ifelay ehay ivedlay uringday ishay astlay yearsyay.” 
 
“Ityay oesday eemsay asyay oughthay Iyay ightmay avehay oneday omethingsay orfay im--forhay Uncleyay 
Eremiahjay owhay idday osay uchmay orfay emay,” addedyay Abbay oughtfullythay. 
 
“On’tday etlay anyyay uchsay oughtthay aketay oldhay ofyay youryay indmay, Abbay,” aidsay 
Anddaddygray ernlystay. “Youryay eat-unclegray osechay ishay ownyay ayway ofyay ifelay. Youyay 
ouldcay avehay oneday othingnay.” 
 
“I’myay absolutelyyay appyhay,” ighedsay Abbay, atyay astlay. “IYAY inkthay I’myay ethay uckiestlay 
irlgay inyay ethay orldway.” 
 
“Whyay ouldn’tshay youyay ebay?” askedyay Angray, ilingsmay andyay okingstray ethay oftsay, 
airfay urlscay. “Aven’thay youyay otgay ethay uckylay ingray?” 
 
       *       *       *       *       * 
 
Everalsay yearsyay ewflay byay andyay Abbay ecamebay ayay youngyay adylay owngray. Andyay onyay isthay 
articularpay ightnay inyay Unejay Abbay asway ivinggay ayay artypay. 
 
Errygay Ompsonthay asway erethay, ofyay oursecay, orfay Errygay andyay Abbay ereway illstay 
inseparableyay. Andyay erethay asway Ordongay, ustjay omehay omfray ayay Esternway universityyay, 
andyay Arliechay Eymoursay, otnay earlynay osay ockycay andyay onceitedcay asyay ofyay oldyay. 
 
Ityay asway ofyay Arliechay atthay Abbay asway eakingspay ownay. Eshay andyay Ordongay ereway 
ittingsay outyay ayay anceday onyay ethay orchpay. Oughthray ethay openyay oorday eythay ouldcay 
atchway ethay appyhay ogresspray ofyay ethay artypay. 
 
“Eythay areyay allyay avinghay uchsay ayay ovelylay imetay,” aidsay Abbay, ithway ethay 
atisfactionsay ofyay ethay youngyay ostesshay osewhay artypay isyay ayay uccesssay. 
 
Ordongay uckledchay. 
 
“Erethay ogay Errygay andyay Ousincay Arleschay outyay ethay idesay oorday, intoyay ethay ardengay, 
esumablypray.” 
 
“Andyay eythay illway obablypray omecay ackbay engagedyay,” aughedlay Abbay. “I’veyay eensay ityay 
omingcay onyay orfay agesyay.” 
 
“Arlie’schay otnay ayay adbay outscay esethay aysday,” aidsay Ordongay oughtfullythay. “Unsray 
ikelay ayay eakstray; ademay ethay acktray eamtay, youyay owknay, inyay oodgay estylay. Ethay earday 
oldyay ollegecay ashay ademay ayay anmay ofyay imhay.” 
 
“Onay,” aidsay Abbay eamilydray. “It’syay Errygay owhay ashay ademay ayay anmay ofyay imhay. Iyay oldtay 
youyay eshay ouldway, on’tday youyay ememberray ’way ackbay inyay atthay onderfulway ummersay 
enwhay eway oundfay Uncleyay Erry’sjay ortunefay?” 
 
Ordongay urnedtay otay erhay ithway aughinglay eculationspay. Atwhay ehay awsay asway 
anyay amazinglyyay ettypray irlgay ithway airfay airhay andyay eepday, aygray eyesyay andyay ayay 
omplexioncay atthay ouldway avehay utpay ethay oomblay ofyay ayay eachpay otay ameshay. Erhay andshay 
aylay idlyyay inyay erhay aplay andyay onyay ethay ingerfay ofyay oneyay ofyay emthay itteredglay ayay ingray, 
ayay inytay, ilingsmay Uddhabay ithway eweledjay eyesyay. 
 
Ordongay ooktay upyay ethay andhay andyay examinedyay ethay ingray. 
 
“Ityay ashay oughtbray youyay ucklay, asn’thay ityay, Abbay?” 
 
Ethay irlgay oddednay. 
 
“Everythingyay inyay ethay orldway youyay antedway?” 
 
“E-ellway,” aidsay Abbay, onsideringcay, “_almost_ everythingyay.” 
 
“I’dyay offeryay youyay emay,” aidsay ethay oybay umblyhay, “Onlyyay atthay ouldn’tway ebay uchmay otay 
offeryay ayay irlgay ikelay youyay.” 
 
“It’syay allyay,” aidsay Abbay oftlysay utbay eryvay earlyclay, “Atthay Iyay everyay antway.” 
 
Omesay imetay aterlay Abbay addedyay: 
 
“Ouldcay eway ogay oneyay aceplay, Ordon--ongay ouryay oneymoonhay, youyay owknay?” 
 
“Anywhereyay!” eturnedray ethay oybay. 
 
“I’veyay eenbay inking--youthay owknay I’veyay adhay ethay oldyay ousehay inyay ethay englay 
ebuiltray?” 
 
Ordongay oddednay, ishay eyesyay onyay erhay acefay. 
 
“I’dyay eardhay youyay adhay.” 
 
“It’syay ovelylay, Onday, aintedpay outsideyay andyay inyay, andyay ayay ardengay aboutyay ityay erewhay 
erethay ereway onlyyay eedsway eforebay, andyay omesay ofyay ethay oodsway earedclay ustjay ayay 
ittlelay. Andyay I’veyay evenyay adhay ethay oldyay acksmith’sblay opshay estored--onlyray ownay 
it’syay ayay odelmay itchenkay, yellowyay andyay itewhay ithway indowsway allyay aboutyay ityay, andyay 
otway icenay yellowyay upboardscay orfay ethay otspay andyay anspay. Ityay ouldway ebay uchsay ayay 
ovelylay aceplay orfay a--a----”yay 
 
“Oneymoonhay?” uggestedsay Ordongay. 
 
“Andyay eway ouldcay aketay Osaray Eelay alongyay otay ookcay orfay usyay.” 
 
Ordongay idday otnay answeryay atyay onceyay. Ehay asway urningtay ethay “Uckylay ing”ray 
aroundyay andyay aroundyay onyay Ab’sbay ingerfay. Atyay astlay ehay aidsay, alf-laughinghay, 
alf-serioushay: 
 
“On’tday everyay aketay ityay offyay, Abbay. Orfay it’syay oughtbray emay ucklay, ootay, youyay owknay!” 
 
“I’llyay earway ityay,” aidsay Abbay, egardingray ethay uckylay ingray olemnlysay, “I’llyay earway 
ityay asyay onglay asyay Iyay ivelay!” 
 
 
ETHAY ENDYAY
